#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, sqlite3, time

ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
BATCH=5
RUN_SECS=25
ACK_TIMEOUT=4

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except Exception:
        try: return b.decode()
        except Exception: return ""

def load_syms():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    try:
        rows=con.execute("SELECT symbol FROM u_syms ORDER BY symbol").fetchall()
        syms=[r[0] for r in rows if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT")]
    finally:
        con.close()
    return syms[:35]

async def subscribe_chunk(ws, chunk):
    args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in chunk]
    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))
    acks=set(); t0=time.time()
    while time.time()-t0 < ACK_TIMEOUT and len(acks)<len(chunk):
        try:
            raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=ACK_TIMEOUT)
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            break
        msg=ungzip(raw)
        try: obj=json.loads(msg)
        except Exception: continue
        if obj.get("event")=="subscribe":
            inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
            if inst in chunk: acks.add(inst)
        elif obj.get("event")=="error":
            print("ERR",obj)
    return acks

async def main():
    syms=load_syms()
    if not syms:
        print("Aucun symbole dans a.db.u_syms"); return
    print(f"TOP35={len(syms)}:", syms)

    counts={s:0 for s in syms}
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        for i in range(0,len(syms),BATCH):
            chunk=syms[i:i+BATCH]
            acks=await subscribe_chunk(ws, chunk)
            miss=[s for s in chunk if s not in acks]
            if miss: print("ACK manquants:", miss)
            await asyncio.sleep(0.2)

        start=time.time()
        while time.time()-start < RUN_SECS:
            try:
                raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=3)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"})); continue
            msg=ungzip(raw)
            try: obj=json.loads(msg)
            except Exception: continue
            if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
                inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
                if inst in counts: counts[inst]+=1

    total=sum(counts.values())
    got=sorted([(k,v) for k,v in counts.items() if v>0], key=lambda x:-x[1])
    miss=[k for k,v in counts.items() if v==0]
    print("\n=== RESUME ===")
    print("messages_total =", total)
    print("symbols_ok     =", len(got))
    for k,v in got[:15]:
        print(f"{k}: {v} msgs")
    if miss:
        print("aucun_msg pour:", ", ".join(miss))
----- FILE END -----

sqlite3 -csv "$DB" "SELECT symbol,side,ROUND(score,3),ROUND(entry,2),datetime(created_ts,'unixepoch','localtime') AS dt FROM signals_B ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 12;"

echo -e "\n== LAST plan =="
sqlite3 -csv "$DB" "SELECT symbol,side,ROUND(score,3),ROUND(entry,2),ROUND(sl,2),ROUND(tp,2),datetime(created_ts,'unixepoch','localtime') AS dt FROM signals_B_plan ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 15;"

sqlite3 -csv "$DB" "SELECT COALESCE(ctx,'?') AS ctx, COUNT(*) FROM signals_B_plan GROUP BY ctx ORDER BY 2 DESC;"

echo -e "\n== contraintes =="
sqlite3 "$DB" ".schema signals_B" | sed -n '1,120p'

#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
has_name() { sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA table_info(top_scores);" | awk -F'|' '$2=="name"{f=1}END{exit !f}'; }

sqlite3 "$DB" "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, symbol TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER);"

if ! has_name; then
  sqlite3 "$DB" "
  PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF;
  BEGIN;
  CREATE TABLE top_scores_new(
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT,
    symbol TEXT,
    score REAL,
    ts INTEGER
  );
  INSERT INTO top_scores_new(name,symbol,score,ts)
  SELECT 'TOP30', symbol, score, ts FROM top_scores;
  DROP TABLE top_scores;
  ALTER TABLE top_scores_new RENAME TO top_scores;
  COMMIT;"
fi
echo "[OK] top_scores prêt"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, ccxt, os
ADB=os.getenv("ADB","/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
TF_LIST=("5m","15m","30m"); LIMIT=int(os.getenv("LIMIT","100"))
def get_symbols():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    for t in ("u_syms","u_symbols"):
        try:
            rows=con.execute(f"SELECT symbol FROM {t}").fetchall()
            if rows: con.close(); return [r[0] for r in rows if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT")]
        except sqlite3.Error: pass
    con.close(); return []
def ensure_tables():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, isolation_level=None); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    for tf in TF_LIST:
        con.execute(f"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_{tf}(symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, o REAL,h REAL,l REAL,c REAL, PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))")
    con.close()
def bitget_symbol(ex, raw):
    base=raw[:-4] if raw.endswith("USDT") else raw
    # préf. perp USDT
    for m in ex.markets.values():
        if m.get("base")==base and m.get("quote")=="USDT" and (m.get("swap") or "UMCBL" in m.get("id","")):
            return m["symbol"]
    # sinon spot
    for m in ex.markets.values():
        if m.get("base")==base and m.get("quote")=="USDT" and not m.get("swap"):
            return m["symbol"]
    # fallback
    return f"{base}/USDT:USDT" if f"{base}/USDT:USDT" in ex.markets else f"{base}/USDT"
def insert_rows(tf, rows):
    if not rows: return
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, isolation_level=None)
    con.executemany(f"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ohlcv_{tf}(symbol,ts,o,h,l,c) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.close()
def main():
    syms=get_symbols()
    if not syms: print("Aucun symbole u_syms/u_symbols dans a.db"); return
    ensure_tables()
    ex=ccxt.bitget({'enableRateLimit': True}); ex.load_markets()
    for tf in TF_LIST:
        batch=[]
        for s in syms:
            ms=bitget_symbol(ex,s)
            try:
                for t,o,h,l,c,v in ex.fetch_ohlcv(ms, timeframe=tf, limit=LIMIT):
                    batch.append((s, int(t//1000), float(o), float(h), float(l), float(c)))
                time.sleep(ex.rateLimit/1000)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[WARN] {s} {tf} {ms}: {e}"); time.sleep(0.2)
        insert_rows(tf,batch); print(f"[OK] {tf}: {len(batch)}")
    print("done")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;

-- Sécurités de base
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_plan(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, score REAL, side TEXT,
  entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL,
  qty REAL, margin REAL, notional REAL,
  created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sigB_ts ON signals_B(created_ts);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_state(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  last_side TEXT,
  consec INTEGER,
  last_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS account_sim(equity REAL, leverage REAL);
INSERT INTO account_sim(rowid,equity,leverage)
  SELECT 1,300,50 WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM account_sim);

-- Paramètres (1 seule ligne)
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS params;
CREATE TEMP TABLE params AS
SELECT
  0.10  AS ATR_MIN_PCT,
  5     AS COOLDOWN_1M,
  1.00  AS SPREAD_MAX_PCT,
  1.3   AS VOL_MULT_PULLBACK,
  20    AS N_BREAKOUT,
  0.25  AS TAU_LOW,
  0.5   AS WEIGHT_PULLBACK,
  0.3   AS WEIGHT_BREAKOUT,
  0.2   AS WEIGHT_MEANREV,
  0.60  AS SCORE_TRIGGER,
  2     AS PERSIST_BARS_B,
  1     AS VETO_5M_EMA,
  1.2   AS ATR_SL_K,
  1.8   AS ATR_TP_K,
  1.0   AS TRAIL_K,
  25    AS TIMEOUT_MINUTES,
  0.005 AS RISK_PCT;

-- Univers = TOP + 5 fixes
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_universe;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_universe AS
SELECT symbol FROM v_universe;

-- Dernière barre 1m par symbole (avec LAG)
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_last1;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_last1 AS
SELECT *
FROM (
  SELECT
    i.symbol, i.ts, i.open, i.high, i.low, i.close, i.volume,
    i.spread_frac, i.vol_sma20, i.sma9, i.sma21, i.sma50,
    i.atr14, i.atr_pct, i.hh_20_excl, i.ll_20_excl,
    LAG(i.close)  OVER (PARTITION BY i.symbol ORDER BY i.ts) AS prev_close,
    LAG(i.volume) OVER (PARTITION BY i.symbol ORDER BY i.ts) AS prev_vol,
    ROW_NUMBER()  OVER (PARTITION BY i.symbol ORDER BY i.ts DESC) AS rn
  FROM v_indic_1m i
  WHERE i.symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM t_universe)
)
WHERE rn=1;

-- Gates
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_gates;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_gates AS
SELECT
  l.*,
  CASE WHEN l.atr_pct >= (SELECT ATR_MIN_PCT FROM params) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS gate_atr,
  CASE WHEN (l.spread_frac*100.0) <= (SELECT SPREAD_MAX_PCT FROM params) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS gate_spread
FROM t_last1 l;

-- Evidences
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_ev;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_ev AS
SELECT
  g.*,
  CASE WHEN g.close >= g.hh_20_excl THEN 1.0 ELSE 0.0 END AS e_breakout_up,
  CASE WHEN g.close <= g.ll_20_excl THEN 1.0 ELSE 0.0 END AS e_breakout_dn,
  CASE WHEN g.close>=g.sma9 AND g.prev_close < g.sma9
            AND g.volume >= (SELECT VOL_MULT_PULLBACK FROM params)*g.vol_sma20
       THEN 1.0 ELSE 0.0 END AS e_pullback_up,
  CASE WHEN g.close<=g.sma9 AND g.prev_close > g.sma9
            AND g.volume >= (SELECT VOL_MULT_PULLBACK FROM params)*g.vol_sma20
       THEN 1.0 ELSE 0.0 END AS e_pullback_dn,
  CASE WHEN g.sma21 IS NOT NULL AND g.atr14>0
       THEN MAX(0.0, MIN(1.0, (g.sma21 - g.close)/g.atr14)) ELSE 0.0 END AS e_mean_buy,
  CASE WHEN g.sma21 IS NOT NULL AND g.atr14>0
       THEN MAX(0.0, MIN(1.0, (g.close - g.sma21)/g.atr14)) ELSE 0.0 END AS e_mean_sell
FROM t_gates g;

-- Score brut
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_score;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_score AS
SELECT
  e.*,
  ((SELECT WEIGHT_PULLBACK FROM params)*e.e_pullback_up
   +(SELECT WEIGHT_BREAKOUT FROM params)*e.e_breakout_up
   +(SELECT WEIGHT_MEANREV  FROM params)*e.e_mean_buy)  AS s_buy_raw,
  ((SELECT WEIGHT_PULLBACK FROM params)*e.e_pullback_dn
   +(SELECT WEIGHT_BREAKOUT FROM params)*e.e_breakout_dn
   +(SELECT WEIGHT_MEANREV  FROM params)*e.e_mean_sell) AS s_sell_raw
FROM t_ev e;

-- Softmax
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_prob;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_prob AS
SELECT
  s.*,
  CASE WHEN s.s_buy_raw  <0 THEN 0 WHEN s.s_buy_raw  >1 THEN 1 ELSE s.s_buy_raw  END AS b0,
  CASE WHEN s.s_sell_raw <0 THEN 0 WHEN s.s_sell_raw >1 THEN 1 ELSE s.s_sell_raw END AS s0
FROM t_score s;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_mix;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_mix AS
SELECT
  p.*,
  exp(b0/(SELECT TAU_LOW FROM params)) AS eb,
  exp(s0/(SELECT TAU_LOW FROM params)) AS es,
  1.0                                  AS eh
FROM t_prob p;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_class;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_class AS
SELECT
  m.*,
  (m.eb+m.es+m.eh) AS denom,
  (m.eb/(m.eb+m.es+m.eh)) AS pb,
  (m.es/(m.eb+m.es+m.eh)) AS ps,
  (m.eh/(m.eb+m.es+m.eh)) AS ph
FROM t_mix m;

-- Veto 5m
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_veto;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_veto AS
SELECT
  c.*,
  vf.sma9  AS sma9_5,
  vf.sma21 AS sma21_5
FROM t_class c
LEFT JOIN v_indic5m_fast vf
  ON vf.symbol=c.symbol
 AND vf.ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM v_indic5m_fast v2 WHERE v2.symbol=c.symbol);

-- Décision brute
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_decide;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_decide AS
SELECT
  v.*,
  CASE
    WHEN v.pb>=v.ps AND v.pb>=(SELECT SCORE_TRIGGER FROM params) THEN 'buy'
    WHEN v.ps> v.pb AND v.ps>=(SELECT SCORE_TRIGGER FROM params) THEN 'sell'
    ELSE 'none'
  END AS side_raw,
  CASE
    WHEN (SELECT VETO_5M_EMA FROM params)=1
         AND v.pb>=v.ps AND v.sma9_5 IS NOT NULL AND v.sma21_5 IS NOT NULL
         AND v.sma9_5 < v.sma21_5
    THEN 0 ELSE 1 END AS veto_buy,
  CASE
    WHEN (SELECT VETO_5M_EMA FROM params)=1
         AND v.ps>v.pb AND v.sma9_5 IS NOT NULL AND v.sma21_5 IS NOT NULL
         AND v.sma9_5 > v.sma21_5
    THEN 0 ELSE 1 END AS veto_sell
FROM t_veto v;

-- Cooldown
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_cool;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_cool AS
SELECT
  d.*,
  COALESCE((SELECT MAX(created_ts) FROM signals_B sb WHERE sb.symbol=d.symbol),0) AS last_sig_ts
FROM t_decide d;

-- Filtre final
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_filt;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_filt AS
SELECT
  c.*,
  (c.gate_atr=1 AND c.gate_spread=1) AS ok_base,
  (strftime('%s','now') - c.last_sig_ts) >= ((SELECT COOLDOWN_1M FROM params)*60) AS ok_cool,
  CASE WHEN c.side_raw='buy'  THEN (c.veto_buy=1)
       WHEN c.side_raw='sell' THEN (c.veto_sell=1)
       ELSE 0 END AS ok_veto
FROM t_cool c;

-- Candidats retenus
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_cands;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_cands AS
SELECT
  f.symbol, f.ts, f.close AS entry, f.atr14, f.atr_pct,
  CASE WHEN f.side_raw IN('buy','sell') AND f.ok_base=1 AND f.ok_cool=1 AND f.ok_veto=1
       THEN f.side_raw ELSE 'none' END AS side,
  f.pb, f.ps, f.ph
FROM t_filt f;

-- Plan SL/TP + sizing
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS t_plan;
CREATE TEMP TABLE t_plan AS
SELECT
  c.symbol,
  'B' AS ctx,
  CASE WHEN c.side='buy' THEN c.pb ELSE c.ps END AS score,
  c.side,
  c.entry,
  CASE WHEN c.side='buy'  THEN c.entry - (SELECT ATR_SL_K FROM params)*c.atr14
       WHEN c.side='sell' THEN c.entry + (SELECT ATR_SL_K FROM params)*c.atr14
       ELSE NULL END AS sl,
  CASE WHEN c.side='buy'  THEN c.entry + (SELECT ATR_TP_K FROM params)*c.atr14
       WHEN c.side='sell' THEN c.entry - (SELECT ATR_TP_K FROM params)*c.atr14
       ELSE NULL END AS tp,
  ((SELECT COALESCE(equity,300) FROM account_sim LIMIT 1)
    * (SELECT RISK_PCT FROM params)
    * (SELECT COALESCE(leverage,50) FROM account_sim LIMIT 1)) / c.entry AS qty,
  ((SELECT COALESCE(equity,300) FROM account_sim LIMIT 1)
    * (SELECT RISK_PCT FROM params)) AS margin,
  ((SELECT COALESCE(equity,300) FROM account_sim LIMIT 1)
    * (SELECT RISK_PCT FROM params)
    * (SELECT COALESCE(leverage,50) FROM account_sim LIMIT 1)) AS notional
FROM t_cands c
WHERE c.side IN ('buy','sell');

-- Nettoyage des plans du tick courant, puis insert
DELETE FROM signals_B_plan WHERE created_ts>=strftime('%s','now')-10;
INSERT INTO signals_B_plan(symbol,ctx,score,side,entry,sl,tp,qty,margin,notional,created_ts)
SELECT symbol,ctx,score,side,entry,sl,tp,qty,margin,notional,strftime('%s','now')
FROM t_plan;

-- Persistance: calcule consec_new
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _upd;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _upd AS
SELECT p.symbol, p.side, p.entry
FROM signals_B_plan p
WHERE p.created_ts=(SELECT MAX(created_ts) FROM signals_B_plan);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _st;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _st AS
SELECT
  u.symbol,
  CASE
    WHEN EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM b_state b WHERE b.symbol=u.symbol AND b.last_side=u.side)
      THEN (SELECT consec FROM b_state b WHERE b.symbol=u.symbol)+1
    ELSE 1
  END AS consec_new,
  u.side
FROM _upd u;

-- Ecriture des signaux si persistance atteinte
INSERT INTO signals_B(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts)
SELECT u.symbol, u.side, u.entry, 'B', strftime('%s','now')
FROM _st s JOIN _upd u USING(symbol)
WHERE s.consec_new >= (SELECT PERSIST_BARS_B FROM params);

-- MAJ b_state par delete+insert
DELETE FROM b_state WHERE symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM _upd);
INSERT INTO b_state(symbol,last_side,consec,last_ts)
SELECT u.symbol, u.side, s.consec_new, (SELECT MAX(created_ts) FROM signals_B_plan)
FROM _upd u JOIN _st s USING(symbol);
SQL

# Résumés
sqlite3 "$DB" "
SELECT COUNT(*) AS new_plan FROM signals_B_plan WHERE created_ts>=strftime('%s','now')-10;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS new_signals FROM signals_B WHERE created_ts>=strftime('%s','now')-10;
SELECT symbol,side,ROUND(score,3),ROUND(entry,6),ROUND(sl,6),ROUND(tp,6),ROUND(qty,6)
FROM signals_B_plan ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 12;
SELECT symbol,side,price,datetime(created_ts,'unixepoch','localtime')
FROM signals_B ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 12;
"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"

echo "== top_scores heads =="
sqlite3 -box "$DB" "SELECT name, ts, COUNT(*) AS n FROM top_scores GROUP BY name, ts ORDER BY ts DESC, name LIMIT 5;"

echo "== sample of latest set =="
sqlite3 -box "$DB" "
WITH latest AS (
  SELECT s.name, s.ts
  FROM top_scores s
  JOIN (SELECT name, MAX(ts) ts FROM top_scores GROUP BY name) m
    ON m.name=s.name AND m.ts=s.ts
  ORDER BY s.ts DESC
  LIMIT 1
)
SELECT s.name, s.ts, s.symbol, printf('%.4f', s.score) AS score
FROM top_scores s JOIN latest l ON l.name=s.name AND l.ts=s.ts
ORDER BY s.score DESC LIMIT 10;"

echo "== metrics_missing =="
sqlite3 -box "$DB" "
WITH latest AS (
  SELECT s.name, s.ts
  FROM top_scores s
  JOIN (SELECT name, MAX(ts) ts FROM top_scores GROUP BY name) m
    ON m.name=s.name AND m.ts=s.ts
  ORDER BY s.ts DESC
  LIMIT 1
)
SELECT s.symbol
FROM top_scores s JOIN latest l ON l.name=s.name AND l.ts=s.ts
LEFT JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.symbol IS NULL
LIMIT 20;"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
. /opt/scalp/project/.env
OLD=/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db
[ -f "$OLD" ] || { echo "Skip: no $OLD"; exit 0; }

has() { sqlite3 "$OLD" "SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='$1';"; }

# U: top_scores, candidates si présents
if [ "$(has top_scores)" = "1" ]; then
  sqlite3 "$UDB" "ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
  INSERT OR IGNORE INTO top_scores SELECT name,symbol,score,ts FROM old.top_scores;
  DETACH DATABASE old;"
fi
if [ "$(has candidates)" = "1" ]; then
  sqlite3 "$UDB" "ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
  INSERT OR IGNORE INTO candidates SELECT symbol,vol24,turn24,spread,score,ts FROM old.candidates;
  DETACH DATABASE old;"
fi

# A: ohlcv_* + contexts_A si présents
for T in ohlcv_1m ohlcv_5m ohlcv_15m ohlcv_30m contexts_A; do
  if [ "$(has $T)" = "1" ]; then
    case "$T" in
      contexts_A)
        sqlite3 "$ADB" "ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
        INSERT OR IGNORE INTO contexts_A(symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,ts)
        SELECT symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,ts FROM old.contexts_A;
        DETACH DATABASE old;"
      ;;
      *)
        sqlite3 "$ADB" "ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
        INSERT OR IGNORE INTO $T SELECT * FROM old.$T;
        DETACH DATABASE old;"
      ;;
    esac
  fi
done

# B: ticks + signals_B*
for T in ticks signals_B_plan signals_B; do
  if [ "$(has $T)" = "1" ]; then
    sqlite3 "$BDB" "ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
    INSERT OR IGNORE INTO $T SELECT * FROM old.$T;
    DETACH DATABASE old;"
  fi
done

# X: comptes/ordres/positions/trades si présents
if [ "$(has account_sim)" = "1" ]; then
  sqlite3 "$XDB" "ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
  INSERT OR REPLACE INTO account_sim(id,balance,equity,used_margin,leverage,ts)
  SELECT 1,COALESCE(balance,300),COALESCE(equity,300),COALESCE(used_margin,0),COALESCE(leverage,50),strftime('%s','now')
  FROM old.account_sim LIMIT 1; DETACH DATABASE old;"
fi
for T in orders_sim positions_open trades_closed; do
  if [ "$(has $T)" = "1" ]; then
    sqlite3 "$XDB" "ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
    INSERT OR IGNORE INTO $T SELECT * FROM old.$T; DETACH DATABASE old;"
  fi
done
echo "Migration tolérante OK."
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- Construire un pool large: dernier TOP35, TOP30, TOP100_VOL, FIXED5
WITH latest AS (
  SELECT name, MAX(ts) AS ts
  FROM top_scores
  WHERE name IN ('TOP35','TOP30','TOP100_VOL','FIXED5')
  GROUP BY name
),
pool AS (
  SELECT DISTINCT s.symbol
  FROM top_scores s
  JOIN latest l ON l.name=s.name AND l.ts=s.ts
)
-- Backfill métriques manquantes avec valeurs “safe”
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO metrics_universe(symbol, vol_usdt_24h, price, spread_bps, active)
SELECT p.symbol,
       2.0e7      AS vol_usdt_24h,  -- 20M USDT
       1.0        AS price,
       10.0       AS spread_bps,
       1          AS active
FROM pool p
LEFT JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.symbol IS NULL;
SQL
echo "Backfill done."

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
. /opt/scalp/project/.env
NOW=$(date +%s)

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- Défauts au cas où
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS retention_cfg(tf TEXT PRIMARY KEY, keep_secs INTEGER, keep_rows INTEGER);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO retention_cfg(tf,keep_secs,keep_rows) VALUES
 ('1m',  864000, 5000),
 ('5m', 5184000, 4000),
 ('15m',5184000, 3000),
 ('30m',5184000, 2000);

-- Purge temporelle
DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m  WHERE ts < $NOW - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='1m');
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m  WHERE ts < $NOW - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='5m');
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m WHERE ts < $NOW - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='15m');
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m WHERE ts < $NOW - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='30m');

-- Cap par symbole avec ROW_NUMBER (SQLite >=3.25)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid, ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn
    FROM ohlcv_1m
  ) WHERE rn > (SELECT keep_rows FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='1m')
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid, ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn
    FROM ohlcv_5m
  ) WHERE rn > (SELECT keep_rows FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='5m')
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid, ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn
    FROM ohlcv_15m
  ) WHERE rn > (SELECT keep_rows FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='15m')
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid, ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn
    FROM ohlcv_30m
  ) WHERE rn > (SELECT keep_rows FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='30m')
);

-- Contextes A: 7 jours
DELETE FROM contexts_A WHERE ts < $NOW - 604800;
SQL

sqlite3 "$BDB" "DELETE FROM ticks WHERE ts < $NOW - 172800; DELETE FROM signals_B_plan WHERE ts < $NOW - 259200; DELETE FROM signals_B WHERE created_ts < $NOW - 604800;"
sqlite3 "$XDB" "DELETE FROM orders_sim WHERE created_ts < $NOW - 2592000; DELETE FROM trades_closed WHERE closed_ts < $NOW - 15552000;"

echo "[clean_retention] done @ $NOW"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
now_ms=$(date +%s%3N)
echo "== ticks coverage =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$TDB" "SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) AS symbols, COUNT(*) AS rows FROM ticks;"
echo "== last per symbol (latency ms) =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$TDB" "
WITH last AS (
  SELECT symbol, MAX(ts_ms) AS ts FROM ticks GROUP BY symbol
)
SELECT l.symbol, l.ts, $now_ms - l.ts AS latency_ms
FROM last ORDER BY latency_ms;
"
echo "== rows last 5 min =="
cut_ms=$(( $(date +%s%3N) - 5*60*1000 ))
sqlite3 -tabs "$TDB" "
SELECT symbol, COUNT(*) FROM ticks
WHERE ts_ms >= $cut_ms
GROUP BY symbol ORDER BY 2 DESC LIMIT 10;"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
UDB="${UDB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
ADB="${ADB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"

attempts=0
max=5
while :; do
  if sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS u_syms(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
DELETE FROM u_syms;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO u_syms(symbol)
SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current;
COMMIT;
DETACH DATABASE udb;
SQL
  then
    echo "sync u.db → a.db.u_syms done"
    exit 0
  fi
  attempts=$((attempts+1))
  if [ $attempts -ge $max ]; then
    echo "sync failed after $attempts attempts" >&2
    exit 1
  fi
  sleep 1
done

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
N_KEEP="${N_KEEP_SIGNALS:-100000}"       # nb de signaux à garder
DAYS_KEEP="${DAYS_KEEP_SIGNALS:-14}"     # rétention (jours)

sqlite3 "$DB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=20000;

-- Cohérence : supprime ordres orphelins
DELETE FROM orders_sim
 WHERE signal_id NOT IN (SELECT id FROM signals_B);

-- Purge signals_B hors fenêtre (id anciens ET plus vieux que X jours)
DELETE FROM signals_B
 WHERE id NOT IN (SELECT id FROM signals_B ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT $N_KEEP)
   AND created_ts < strftime('%s','now','-$DAYS_KEEP days');

-- Index utiles (idempotents)
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_signalsB_created ON signals_B(created_ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_orders_sim_signal ON orders_sim(signal_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_orders_sim_created ON orders_sim(created_ts);

PRAGMA optimize;
PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE);
SQL

# VACUUM hebdo (verrou exclusif, court)
if [ "$(date +%u)" = "7" ]; then
  sqlite3 "$DB" "VACUUM;"
fi

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -e
BASE="/opt/scalp/project"
DATA="$BASE/data"
LOG="$BASE/logs"
mkdir -p "$DATA" "$LOG"

echo "[1] Sélection dynamique de coins..."
cat > "$BASE/scripts/top35_select.py" <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, json, time
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

con=sqlite3.connect(DB)
cur=con.cursor()

cur.execute("""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tops(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  name TEXT, symbol TEXT, vol REAL, vola REAL,
  turnover REAL, spread REAL, ts INTEGER
);
""")

# Simule la récupération des coins avec indicateurs (vol24h, turnover, volatilité)
symbols = [
    ("BTCUSDT", 1.0, 0.9, 1.0, 0.01),
    ("ETHUSDT", 0.8, 0.7, 0.8, 0.015),
    ("BNBUSDT", 0.7, 0.6, 0.7, 0.02),
    ("SOLUSDT", 0.6, 0.5, 0.6, 0.025),
    ("XRPUSDT", 0.5, 0.4, 0.5, 0.03)
]
# Ajoute 30 symboles factices pour simuler le tri
for i in range(30):
    symbols.append((f"ALT{i}USDT", 0.1+i*0.02, 0.1+i*0.015, 0.2+i*0.01, 0.05))

# Sélection par volatilité × volume
symbols.sort(key=lambda x: x[1]*x[2]*x[3]/x[4], reverse=True)
top35 = symbols[:35]
ts = int(time.time())

for sym in top35:
    cur.execute("INSERT INTO tops(name,symbol,vol,vola,turnover,spread,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                ("TOP35", sym[0], sym[1], sym[2], sym[3], sym[4], ts))
con.commit()
print(f"[TOP35] Enregistrés {len(top35)} paires à {ts}")
PY

chmod +x "$BASE/scripts/top35_select.py"
python3 "$BASE/scripts/top35_select.py" | tee "$LOG/top35_select.log"

echo "[2] Analyse A : génération de contexte"
cat > "$BASE/scripts/analyze_A.py" <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, json, time, statistics
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
OUT="/opt/scalp/project/data/analyse_A_out.json"
con=sqlite3.connect(DB)
cur=con.cursor()
rows=cur.execute("SELECT symbol,vol,vola,turnover,spread FROM tops WHERE ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM tops)").fetchall()
out={}
for sym,vol,vola,turn,sp in rows:
    ctx={
        "symbol":sym,
        "strength":round(vol*vola*turn/(sp+1e-6),6),
        "trend":"bull" if vola>0.5 else "bear",
        "volatility":vola,
        "turnover":turn,
        "spread":sp
    }
    out[sym]=ctx
with open(OUT,"w") as f: json.dump(out,f,indent=2)
print(f"[AnalyseA] {len(out)} contextes écrits dans {OUT}")
PY

chmod +x "$BASE/scripts/analyze_A.py"
python3 "$BASE/scripts/analyze_A.py" | tee "$LOG/analyze_A.log"

echo "[3] Analyse B : signaux affinés"
cat > "$BASE/scripts/analyze_B.py" <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, random, sqlite3
IN="/opt/scalp/project/data/analyse_A_out.json"
OUT="/opt/scalp/project/data/signals_B.json"
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

with open(IN) as f:
    ctx=json.load(f)

signals=[]
for sym,data in ctx.items():
    # score basé sur strength et trend
    strength=data["strength"]
    bias=1 if data["trend"]=="bull" else -1
    r=random.uniform(-0.3,0.3)
    signal_strength=strength*(1+r)
    if abs(signal_strength)>0.3:
        signals.append({
            "symbol":sym,
            "side":"buy" if bias>0 else "sell",
            "score":round(signal_strength,4),
            "reason":"ctx_strength",
            "created_ts":int(time.time())
        })

# écriture JSON
with open(OUT,"w") as f: json.dump(signals,f,indent=2)
print(f"[AnalyseB] {len(signals)} signaux raffinés -> {OUT}")

# insertion DB
con=sqlite3.connect(DB)
con.execute("""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
 symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
)
""")
for s in signals:
    con.execute("INSERT INTO signals_B(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)",
                (s["symbol"], s["side"], 0.0, s["reason"], s["created_ts"]))
con.commit()
con.close()
PY

chmod +x "$BASE/scripts/analyze_B.py"
python3 "$BASE/scripts/analyze_B.py" | tee "$LOG/analyze_B.log"

echo "[4] Vérification du flux DB"
sqlite3 "$DATA/scalp.db" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM tops;"
sqlite3 "$DATA/scalp.db" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM signals_B;"
echo "[OK] Pipeline Top35 → AnalyseA → AnalyseB terminé"
----- FILE END -----

Size: 1420
MTime: 2025-10-08 06:28:57.886121347 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TDB=/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db
KEEP_SECS=${KEEP_SECS:-900}      # 15 min
KEEP_ROWS=${KEEP_ROWS:-2000}     # par symbole
BATCH=${BATCH:-2000}             # deletes max par run
INC_VAC=${INC_VAC:-200}          # pages à libérer

sqlite3 "$TDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- 1) purge temporelle en lot
WITH c AS (SELECT strftime('%s','now')-$KEEP_SECS AS cut)
DELETE FROM ticks
 WHERE ts < (SELECT cut FROM c)
 LIMIT $BATCH;

-- 2) cap par symbole: supprime l'excès le plus ancien (sans window)
CREATE TEMP TABLE IF NOT EXISTS _sym(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
DELETE FROM _sym;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO _sym
SELECT symbol FROM ticks GROUP BY symbol
HAVING COUNT(*) > $KEEP_ROWS;

-- pour chaque symbole en excès, retire l'ancien surplus par lot
SQL

# boucle symboles excédentaires (minimise le temps bloquant)
sqlite3 -newline $'\n' -list "$TDB" "SELECT symbol FROM _sym;" | while read -r s; do
  [ -z "$s" ] && continue
  sqlite3 "$TDB" "
    DELETE FROM ticks
     WHERE symbol='$s'
       AND ts < (SELECT MIN(ts) FROM (
                   SELECT ts FROM ticks WHERE symbol='$s' ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT $KEEP_ROWS
                 ))
     LIMIT $BATCH;"
done

# 3) mini libération d'espace, non bloquante
sqlite3 "$TDB" "PRAGMA incremental_vacuum=$INC_VAC; PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(PASSIVE);"
echo "[clean_ticks_online] ok"
----- FILE END -----

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/migrate_ticks_ts_ms.sh
Size: 1230
MTime: 2025-10-10 10:48:50.074287407 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
sqlite3 "$TDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
-- si la colonne ts_ms existe déjà, rien à faire
SELECT 1 FROM pragma_table_info('ticks') WHERE name='ts_ms';
SQL
if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  sqlite3 "$TDB" ".schema ticks" | grep -q 'CREATE TABLE' || {
    echo "no ticks table, creating"
  }
  sqlite3 "$TDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
-- renommage si besoin
ALTER TABLE ticks RENAME TO ticks_old;
-- nouveau schéma
CREATE TABLE ticks(
  symbol  TEXT NOT NULL,
  instId  TEXT NOT NULL,
  tradeId TEXT NOT NULL,
  ts_ms   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  price   REAL NOT NULL,
  size    REAL NOT NULL,
  side    TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(instId, tradeId)
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_sym_ts ON ticks(symbol, ts_ms DESC);
-- tentative de copie depuis ancien schéma (ts en secondes ou ms)
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks(symbol,instId,tradeId,ts_ms,price,size,side)
SELECT
  COALESCE(symbol, instId) AS symbol,
  instId,
  COALESCE(tradeId, printf('%s-%d', instId, ts)) AS tradeId,
  CASE WHEN ts>1e12 THEN ts ELSE ts*1000 END AS ts_ms,
  price, size, side
FROM ticks_old;
DROP TABLE ticks_old;
COMMIT;
SQL
fi
echo "migration ticks: OK"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, websockets

URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
payload = {
    "op": "subscribe",
    "args": [
        {"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "trade", "instId": "BTCUSDT"},
        {"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "trade", "instId": "ETHUSDT"}
    ]
}

async def main():
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(payload))
        print(">>", payload)
        for _ in range(10):
            msg = await ws.recv()
            print("<<", msg)

asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
sqlite3 "$UDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- crée table universe si absente
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS universe (
  ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  name TEXT,
  score REAL,
  PRIMARY KEY(ts, symbol)
);

-- s'il existe une vue ou table _cand35, on prend la plus récente
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO universe(ts, symbol, name, score)
SELECT MAX(ts) AS ts, symbol, symbol AS name, score
FROM (
  SELECT ts, symbol, score FROM _cand35
  UNION ALL
  SELECT ts, symbol, 0.0 FROM _eligible_dedup
)
GROUP BY symbol;

-- vue standard
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_universe_current;
CREATE VIEW v_universe_current AS
SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM universe
ORDER BY symbol
LIMIT 35;
SQL

MTime: 2025-10-10 08:46:02.703201027 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
SCRIPTS="$ROOT/scripts"
LOG="$ROOT/logs/ohlcv_daemon.log"
STEP=300         # 5 min
OFFSET=1         # hh:mm:01
GRACE=4          # re-essai si la close n'est pas dispo
RETRY=1

mkdir -p "$ROOT/logs"

align() {
  now=$(date +%s)
  next=$(( now - (now % STEP) + STEP + OFFSET ))
  sleep $(( next - now ))
}

expected_ts() {
  # timestamp de la bougie 5m qui vient de se clore
  n=$(date +%s)
  echo $(( n - (n % STEP) ))
}

have_expected() {
  exp="$1"
  sqlite3 -noheader "$ROOT/data/a.db" "
SELECT MIN(ok) FROM (
  SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END ok FROM ohlcv_5m
  UNION ALL
  SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END FROM ohlcv_15m
  UNION ALL
  SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END FROM ohlcv_30m
);" 2>/dev/null
}

run_cycle() {
  "$SCRIPTS/fetch_ohlcv_once.sh"  >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  "$SCRIPTS/harden_o_db.sh"       >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  "$SCRIPTS/purge_non_current.sh" >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
}

while true; do
  align
  exp=$(expected_ts)
  run_cycle
  ok=$(have_expected "$exp" || echo 0)
  if [ "$ok" != "1" ] && [ "$RETRY" -gt 0 ]; then
    sleep "$GRACE"
    run_cycle
  fi
done
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

echo "🧹 Reset complet scalp paper trader..."

# 1️⃣ Stop tous les services avant nettoyage
systemctl stop scalp-paper.service scalp-router.service scalp-B.service 2>/dev/null || true

# 2️⃣ Réinitialise les tables clés
sqlite3 "$DB" <<"SQL"
PRAGMA foreign_keys=off;
DELETE FROM signals_B;
DELETE FROM orders_sim;
DELETE FROM positions_open;
DELETE FROM trades_closed;

UPDATE account_sim
   SET balance=100.0,
       equity=100.0,
       used_margin=0.0,
       updated_ts=strftime('%s','now')
 WHERE id=1;
PRAGMA foreign_keys=on;
SQL

# 3️⃣ Vérifie structure minimale
echo "📊 Tables présentes :"
sqlite3 "$DB" ".tables" | tr ' ' '\n' | grep -E 'signals_B|orders_sim|account_sim'

# 4️⃣ Relance services dans l'ordre logique
echo "🚀 Relance des services..."
systemctl restart scalp-B.service
sleep 2
systemctl restart scalp-router.service
sleep 2
systemctl restart scalp-paper.service
sleep 3

# 5️⃣ Vérifie santé et dernier signal
echo
echo "📈 État rapide :"
sqlite3 "$DB" -cmd ".mode column" -cmd ".headers on" "SELECT COUNT(*) AS signals_B FROM signals_B;"

echo
echo "✅ Reset complet et relance OK."

Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/build_a_once.sh
Size: 4783
MTime: 2025-10-10 09:59:29.724213066 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _src;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _src AS
SELECT symbol,'5m' tf,ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_5m
UNION ALL SELECT symbol,'15m',ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_15m
UNION ALL SELECT symbol,'30m',ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_30m;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _base;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _base AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,o,h,l,c,v,
       LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS cp
FROM _src;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _rsi;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _rsi AS
WITH g AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
         MAX(c-COALESCE(cp,c),0) AS g,
         MAX(COALESCE(cp,c)-c,0) AS l
  FROM _base
)
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       100-100.0/(1+AVG(g) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)
                    /NULLIF(AVG(l) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING),0)) AS rsi
FROM g;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _ema;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _ema AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       AVG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 9 PRECEDING)  AS ema_f,
       AVG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 21 PRECEDING) AS ema_s
FROM _base;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _macd;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _macd AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       (ema_f-ema_s) AS macd,
       AVG(ema_f-ema_s) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 8 PRECEDING) AS macd_sig
FROM _ema;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _adx;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _adx AS
WITH x AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,h,l,
         LAG(h) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS hp,
         LAG(l) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS lp
  FROM _base
),
dm AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
         MAX(h-COALESCE(hp,h),0) AS dmp,
         MAX(COALESCE(lp,l)-l,0) AS dmm
  FROM x
)
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       100*ABS(AVG(dmp) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)
             -AVG(dmm) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING))
       /(AVG(dmp) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)
        +AVG(dmm) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)+0.001) AS adx
FROM dm;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _obv;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _obv AS
WITH x AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,c,v,
         LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS cp
  FROM _base
),
o AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
         SUM(CASE WHEN cp IS NULL THEN 0
                  WHEN c>cp THEN v
                  WHEN c<cp THEN -v
                  ELSE 0 END) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS obv
  FROM x
)
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,obv,
       obv-LAG(obv,20) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS obv_slope
FROM o;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _merge;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _merge AS
SELECT b.symbol,b.tf,b.ts,b.c,b.v,
       e.ema_f,e.ema_s,m.macd,m.macd_sig,
       r.rsi,a.adx,o.obv_slope
FROM _base b
LEFT JOIN _ema e USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _macd m USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _rsi r USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _adx a USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _obv o USING(symbol,tf,ts);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _s_tf;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _s_tf AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       ((ema_f-ema_s)/NULLIF(ABS(ema_f)+ABS(ema_s),0))*0.4 +
       ((macd-macd_sig)/NULLIF(ABS(macd)+ABS(macd_sig),0))*0.3 +
       ((rsi-50)/50.0)*0.2 +
       ((adx-20)/20.0)*0.1 +
       (obv_slope/NULLIF(ABS(obv_slope)+1,0))*0.1 AS s
FROM _merge;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _S;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _S AS
WITH w AS (SELECT 0.5 AS w30,0.3 AS w15,0.2 AS w5)
SELECT s.symbol,
       SUM(CASE 
              WHEN tf='30m' THEN s.s*(SELECT w30 FROM w)
              WHEN tf='15m' THEN s.s*(SELECT w15 FROM w)
              WHEN tf='5m'  THEN s.s*(SELECT w5  FROM w)
              ELSE 0 END) AS S
FROM _s_tf s GROUP BY s.symbol;

-- Normalisation des probas: somme = 1
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _probs;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _probs AS
WITH raw AS (
  SELECT symbol,S,
         CASE WHEN S>0 THEN S ELSE 0 END AS pb_raw,
         CASE WHEN S<0 THEN -S ELSE 0 END AS ps_raw,
         CASE WHEN ABS(S)<=1 THEN 1-ABS(S) ELSE 0 END AS ph_raw
  FROM _S
),
z AS (
  SELECT symbol,S,pb_raw,ph_raw,ps_raw,(pb_raw+ph_raw+ps_raw) AS z FROM raw
)
SELECT symbol,S,
       CASE WHEN z=0 THEN 0.0 ELSE pb_raw/z END AS pb,
       CASE WHEN z=0 THEN 1.0 ELSE ph_raw/z END AS ph,
       CASE WHEN z=0 THEN 0.0 ELSE ps_raw/z END AS ps
FROM z;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _ctx;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _ctx AS
SELECT symbol,S,pb,ph,ps,
       CASE WHEN S>0.25 THEN 'bullish'
            WHEN S<-0.25 THEN 'bearish'
            ELSE 'range' END AS ctx
FROM _probs;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO a_context_state(symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,s,updated_at)
SELECT symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,S,datetime('now') FROM _ctx;

INSERT INTO a_signals(ts,symbol,s,pb,ph,ps,ctx)
SELECT datetime('now'),symbol,S,pb,ph,ps,ctx FROM _ctx;

COMMIT;
SQL

echo "A: build done (normalized probs)."
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
VER="${VER:?specify VER, ex: VER=analysisA-2025-10-10T12-00Z}"

# Health strict avant marquage
"$ROOT/bin/health_a_strict.sh" >/dev/null

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
DELETE FROM a_snapshots WHERE version='$VER';
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO a_final_marks(version, symbols, bullish, bearish, range)
SELECT '$VER',
       COUNT(*),
       SUM(ctx='bullish'),
       SUM(ctx='bearish'),
       SUM(ctx='range')
FROM a_context_state;

INSERT INTO a_snapshots(version, symbol, s, pb, ph, ps, ctx)
SELECT '$VER', symbol, s, pb, ph, ps, ctx
FROM a_context_state;
SQL

echo "A final marked: $VER"

Size: 626
MTime: 2025-10-10 12:11:04.510475959 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- création ou remplacement
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS a_context_state;
CREATE TABLE a_context_state AS
SELECT
  symbol,
  CASE WHEN prob_bull > prob_bear AND prob_bull > 0.55 THEN 'bullish'
       WHEN prob_bear > prob_bull AND prob_bear > 0.55 THEN 'bearish'
       ELSE 'range' END AS ctx,
  prob_bull AS pb,
  prob_hold AS ph,
  prob_sell AS ps,
  (prob_bull - prob_bear) AS s,
  datetime('now') AS updated_at
FROM a_signals;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_a_ctx_symbol ON a_context_state(symbol);
SQL

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
fail(){ echo "FAIL: $*" >&2; exit 1; }

echo "== latest plans =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$BDB" "
WITH last_ts AS (SELECT MAX(ts_utc) t FROM b_plans)
SELECT symbol, side, ROUND(score,2), ROUND(price,6), ROUND(sl,6), ROUND(tp,6),
       ROUND(size_usd,2), ROUND(vol_win,3)
FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT t FROM last_ts)
ORDER BY score DESC LIMIT 12;
"

WITH last_ts AS (SELECT MAX(ts_utc) t FROM b_plans),
chk AS (SELECT side, price, sl, tp FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT t FROM last_ts))
SELECT COUNT(*) FROM chk
WHERE (side='BUY'  AND NOT(sl<price AND tp>price))
   OR (side='SELL' AND NOT(sl>price AND tp<price));
")
[ "$bad" = "0" ] || fail "SL/TP incohérents ($bad)"

echo "OK: b.db health strict"

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="${ROOT:-/opt/scalp/project}"
BIN="$ROOT/bin"
DB="${DB:-$ROOT/data/u.db}"
VER="${VER:-universe-2025-10-09T16-28Z}"
mkdir -p "$BIN" "$(dirname "$DB")"

# 1) Table de release + pragma version
sqlite3 "$DB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
PRAGMA user_version=1001;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_release(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  file TEXT NOT NULL,
  sha256 TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  PRIMARY KEY(version,file)
);
SQL

# 2) build_universe.sh figé
cat > "$BIN/build_universe.sh" <<'SH'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$DB")"
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;

INSERT INTO universe_runs(started_at, status) VALUES(datetime('now'), 'running');
CREATE TEMP TABLE _run(id INTEGER); INSERT INTO _run VALUES (last_insert_rowid());
CREATE TEMP TABLE _status(ok INTEGER, reason TEXT); INSERT INTO _status VALUES (1,NULL);

CREATE TEMP TABLE _p AS
SELECT
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_usdt_volume_24h') AS REAL) AS min_vol,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_price') AS REAL) AS min_price,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='max_spread_bps') AS REAL) AS max_spread_bps,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_count') AS INTEGER) AS min_count,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='target_count') AS INTEGER) AS target_count,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='max_churn') AS REAL) AS max_churn;

-- Pool multi-sources
CREATE TEMP TABLE _latest AS
SELECT name, MAX(ts) AS ts
FROM top_scores
WHERE name IN ('TOP35','TOP30','TOP100_VOL','FIXED5')
GROUP BY name;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _pool0 AS
SELECT s.symbol, s.score, s.name,
       CASE s.name
         WHEN 'TOP35' THEN 1
         WHEN 'TOP30' THEN 2
         WHEN 'TOP100_VOL' THEN 3
         WHEN 'FIXED5' THEN 4
         ELSE 9
       END AS pri
FROM top_scores s
JOIN _latest l ON l.name=s.name AND l.ts=s.ts;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _pool AS
WITH ranked AS (
  SELECT symbol, score, name, pri,
         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY pri ASC, score DESC) AS r
  FROM _pool0
)
SELECT symbol, score, name, pri
FROM ranked
WHERE r=1
ORDER BY pri ASC, score DESC;

UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'no_top_scores')
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _pool)=0;

-- Filtres pass1
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible1 AS
SELECT p.symbol, p.score
FROM _pool p
JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p)
  AND p.symbol NOT IN (SELECT symbol FROM blacklist);

-- Whitelist + core
INSERT INTO _eligible1(symbol,score)
SELECT w.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM whitelist w
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=w.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p);

INSERT INTO _eligible1(symbol,score)
SELECT c.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM core_symbols c
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=c.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p);

-- Filtres pass2 relaxés si pass1 insuffisant
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible2 AS
SELECT p.symbol, p.score
FROM _pool p
JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p)
  AND p.symbol NOT IN (SELECT symbol FROM blacklist);

INSERT INTO _eligible2(symbol,score)
SELECT w.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM whitelist w
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=w.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p);

INSERT INTO _eligible2(symbol,score)
SELECT c.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM core_symbols c
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=c.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p);

-- Fusion + coupe
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible_final AS
SELECT symbol, MAX(score) AS score FROM (
  SELECT * FROM _eligible1
  UNION ALL
  SELECT * FROM _eligible2
  WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _eligible1) < (SELECT min_count FROM _p)
) GROUP BY symbol;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _cand AS
SELECT symbol, score
FROM _eligible_final
ORDER BY score DESC
LIMIT (SELECT target_count FROM _p);

-- Min requis
UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'too_few_symbols')
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _cand) < (SELECT min_count FROM _p);

-- Churn
CREATE TEMP TABLE _prev AS
SELECT symbol
FROM universe_snapshots
WHERE run_id = (SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs WHERE status='published' ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1);

CREATE TEMP TABLE _churn AS
WITH prev_c AS (SELECT COUNT(*) AS c FROM _prev),
inter_c AS (SELECT COUNT(*) AS c FROM _cand c JOIN _prev p USING(symbol)),
r AS (
  SELECT (SELECT c FROM prev_c) AS prev_cnt,
         (SELECT c FROM inter_c) AS inter_cnt,
         (SELECT target_count FROM _p) AS tgt,
         (SELECT max_churn FROM _p) AS max_churn
)
SELECT prev_cnt, inter_cnt, tgt,
       CASE WHEN tgt>0 THEN 1.0 - (1.0*inter_cnt/tgt) ELSE 1.0 END AS churn,
       max_churn
FROM r;

UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'high_churn')
WHERE (SELECT prev_cnt FROM _churn) = (SELECT tgt FROM _churn)
  AND (SELECT churn FROM _churn) > (SELECT max_churn FROM _churn);

-- Publication
INSERT INTO universe_snapshots(run_id, symbol)
SELECT (SELECT id FROM _run), symbol
FROM _cand
WHERE (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1;

UPDATE universe_runs
SET status = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1 THEN 'published' ELSE 'failed' END,
    finished_at = datetime('now'),
    count = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1 THEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _cand) END,
    reason = (SELECT reason FROM _status),
    symbol_list = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1
      THEN (SELECT GROUP_CONCAT(symbol, ',') FROM (SELECT symbol FROM _cand ORDER BY score DESC)) END
WHERE run_id=(SELECT id FROM _run);

COMMIT;
SQL

status=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT status FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
run_id=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
reason=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT reason FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
echo "run_id=$run_id status=$status reason=${reason:-none}"
[ "$status" = "published" ] && sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(*) AS count FROM v_universe_current;"
SH
chmod +x "$BIN/build_universe.sh"

# 3) health_universe.sh figé
cat > "$BIN/health_universe.sh" <<'SH'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
sqlite3 -tabs "$DB" "
WITH last AS (
  SELECT run_id, finished_at, count, reason
  FROM universe_runs WHERE status='published'
  ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1
)
SELECT 'run_id', run_id FROM last
UNION ALL SELECT 'finished_at', finished_at FROM last
UNION ALL SELECT 'count', count FROM last
UNION ALL SELECT 'available_now', (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_universe_current);
"
SH
chmod +x "$BIN/health_universe.sh"

# 4) run_universe_daemon.sh figé
cat > "$BIN/run_universe_daemon.sh" <<'SH'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
INTERVAL_SEC="${INTERVAL_SEC:-7200}"
RETRY_DELAY="${RETRY_DELAY:-600}"
MAX_RETRY="${MAX_RETRY:-2}"

while true; do
  if DB="$DB" "$(dirname "$0")/build_universe.sh"; then
    sleep "$INTERVAL_SEC"
  else
    i=0
    while [ $i -lt $MAX_RETRY ]; do
      sleep "$RETRY_DELAY"
      if DB="$DB" "$(dirname "$0")/build_universe.sh"; then
        break
      fi
      i=$((i+1))
    done
    sleep "$INTERVAL_SEC"
  fi
done
SH
chmod +x "$BIN/run_universe_daemon.sh"

# 5) Empreintes et enregistrement
for f in build_universe.sh health_universe.sh run_universe_daemon.sh; do
  sha=$(sha256sum "$BIN/$f" | awk '{print $1}')
  sqlite3 "$DB" "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO code_release(version,file,sha256) VALUES('$VER','$f','$sha');"
done

echo "Release $VER figée dans $BIN et enregistrée dans $DB"
----- FILE END -----

Size: 2694
MTime: 2025-10-07 10:22:14.591413905 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF;

-- 1) Champs requis
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS orders_sim(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  signal_id INTEGER, symbol TEXT, side TEXT,
  qty REAL, price REAL, used_margin REAL, created_ts INTEGER, ts INTEGER
);
-- ajoute created_ts si manquant
WITH t AS (SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='orders_sim')
SELECT 1 FROM t;  -- no-op
-- add column if needed
-- (ALTER TABLE fails if exists, so guarded)
WITH cols AS (SELECT name AS col FROM pragma_table_info('orders_sim'))
SELECT 1 FROM cols WHERE col='created_ts';

-- si la colonne n'existe pas, on l'ajoute
-- sqlite3 ne supporte pas IF NOT EXISTS ici, on teste côté shell
SQL
# si la colonne n'existe pas, l'ajouter
if ! sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA table_info(orders_sim);" | awk -F'|' '$2=="created_ts"{f=1}END{exit !f}'; then
  sqlite3 "$DB" "ALTER TABLE orders_sim ADD COLUMN created_ts INTEGER;"
fi

# 2) Vues santé
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_health;
CREATE VIEW v_health AS
WITH
s AS (
  SELECT
    COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) AS last_sig,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE created_ts >= strftime('%s','now')-60) AS ticks_60s
  FROM signals_B
),
o AS (
  SELECT
    COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) AS last_ord,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE created_ts >= strftime('%s','now')-60) AS orders_60s
  FROM orders_sim
)
SELECT
  datetime(s.last_sig,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_sig_dt,
  datetime(o.last_ord,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ord_dt,
  s.ticks_60s,
  o.orders_60s
FROM s,o;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_progress;
CREATE VIEW v_progress AS
WITH
a AS (SELECT balance,equity,COALESCE(used_margin,0) AS used_margin, COALESCE(leverage,50) AS leverage, updated FROM account_sim LIMIT 1),
rp AS (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(pnl),0) AS realized_pnl FROM trades_closed),
op AS (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(u_pnl),0) AS open_pnl FROM positions_open),
s AS (SELECT COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) AS last_sig FROM signals_B),
o AS (SELECT COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) AS last_ord FROM orders_sim)
SELECT
  datetime((SELECT last_sig FROM s),'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_sig_dt,
  datetime((SELECT last_ord FROM o),'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ord_dt,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM signals_B WHERE created_ts>=strftime('%s','now')-60) AS ticks_60s,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders_sim WHERE created_ts>=strftime('%s','now')-60) AS orders_60s,
  a.balance, a.equity, a.used_margin, a.leverage,
  ROUND((SELECT realized_pnl FROM rp),6) AS realized_pnl,
  ROUND((SELECT open_pnl FROM op),6)     AS open_pnl,
  datetime(a.updated,'unixepoch','localtime') AS updated
FROM a;

SQL

echo "[OK] v_health et v_progress recréées."
----- FILE END -----

Size: 1642
MTime: 2025-10-07 09:28:45.757602917 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF;

-- Tables minimales
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS account_sim(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  balance REAL, equity REAL, used_margin REAL,
  updated INTEGER, leverage REAL
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS router_state(k TEXT PRIMARY KEY, v INTEGER);

-- Remise à zéro du compte
WITH cur AS (SELECT COALESCE(leverage,50.0) AS lev FROM account_sim LIMIT 1)
INSERT INTO account_sim(balance,equity,used_margin,updated,leverage)
SELECT 300.0, 300.0, 0.0, strftime('%s','now'), COALESCE((SELECT lev FROM cur),50.0)
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM account_sim);
UPDATE account_sim
   SET balance=300.0,
       equity=300.0,
       used_margin=0.0,
       updated=strftime('%s','now');

-- Purge ordres/positions/trades
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS positions_open;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS trades_closed;
CREATE TABLE positions_open(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  order_id INTEGER, symbol TEXT, side TEXT,
  qty REAL, entry_price REAL, last REAL, u_pnl REAL,
  opened_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE trades_closed(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, side TEXT, qty REAL,
  entry_price REAL, exit_price REAL, pnl REAL,
  opened_ts INTEGER, closed_ts INTEGER
);

-- Garder orders_sim mais le vider proprement
DELETE FROM orders_sim;

-- Router: repartir depuis ~100 ticks avant le dernier disponible
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO router_state(k,v) VALUES('last_signal_id',0);
WITH m AS (SELECT COALESCE(MAX(id),0) AS mx FROM signals_B)
UPDATE router_state SET v=MAX(0,(SELECT mx FROM m)-100) WHERE k='last_signal_id';

VACUUM;
SQL
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- Charger seuils
WITH cfg AS (SELECT * FROM retention_cfg)
-- 5m : garde les 1000 plus récentes / symbole
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM ohlcv_5m t2 WHERE t2.symbol=ohlcv_5m.symbol AND t2.ts>=ohlcv_5m.ts)
      > (SELECT keep_rows FROM cfg WHERE tf='5m');

-- 15m
WITH cfg AS (SELECT * FROM retention_cfg)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM ohlcv_15m t2 WHERE t2.symbol=ohlcv_15m.symbol AND t2.ts>=ohlcv_15m.ts)
      > (SELECT keep_rows FROM cfg WHERE tf='15m');

-- 30m
WITH cfg AS (SELECT * FROM retention_cfg)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM ohlcv_30m t2 WHERE t2.symbol=ohlcv_30m.symbol AND t2.ts>=ohlcv_30m.ts)
      > (SELECT keep_rows FROM cfg WHERE tf='30m');

-- Purge aussi par temps si au-delà du max (sécurité)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m  WHERE ts < strftime('%s','now') - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='5m');
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m WHERE ts < strftime('%s','now') - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='15m');
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m WHERE ts < strftime('%s','now') - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='30m');
SQL

# Reclaim disque
sqlite3 "$ADB" 'VACUUM;'

#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

has_col(){ sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA table_info(account_sim);" | awk -F'|' -v c="$1" '$2==c{f=1}END{exit !f}'; }

# purge
sqlite3 "$DB" "
PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF;
DELETE FROM orders_sim;
DELETE FROM positions_open;
DELETE FROM trades_closed;
DELETE FROM signals_B;
UPDATE router_state SET v=0 WHERE k='last_signal_id';
DELETE FROM account_sim;
"

# insert selon schéma présent
if has_col floating_pnl; then
  sqlite3 "$DB" "
  INSERT INTO account_sim(balance,equity,floating_pnl,used_margin,updated,leverage)
  VALUES(300.0,300.0,0.0,0.0,strftime('%s','now'),50);
  VACUUM;"
else
  sqlite3 "$DB" "
  INSERT INTO account_sim(balance,equity,used_margin,updated,leverage)
  VALUES(300.0,300.0,0.0,strftime('%s','now'),50);
  VACUUM;"
fi

echo '[RESET] OK: balance=equity=300, used_margin=0, leverage=50'

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db
UDB=/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- 1) Voir u.db
ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;

-- 2) Univers = TOP30 courant + 5 fixes
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS universe_keep;
CREATE TABLE universe_keep(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO universe_keep(symbol)
SELECT symbol
FROM udb.top_scores
WHERE name='TOP30'
  AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM udb.top_scores WHERE name='TOP30')
LIMIT 30;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO universe_keep(symbol)
VALUES ('BTCUSDT'),('ETHUSDT'),('BNBUSDT'),('SOLUSDT'),('XRPUSDT');

-- 3) Supprime tout ce qui n’est pas dans l’univers (NOT EXISTS évite le piège NULL)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m  AS t WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM universe_keep u WHERE u.symbol=t.symbol);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m  AS t WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM universe_keep u WHERE u.symbol=t.symbol);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m AS t WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM universe_keep u WHERE u.symbol=t.symbol);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m AS t WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM universe_keep u WHERE u.symbol=t.symbol);

DETACH DATABASE udb;

-- 4) Cap N barres/symbole par TF (keep_rows dans retention_cfg)
-- helper: retourne seuil
CREATE TEMP TABLE _kr(tf TEXT PRIMARY KEY, n INTEGER);
INSERT INTO _kr SELECT tf, keep_rows FROM retention_cfg;

-- 1m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM ohlcv_1m x
  WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_1m y WHERE y.symbol=x.symbol AND y.ts>=x.ts)
        > (SELECT n FROM _kr WHERE tf='1m')
);

-- 5m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM ohlcv_5m x
  WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_5m y WHERE y.symbol=x.symbol AND y.ts>=x.ts)
        > (SELECT n FROM _kr WHERE tf='5m')
);

-- 15m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM ohlcv_15m x
  WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_15m y WHERE y.symbol=x.symbol AND y.ts>=x.ts)
        > (SELECT n FROM _kr WHERE tf='15m')
);

-- 30m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM ohlcv_30m x
  WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_30m y WHERE y.symbol=x.symbol AND y.ts>=x.ts)
        > (SELECT n FROM _kr WHERE tf='30m')
);

VACUUM;
SQL
echo "[purge_universe_and_cap] done"

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/build_b_once.sh
Size: 3461
MTime: 2025-10-10 12:18:45.277774751 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
TDB="$ROOT/data/t.db"
UDB="$ROOT/data/u.db"
BDB="$ROOT/data/b.db"

SQLQ=$(cat <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$ADB"' AS adb;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$TDB"' AS tdb;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$UDB"' AS udb;

-- Paramètres
WITH P AS (
  SELECT
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='min_score_buy')   AS REAL) AS min_sb,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='max_score_sell')  AS REAL) AS max_ss,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='lookback_sec')    AS INTEGER) AS lb,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='min_sl_pct')      AS REAL) AS min_sl,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='rr')              AS REAL) AS rr,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='size_usd_base')   AS REAL) AS sbase,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='size_scale')      AS REAL) AS sscale
)
-- Univers en cours
, U AS (
  SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current
)
-- Score A normalisé 0..100 et flag BUY/SELL/NONE
, A AS (
  SELECT s.symbol,
         50.0 + 50.0*MAX(MIN(s.s,1.0),-1.0) AS score,
         CASE
           WHEN s.s>=0.25 THEN 'BUY'
           WHEN s.s<=-0.25 THEN 'SELL'
           ELSE 'NONE'
         END AS flag
  FROM adb.a_context_state s
  JOIN U USING(symbol)
)
-- Référence ticks sur fenêtre lookback
, REF AS (
  SELECT
    symbol,
    MAX(ts_ms) AS ts_last,
    MAX(price) AS pmax,
    MIN(price) AS pmin,
    (SELECT price FROM tdb.ticks t2 WHERE t2.symbol=t.symbol ORDER BY ts_ms DESC LIMIT 1) AS plast
  FROM tdb.ticks t
  WHERE ts_ms >= (CAST(strftime('%s','now') AS INTEGER)*1000 - (SELECT lb*1000 FROM P))
  GROUP BY symbol
)
-- Candidats BUY
, CB AS (
  SELECT A.symbol,'BUY' AS side, A.score, R.plast, R.pmax, R.pmin,
         CASE WHEN R.plast>0 THEN (R.pmax-R.pmin)/R.plast*100 ELSE 0 END AS vol_pct
  FROM A JOIN REF R USING(symbol), P
  WHERE A.flag='BUY' AND A.score >= (SELECT min_sb FROM P)
)
-- Candidats SELL
, CS AS (
  SELECT A.symbol,'SELL' AS side, A.score, R.plast, R.pmax, R.pmin,
         CASE WHEN R.plast>0 THEN (R.pmax-R.pmin)/R.plast*100 ELSE 0 END AS vol_pct
  FROM A JOIN REF R USING(symbol), P
  WHERE A.flag='SELL' AND A.score <= (SELECT max_ss FROM P)
)
, C AS (SELECT * FROM CB UNION ALL SELECT * FROM CS)
-- Gestion du risque: SL% = max(vol*1.2, min_sl)
, RISK AS (
  SELECT C.*,
         MAX(vol_pct*1.20, (SELECT min_sl FROM P)) AS sl_pct,
         (SELECT rr FROM P) AS rr,
         (SELECT sbase FROM P) AS sbase,
         (SELECT sscale FROM P) AS sscale
  FROM C
)
-- Plan: SL/TP/size
, PLAN AS (
  SELECT
    symbol, side, score,
    plast AS price,
    CASE WHEN side='BUY'  THEN plast*(1.0 - sl_pct/100.0)
         ELSE plast*(1.0 + sl_pct/100.0) END AS sl,
    CASE WHEN side='BUY'  THEN plast*(1.0 + (sl_pct*rr)/100.0)
         ELSE plast*(1.0 - (sl_pct*rr)/100.0) END AS tp,
    MIN(MAX(sbase*(1.0 + sscale*((score-60.0)/40.0)), sbase*0.5), sbase*3.0) AS size_usd,
    vol_pct
  FROM RISK
)
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO b_plans(ts_utc,symbol,side,score,price,sl,tp,size_usd,vol_win,src)
SELECT datetime('now'), symbol, side, score, price, sl, tp, size_usd, vol_pct, 'ticks' FROM PLAN;

DETACH DATABASE adb; DETACH DATABASE tdb; DETACH DATABASE udb;
SQL
)

# retries soft contre "database is locked"
for i in 1 2 3 4 5; do
  if sqlite3 "$BDB" "$SQLQ"; then
    echo "B: build ok"; exit 0
  fi
  sleep 0.8
done
echo "B: build failed (locked)"; exit 1
----- FILE END -----

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/freeze_a_release.sh
Size: 1391
MTime: 2025-10-10 09:54:51.436342062 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
BIN="$ROOT/bin"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
mkdir -p "$BIN"

# Tables de versionnage si absentes
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_release(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  file TEXT NOT NULL,
  sha256 TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  PRIMARY KEY(version,file)
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS a_final_marks(
  version TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  symbols INTEGER NOT NULL,
  bullish INTEGER NOT NULL,
  bearish INTEGER NOT NULL,
  range   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS a_snapshots(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  s REAL NOT NULL, pb REAL NOT NULL, ph REAL NOT NULL, ps REAL NOT NULL, ctx TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(version,symbol)
);
SQL

# Figer scripts
install -m 0755 "$ROOT/scripts/build_a_once.sh"   "$BIN/build_a_once.sh"

Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/fix_universe_view.sh
Size: 503
MTime: 2025-10-10 11:51:32.006729196 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
sqlite3 "$UDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_universe_current;
CREATE VIEW v_universe_current AS
WITH ranked AS (
  SELECT symbol,
         MAX(ts) AS ts_max
  FROM universe
  GROUP BY symbol
),
latest AS (
  SELECT u.symbol, u.ts, u.name
  FROM universe u
  JOIN ranked r ON u.symbol=r.symbol AND u.ts=r.ts_max
)
SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM latest
WHERE symbol IS NOT NULL
ORDER BY symbol
LIMIT 35;
SQL
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
VER="${VER:?specify VER}"

echo "== CODE HASHES =="
sqlite3 -csv "$ADB" "SELECT file,sha256 FROM code_release ORDER BY file" 2>/dev/null | while IFS=, read -r f ref; do
  [ -f "$ROOT/bin/$f" ] || { echo "$f missing"; continue; }
  cur=$(sha256sum "$ROOT/bin/$f" | awk '{print $1}')
  match=no; [ "$cur" = "$ref" ] && match=yes
  echo "$f expected=$ref current=$cur match=$match"
done

echo "== FINAL MARKS =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "SELECT version, tf, max_ts, symbols, rows_per_symbol, created_at FROM o_final_marks WHERE version='$VER' ORDER BY tf;"

echo "== HEALTH STRICT =="
"$ROOT/bin/health_o_strict.sh"

ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"

Size: 1631
MTime: 2025-10-08 10:07:51.451320178 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
LOCK="/opt/scalp/locks/a.db.lock"
SQL_BLOCK=$(cat <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=60000;
BEGIN; -- DEFERRED pour éviter le lock immédiat
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ctx_A_last3(
  symbol TEXT,
  ts_ctx INTEGER,
  decision TEXT,
  pB REAL, pS REAL, pH REAL,
  ts_5m INTEGER, age_5m_min REAL,
  ts_15m INTEGER, age_15m_min REAL,
  ts_30m INTEGER, age_30m_min REAL,
  updated_ts INTEGER,
  PRIMARY KEY(symbol, updated_ts)
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ctx_A_last3
(symbol,ts_ctx,decision,pB,pS,pH,ts_5m,age_5m_min,ts_15m,age_15m_min,ts_30m,age_30m_min,updated_ts)
SELECT a.symbol, a.ts,
  CASE WHEN a.pB>=0.55 AND a.pS<=0.35 THEN 'BUY'
       WHEN a.pS>=0.55 AND a.pB<=0.35 THEN 'SELL'
       WHEN a.pH>=a.pB AND a.pH>=a.pS THEN 'HOLD'
       ELSE 'NONE' END,
  ROUND(a.pB,3), ROUND(a.pS,3), ROUND(a.pH,3),
  f5.ts,  ROUND((strftime('%s','now')-f5.ts)/60.0,1),
  f15.ts, ROUND((strftime('%s','now')-f15.ts)/60.0,1),
  f30.ts, ROUND((strftime('%s','now')-f30.ts)/60.0,1),
  strftime('%s','now')
FROM ctx_A a
LEFT JOIN v_ctx_tf_5m  f5  USING(symbol)
LEFT JOIN v_ctx_tf_15m f15 USING(symbol)
LEFT JOIN v_ctx_tf_30m f30 USING(symbol);

DELETE FROM ctx_A_last3
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY updated_ts DESC) rn
    FROM ctx_A_last3
  ) t WHERE t.rn>3
);
COMMIT;
SQL
)
# Retry avec attente exponentielle
for i in 1 2 3 4 5; do
  if /usr/bin/flock -w 120 "$LOCK" /usr/bin/sqlite3 -batch "$DB" "$SQL_BLOCK"; then
    exit 0
  fi
  sleep $(( i*i ))
done
echo "snapshot: échec après retries" >&2
exit 1
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="${ROOT:-/opt/scalp/project}"
DB="${DB:-$ROOT/data/u.db}"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS final_marks(
  version TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  run_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
  count INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);
WITH last_pub AS (
  SELECT run_id, count FROM universe_runs
  WHERE status='published'
  ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1
)
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO final_marks(version, run_id, count)
SELECT '$VER', run_id, count FROM last_pub;
SQL

echo "Final mark created for version=$VER"

MTime: 2025-10-09 17:56:27.796461901 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$DB")"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- Sources
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(
  ts TEXT NOT NULL,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  score REAL NOT NULL
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_top_scores_name_ts ON top_scores(name, ts);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS metrics_universe(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  vol_usdt_24h REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  price REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  spread_bps REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 9999,
  active INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1
);

-- Paramètres et listes
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS params(
  key TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  value TEXT NOT NULL
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO params(key,value) VALUES
 ('min_usdt_volume_24h','10000000'),
 ('min_price','0.01'),
 ('max_spread_bps','15'),
 ('min_count','28'),
 ('target_count','35'),
 ('max_churn','0.6'),
 ('score_list_primary','TOP35'),
 ('score_list_fallback','TOP50');

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS whitelist(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS blacklist(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS core_symbols(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO core_symbols(symbol) VALUES ('BTCUSDT'),('ETHUSDT');

-- Publications
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS universe_runs(
  run_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
  started_at TEXT NOT NULL,
  finished_at TEXT,
  status TEXT NOT NULL,             -- running | failed | published
  reason TEXT,
  count INTEGER,
  symbol_list TEXT
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_status_finished ON universe_runs(status, finished_at);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS universe_snapshots(
  run_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(run_id, symbol),
  FOREIGN KEY(run_id) REFERENCES universe_runs(run_id)
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_snapshots_run ON universe_snapshots(run_id);

-- Vue courante lisible par o.db
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_universe_current AS
SELECT s.symbol
FROM universe_snapshots s
WHERE s.run_id = (
  SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs
  WHERE status='published'
  ORDER BY finished_at DESC
  LIMIT 1
);

-- Meta de debug
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_universe_meta AS
WITH last AS (
  SELECT run_id, finished_at FROM universe_runs
  WHERE status='published'
  ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1
)
SELECT s.symbol, l.run_id, l.finished_at AS published_at
FROM last l
JOIN universe_snapshots s USING(run_id);
SQL

echo "DDL applied on $DB"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

# positions_open.side NULL -> 'buy'
sqlite3 "$DB" "UPDATE positions_open SET side='buy' WHERE side IS NULL OR TRIM(side)='';"

# créer account_sim si absent
sqlite3 "$DB" "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS account_sim(balance REAL, equity REAL);"

# ajouter colonne updated si absente
if ! sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA table_info(account_sim);" | awk -F'|' '$2=="updated"{f=1}END{exit !f}'; then
  sqlite3 "$DB" "ALTER TABLE account_sim ADD COLUMN updated INTEGER;"
fi

# initialiser une ligne si vide
if [ "$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM account_sim;")" = "0" ]; then
  sqlite3 "$DB" "INSERT INTO account_sim(balance,equity,updated) VALUES(1000,1000,strftime('%s','now'));"
fi

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="${ADB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"

echo "== coverage per TF (symbols x rows) =="
for t in ohlcv_5m ohlcv_15m ohlcv_30m; do
  printf -- "-- %s\n" "$t"
  sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol), SUM(cnt)
    FROM (SELECT symbol, COUNT(*) cnt FROM $t GROUP BY symbol);"
done

echo "== gaps check (0 attendu) =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "
WITH tf(name,step) AS (VALUES('ohlcv_5m',300),('ohlcv_15m',900),('ohlcv_30m',1800)),
rows AS (
  SELECT 'ohlcv_5m' name,300 step,symbol,COUNT(*) n,MIN(ts) t0,MAX(ts) t1 FROM ohlcv_5m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_15m',900,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_30m',1800,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m GROUP BY symbol
),
gaps AS (
  SELECT name, symbol, MAX(0, ((t1-t0)/step + 1 - n)) AS missing FROM rows
)
SELECT name, SUM(missing) FROM gaps GROUP BY name;"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, websockets

URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"
# Format exact attendu par Bitget : instId complet, suffixe _UMCBL pour USDT-M futures
SYMBOLS = ["BTCUSDT_UMCBL","ETHUSDT_UMCBL","SOLUSDT_UMCBL"]

async def main():
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20) as ws:
        sub = {"op":"subscribe","args":[f"trade:{s}" for s in SYMBOLS]}
        await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
        print(">> sent:", sub)
        for _ in range(10):
            msg = await ws.recv()
            print("<<", msg)

asyncio.run(main())
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
source /opt/scalp/project/.env
OLD=/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db
[ -f "$OLD" ] || { echo "Skip: $OLD absent"; exit 0; }

# univers
sqlite3 "$UDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO top_scores SELECT name,symbol,score,ts FROM old.top_scores;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO candidates SELECT symbol,vol24,turn24,spread,score,ts FROM old.candidates;
DETACH DATABASE old;
SQL

# OHLCV + contexts_A
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ohlcv_1m  SELECT * FROM old.ohlcv_1m;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ohlcv_5m  SELECT * FROM old.ohlcv_5m;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ohlcv_15m SELECT * FROM old.ohlcv_15m;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ohlcv_30m SELECT * FROM old.ohlcv_30m;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO contexts_A SELECT symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,ts,NULL FROM old.contexts_A;
DETACH DATABASE old;
SQL

# ticks + B
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks SELECT symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask FROM old.ticks;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO signals_B_plan SELECT id,symbol,ctx,side,score,entry,sl,tp,ts FROM old.signals_B_plan;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO signals_B SELECT id,symbol,side,price,created_ts FROM old.signals_B;
DETACH DATABASE old;
SQL

# x: account/orders/positions/trades
sqlite3 "$XDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$OLD' AS old;
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO account_sim(id,balance,equity,used_margin,leverage,ts)
SELECT 1,COALESCE(balance,300),COALESCE(equity,300),COALESCE(used_margin,0),COALESCE(leverage,50),strftime('%s','now')
FROM old.account_sim LIMIT 1;

INSERT OR IGNORE INTO orders_sim      SELECT * FROM old.orders_sim;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO positions_open  SELECT * FROM old.positions_open;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO trades_closed   SELECT * FROM old.trades_closed;
DETACH DATABASE old;
SQL

echo "Migration OK."

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="${ADB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"

# 1) Dédoublonner (garde la + récente par (symbol,ts))
for T in 5m 15m 30m; do
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
DELETE FROM ohlcv_${T}
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol, ts ORDER BY rowid DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_${T}
  ) WHERE rn > 1
);
SQL
done

# 2) Compacter à exactement 100 bougies / symbole
for T in 5m 15m 30m; do
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
DELETE FROM ohlcv_${T}
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_${T}
  ) WHERE rn > 100
);
SQL
done

# 3) Contrainte d’unicité (après dédup, donc ça passe)
for T in 5m 15m 30m; do
sqlite3 "$ADB" "CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS uq_ohlcv_${T} ON ohlcv_${T}(symbol, ts);"
done

echo "o.db durci: dedup + 100 fixes + unique(symbol,ts)."

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/compact_ohlcv_universe.sh
Size: 1623
MTime: 2025-10-07 21:11:46.974116943 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db
UDB=/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db

# 1) construire l'univers (TOP30 courant + 5 fixes)
sqlite3 "$ADB" "DROP TABLE IF EXISTS universe_keep;"
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
CREATE TABLE universe_keep(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO universe_keep(symbol)
SELECT symbol FROM '$UDB'.top_scores
WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM '$UDB'.top_scores WHERE name='TOP30')
LIMIT 30;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO universe_keep(symbol) VALUES
 ('BTCUSDT'),('ETHUSDT'),('BNBUSDT'),('SOLUSDT'),('XRPUSDT');
SQL

# 2) supprime tout ce qui n'est pas dans l'univers
for T in ohlcv_1m ohlcv_5m ohlcv_15m ohlcv_30m; do
  sqlite3 "$ADB" "DELETE FROM $T WHERE symbol NOT IN (SELECT symbol FROM universe_keep);"
done

# 3) cap N barres/symbole par TF (keep_rows depuis retention_cfg)
cap_tf() {
  local tbl=$1 tf=$2
  local keep
  keep=$(sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT keep_rows FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='$tf';")
  [ -z "$keep" ] && keep=1000
  # pour chaque symbole de l'univers: calcule ts_cut = MIN(ts) des keep dernières barres
  sqlite3 -csv "$ADB" "SELECT symbol FROM universe_keep;" | while read -r sym; do
    [ -z "$sym" ] && continue
    ts_cut=$(sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT MIN(ts) FROM (SELECT ts FROM $tbl WHERE symbol='$sym' ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT $keep);")
    [ -z "$ts_cut" ] && continue
    sqlite3 "$ADB" "DELETE FROM $tbl WHERE symbol='$sym' AND ts < $ts_cut;"
  done
}

cap_tf ohlcv_1m  1m
cap_tf ohlcv_5m  5m
cap_tf ohlcv_15m 15m
cap_tf ohlcv_30m 30m

# 4) vacuum pour récupérer l'espace
sqlite3 "$ADB" 'VACUUM;'
echo "[compact_ohlcv_universe] done"
