MTime: 2025-10-09 18:01:06.952654814 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
INTERVAL_SEC="${INTERVAL_SEC:-7200}"   # 2h
RETRY_DELAY="${RETRY_DELAY:-600}"      # 10m
MAX_RETRY="${MAX_RETRY:-2}"

while true; do
  if ./build_universe.sh; then
    sleep "$INTERVAL_SEC"
  else
    i=0
    while [ $i -lt $MAX_RETRY ]; do
      sleep "$RETRY_DELAY"
      if ./build_universe.sh; then
        break
      fi
      i=$((i+1))
    done
    sleep "$INTERVAL_SEC"
  fi
done
----- FILE END -----

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/build_universe.sh
Size: 6789
MTime: 2025-10-09 18:21:07.955111277 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$DB")"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

BEGIN IMMEDIATE;

INSERT INTO universe_runs(started_at, status) VALUES(datetime('now'), 'running');
CREATE TEMP TABLE _run(id INTEGER); INSERT INTO _run VALUES (last_insert_rowid());
CREATE TEMP TABLE _status(ok INTEGER, reason TEXT); INSERT INTO _status VALUES (1,NULL);

-- Params
CREATE TEMP TABLE _p AS
SELECT
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_usdt_volume_24h') AS REAL) AS min_vol,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_price') AS REAL) AS min_price,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='max_spread_bps') AS REAL) AS max_spread_bps,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_count') AS INTEGER) AS min_count,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='target_count') AS INTEGER) AS target_count,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='max_churn') AS REAL) AS max_churn;

-- == POOL MULTI-SOURCES ==
-- Récupère le dernier ts par liste
CREATE TEMP TABLE _latest AS
SELECT name, MAX(ts) AS ts
FROM top_scores
WHERE name IN ('TOP35','TOP30','TOP100_VOL','FIXED5')
GROUP BY name;

-- Union avec priorité: TOP35 > TOP30 > TOP100_VOL > FIXED5
CREATE TEMP TABLE _pool0 AS
SELECT s.symbol, s.score, s.name,
       CASE s.name
         WHEN 'TOP35' THEN 1
         WHEN 'TOP30' THEN 2
         WHEN 'TOP100_VOL' THEN 3
         WHEN 'FIXED5' THEN 4
         ELSE 9
       END AS pri
FROM top_scores s
JOIN _latest l ON l.name=s.name AND l.ts=s.ts;

-- Dédup en gardant la meilleure priorité puis meilleur score
CREATE TEMP TABLE _pool AS
WITH ranked AS (
  SELECT symbol, score, name, pri,
         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY pri ASC, score DESC) AS r
  FROM _pool0
)
SELECT symbol, score, name, pri
FROM ranked
WHERE r=1
ORDER BY pri ASC, score DESC;

-- Si pool vide -> fail
UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'no_top_scores')
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _pool)=0;

-- == FILTRES PASS 1 ==
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible1 AS
SELECT p.symbol, p.score
FROM _pool p
JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p)
  AND p.symbol NOT IN (SELECT symbol FROM blacklist);

-- Whitelist + core soumis aux mêmes métriques
INSERT INTO _eligible1(symbol,score)
SELECT w.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM whitelist w
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=w.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p);

INSERT INTO _eligible1(symbol,score)
SELECT c.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM core_symbols c
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=c.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p);

-- == FILTRES PASS 2 RELAXÉS (si besoin) ==
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible2 AS
SELECT p.symbol, p.score
FROM _pool p
JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)     -- volume ÷2
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p) -- spread ×2
  AND p.symbol NOT IN (SELECT symbol FROM blacklist);

INSERT INTO _eligible2(symbol,score)
SELECT w.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM whitelist w
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=w.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p);

INSERT INTO _eligible2(symbol,score)
SELECT c.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM core_symbols c
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=c.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p);

-- Choix final: eligible1, et si insuffisant on ajoute des relaxés
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible_final AS
SELECT symbol, MAX(score) AS score FROM (
  SELECT * FROM _eligible1
  UNION ALL
  SELECT * FROM _eligible2
  WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _eligible1) < (SELECT min_count FROM _p)
) GROUP BY symbol;

-- Coupe à target_count
CREATE TEMP TABLE _cand AS
SELECT symbol, score
FROM _eligible_final
ORDER BY score DESC
LIMIT (SELECT target_count FROM _p);

-- Minimum requis sinon fail
UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'too_few_symbols')
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _cand) < (SELECT min_count FROM _p);

-- Churn check si précédent complet
CREATE TEMP TABLE _prev AS
SELECT symbol
FROM universe_snapshots
WHERE run_id = (SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs WHERE status='published' ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1);

CREATE TEMP TABLE _churn AS
WITH prev_c AS (SELECT COUNT(*) AS c FROM _prev),
inter_c AS (SELECT COUNT(*) AS c FROM _cand c JOIN _prev p USING(symbol)),
r AS (
  SELECT (SELECT c FROM prev_c) AS prev_cnt,
         (SELECT c FROM inter_c) AS inter_cnt,
         (SELECT target_count FROM _p) AS tgt,
         (SELECT max_churn FROM _p) AS max_churn
)
SELECT prev_cnt, inter_cnt, tgt,
       CASE WHEN tgt>0 THEN 1.0 - (1.0*inter_cnt/tgt) ELSE 1.0 END AS churn,
       max_churn
FROM r;

UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'high_churn')
WHERE (SELECT prev_cnt FROM _churn) = (SELECT tgt FROM _churn)
  AND (SELECT churn FROM _churn) > (SELECT max_churn FROM _churn);

-- Publication conditionnelle
INSERT INTO universe_snapshots(run_id, symbol)
SELECT (SELECT id FROM _run), symbol
FROM _cand
WHERE (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1;

UPDATE universe_runs
SET status = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1 THEN 'published' ELSE 'failed' END,
    finished_at = datetime('now'),
    count = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1 THEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _cand) END,
    reason = (SELECT reason FROM _status),
    symbol_list = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1
      THEN (SELECT GROUP_CONCAT(symbol, ',') FROM (SELECT symbol FROM _cand ORDER BY score DESC)) END
WHERE run_id=(SELECT id FROM _run);

COMMIT;
SQL

# Résumé
status=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT status FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
run_id=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
reason=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT reason FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
echo "run_id=$run_id status=$status reason=${reason:-none}"
[ "$status" = "published" ] && sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(*) AS count FROM v_universe_current;"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
BASE="/opt/scalp/project"

echo "[1] stop writers"
pkill -f ws_ctx_ticks || true
pkill -f analyse_A_ctx.py || true
pkill -f materialize_indicators || true

echo "[2] purge WAL/locks"
command -v fuser >/dev/null && fuser -k "$DB" 2>/dev/null || true
rm -f "${DB}-wal" "${DB}-shm"

echo "[3] backup"
cp -f "$DB" "${DB}.bak.$(date +%s)"

echo "[4] integrity_check"
if ! sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA quick_check;" | grep -qx "ok"; then
  echo "[4a] recover -> new db"
  if sqlite3 "$DB" ".recover" >/opt/scalp/project/data/recover.sql 2>/dev/null; then
    mv "$DB" "${DB}.broken.$(date +%s)" || true
    sqlite3 "$DB" ".read /opt/scalp/project/data/recover.sql"
  else
    echo "[4b] dump fallback"
    sqlite3 "$DB" ".output /opt/scalp/project/data/dump.sql" ".dump" ".output stdout"
    mv "$DB" "${DB}.broken.$(date +%s)" || true
    sqlite3 "$DB" ".read /opt/scalp/project/data/dump.sql"
  fi
fi

echo "[5] DDL index OHLCV"
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_5m (symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL, PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts));
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_15m AS SELECT * FROM ohlcv_5m WHERE 0;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_30m AS SELECT * FROM ohlcv_5m WHERE 0;
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ohlcv_5m_sym_ts  ON ohlcv_5m(symbol,ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ohlcv_15m_sym_ts ON ohlcv_15m(symbol,ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ohlcv_30m_sym_ts ON ohlcv_30m(symbol,ts);
SQL

echo "[6] DDL tables indic matérialisées"
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS indic_5m(
  symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
  close REAL, sma20 REAL, sma50 REAL,
  macd REAL, macd_sig REAL, macd_hist REAL,
  rsi14 REAL, atr14 REAL, atr_pct REAL, obv REAL,
  PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts)
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS indic_15m AS SELECT * FROM indic_5m WHERE 0;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS indic_30m AS SELECT * FROM indic_5m WHERE 0;
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_indic5m_symbol_ts  ON indic_5m(symbol,ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_indic15m_symbol_ts ON indic_15m(symbol,ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_indic30m_symbol_ts ON indic_30m(symbol,ts);
SQL

echo "[7] Retention: garde N barres récentes"
# 5m: 4000 (~14 j), 15m: 3000 (~31 j), 30m: 3000 (~62 j)
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
WITH mx AS (SELECT MAX(ts) mx FROM ohlcv_5m)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m WHERE ts < (SELECT mx-4000*300 FROM mx);
WITH mx AS (SELECT MAX(ts) mx FROM ohlcv_15m)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m WHERE ts < (SELECT mx-3000*900 FROM mx);
WITH mx AS (SELECT MAX(ts) mx FROM ohlcv_30m)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m WHERE ts < (SELECT mx-3000*1800 FROM mx);

WITH mx AS (SELECT MAX(ts) mx FROM indic_5m)
DELETE FROM indic_5m WHERE ts < (SELECT mx-4000*300 FROM mx);
WITH mx AS (SELECT MAX(ts) mx FROM indic_15m)
DELETE FROM indic_15m WHERE ts < (SELECT mx-3000*900 FROM mx);
WITH mx AS (SELECT MAX(ts) mx FROM indic_30m)
DELETE FROM indic_30m WHERE ts < (SELECT mx-3000*1800 FROM mx);
SQL

echo "[8] VACUUM + ANALYZE"
sqlite3 "$DB" "VACUUM; ANALYZE;"

echo "[9] OK"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
PIDF="$ROOT/run/ticks.pid"
LOG="$ROOT/logs/ticks_daemon.log"
mkdir -p "$ROOT/run" "$ROOT/logs"

case "${1:-start}" in
  start)
    [ -f "$PIDF" ] && [ -d "/proc/$(cat "$PIDF" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)" ] && { echo "already running"; exit 0; }
    nohup python3 -u "$ROOT/scripts/ws_ticks_writer_v2.py" >>"$LOG" 2>&1 &
    echo $! > "$PIDF"
    echo "started pid=$(cat "$PIDF")"
    ;;
  stop)
    if [ -f "$PIDF" ]; then kill "$(cat "$PIDF")" 2>/dev/null || true; rm -f "$PIDF"; echo "stopped"; else echo "not running"; fi
    ;;
  status)
    if [ -f "$PIDF" ] && [ -d "/proc/$(cat "$PIDF" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)" ]; then echo "running pid=$(cat "$PIDF")"; else echo "not running"; fi
    ;;
  restart)
    "$0" stop; sleep 1; "$0" start;;
  *) echo "usage: $0 {start|stop|status|restart}"; exit 1;;
esac

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
fail(){ echo "FAIL: $*" >&2; exit 1; }

# schéma
cols=$(sqlite3 -noheader "$TDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pragma_table_info('ticks') WHERE name IN ('symbol','instId','tradeId','ts_ms','price','size','side');")
[ "$cols" -eq 7 ] || fail "schema columns"

# set vs univers
setdiff=$(sqlite3 -noheader -separator '|' "$TDB" "
ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
WITH cur AS (SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM ticks),
     uni AS (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)
SELECT (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM uni)) AS extra,
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM uni EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur)) AS missing;
DETACH DATABASE udb;")
echo "setdiff extra|missing: $setdiff"

# fraîcheur et couverture 5 min
echo "== recent =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$TDB" "
WITH now AS (SELECT CAST(strftime('%s','now') AS INTEGER)*1000 AS n),
     cut AS (SELECT (SELECT n FROM now)-5*60*1000 AS c)
SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ticks WHERE ts_ms >= (SELECT c FROM cut);
"
echo "== latency =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$TDB" "
WITH now AS (SELECT CAST(strftime('%s','now') AS INTEGER)*1000 AS n),
     last AS (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts_ms) ts FROM ticks GROUP BY symbol)
SELECT symbol, (SELECT n FROM now)-ts AS latency_ms FROM last ORDER BY latency_ms LIMIT 10;
"

echo "OK: ticks health strict"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db

sqlite3 "$ADB" "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS retention_cfg(tf TEXT PRIMARY KEY, keep_secs INTEGER);"

 ('1m',  864000, 5000),
 ('5m', 5184000, 4000),
 ('15m',5184000, 3000),
 ('30m',5184000, 2000);

UPDATE retention_cfg SET keep_rows=4000  WHERE tf='5m'  AND (keep_rows IS NULL OR keep_rows=0);
UPDATE retention_cfg SET keep_rows=3000  WHERE tf='15m' AND (keep_rows IS NULL OR keep_rows=0);
UPDATE retention_cfg SET keep_rows=2000  WHERE tf='30m' AND (keep_rows IS NULL OR keep_rows=0);
SQL

echo "[patch_retention_keep_rows] ok"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/fix_ticks_schema.sh
Size: 1690
MTime: 2025-10-10 10:52:54.738557571 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

has_tsms=$(sqlite3 "$TDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pragma_table_info('ticks') WHERE name='ts_ms';")
if [ "$has_tsms" = "1" ]; then
  echo "ticks already OK"; exit 0
fi

sqlite3 "$TDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
-- si pas de table ticks, rien à migrer
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(symbol TEXT, instId TEXT, tradeId TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, size REAL, side TEXT);
ALTER TABLE ticks RENAME TO ticks_old;

CREATE TABLE ticks(
  symbol  TEXT NOT NULL,
  instId  TEXT NOT NULL,
  tradeId TEXT NOT NULL,
  ts_ms   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  price   REAL NOT NULL,
  size    REAL NOT NULL,
  side    TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(instId, tradeId)
);

-- cas 1: ancienne colonne ts en secondes ou ms
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks(symbol,instId,tradeId,ts_ms,price,size,side)
SELECT
  COALESCE(symbol, instId) AS symbol,
  COALESCE(instId, symbol) AS instId,
  COALESCE(tradeId, printf('%s-%d', COALESCE(instId,symbol), ts)) AS tradeId,
  CASE WHEN ts>1e12 THEN ts ELSE ts*1000 END AS ts_ms,
  price, size, side
FROM ticks_old
WHERE tradeId IS NOT NULL OR ts IS NOT NULL;

-- cas 2: ancien schéma prix/bid/ask/ts (à défaut de tradeId)
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks(symbol,instId,tradeId,ts_ms,price,size,side)
SELECT
  symbol,
  symbol AS instId,
  printf('%s-%d', symbol, ts) AS tradeId,
  CASE WHEN ts>1e12 THEN ts ELSE ts*1000 END AS ts_ms,
  price, 0.0, ''    -- pas de size/side dispo
FROM ticks_old
WHERE tradeId IS NULL AND ts IS NOT NULL AND price IS NOT NULL;

DROP TABLE ticks_old;
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_sym_ts ON ticks(symbol, ts_ms DESC);
COMMIT;
SQL
echo "ticks schema fixed"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TDB=/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db
NOW=$(date +%s)

sqlite3 "$TDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- Config rétention
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks_retention(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK(id=1),
  keep_secs INTEGER,   -- horizon temps max (ex: 900 = 15 min)
  keep_rows INTEGER    -- cap par symbole
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks_retention(id,keep_secs,keep_rows) VALUES(1,900,2000);

-- 1) purge temporelle
DELETE FROM ticks WHERE ts < $NOW - (SELECT keep_secs FROM ticks_retention WHERE id=1);

-- 2) cap par symbole: garde les N derniers rowid par symbole
WITH cfg AS (SELECT keep_rows n FROM ticks_retention WHERE id=1)
SELECT 1;

-- liste des symboles
SQL

# cap par symbole sans window
sqlite3 -newline $'\n' -list "$TDB" "SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM ticks;" | while read -r sym; do
  [ -z "$sym" ] && continue
  keep=$(sqlite3 "$TDB" "SELECT keep_rows FROM ticks_retention WHERE id=1;")
  sqlite3 "$TDB" "
    DELETE FROM ticks
    WHERE symbol='$sym'
      AND rowid NOT IN (
        SELECT rowid FROM ticks
        WHERE symbol='$sym'
        ORDER BY ts DESC
        LIMIT $keep
      );
  "
done

echo "[clean_ticks] done"
----- FILE END -----

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, gzip, time, sqlite3, websockets, os, signal

UDB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
TDB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
CAP = 35
REFRESH_SEC = 300
PING_SEC = 20
KEEP_ROWS_PER_SYM = int(os.getenv("KEEP_ROWS", "2000"))
KEEP_SECS = int(os.getenv("KEEP_SECS", "900"))  # 15 min

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except: 
        try: return b.decode()
        except: return ""

def tdb_init():
    con = sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None, timeout=10)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
        symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
        ts INTEGER NOT NULL,          -- seconds
        price REAL NOT NULL,
        bid REAL NOT NULL,
        ask REAL NOT NULL,
        PRIMARY KEY(symbol, ts)
    )""")
    con.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_sym_ts ON ticks(symbol,ts)")
    con.close()

def top35():
    # univers courant
    con = sqlite3.connect(UDB)
    cur = con.execute("SELECT symbol FROM v_universe_current LIMIT ?", (CAP,))
    syms = [r[0].upper() for r in cur.fetchall()]
    con.close()
    return [s for s in syms if s.endswith("USDT")][:CAP]

def build_sub_args(syms):
    # v2 public, USDT-FUTURES, suffix UMCBL
    # {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT_UMCBL"}, ...]}
    return [{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId": s+"_UMCBL"} for s in syms]

def parse_msg(msg):
    """
    Forme v2:
    {"action":"snapshot"|"update",
     "arg":{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT_UMCBL"},
     "data":[{"lastPr":"...", "bestBid":"...","bestAsk":"...","ts":"..."}]}
    """
    out = []
    if not isinstance(msg, dict): return out
    if msg.get("action") not in ("snapshot","update"): return out
    arg = msg.get("arg") or {}
    instId = (arg.get("instId") or "").upper()
    if not instId: return out
    sym = instId.split("_")[0]  # BTCUSDT
    for d in msg.get("data", []):
        try:
            last = float(d.get("lastPr") or d.get("last"))
            bid  = float(d.get("bestBid") or last)
            ask  = float(d.get("bestAsk") or last)
            tsms = int(d.get("ts") or d.get("systemTime") or (time.time()*1000))
            ts   = tsms // 1000
            out.append((sym, ts, last, bid, ask))
        except Exception:
            continue
    return out

def write_rows(rows):
    if not rows: return
    con = sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None, timeout=10)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.executemany("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,bid,ask) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    # purge temporelle
    now = int(time.time())
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM ticks WHERE ts < ?", (now - KEEP_SECS,))
    con.commit()
    con.close()
    # purge par symbole sans window
    for sym in {r[0] for r in rows}:
        con = sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None, timeout=10)
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute(f"""
        DELETE FROM ticks
        WHERE symbol=? AND rowid NOT IN (
          SELECT rowid FROM ticks WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT ?
        )""", (sym, sym, KEEP_ROWS_PER_SYM))
        con.commit()
        con.close()

async def ws_loop():
    tdb_init()
    current = set()
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        last_ping = time.time()
        last_refresh = 0
        while True:
            now = time.time()
            if now - last_refresh > REFRESH_SEC or not current:
                want = set(top35())
                add  = sorted(want - current)
                rem  = sorted(current - want)
                if rem:
                    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"unsubscribe","args":build_sub_args(rem)}))
                if add:
                    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":build_sub_args(add)}))
                current = want
                last_refresh = now
                print("T: universe", len(current), sorted(list(current))[:10], flush=True)
            if now - last_ping > PING_SEC:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"})); last_ping = now
            try:
                raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=3.0)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                continue
            msg = ungzip(raw) if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)) else raw
            try:
                obj = json.loads(msg)
            except Exception:
                continue
            if isinstance(obj, dict) and obj.get("event") in ("error","subscribe","unsubscribe"):
                print("T:", obj, flush=True)
                continue
            rows = parse_msg(obj)
            if rows: write_rows(rows)

async def run():
    while True:
        try:
            await ws_loop()
        except Exception as e:
            print("T: ws_err", e, "→ reconnect in 3s", flush=True)
            await asyncio.sleep(3)

def main():
    loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
    for sig in (signal.SIGINT, signal.SIGTERM):
        try: loop.add_signal_handler(sig, loop.stop)
        except NotImplementedError: pass
    loop.run_until_complete(run())

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
BDB="$ROOT/data/b.db"
VER="${VER:?specify VER, ex: VER=analysisB-2025-10-10T12-00Z}"

sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_final_marks(
  version TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  ts_utc TEXT NOT NULL,
  n_pairs INTEGER NOT NULL,
  n_buy INTEGER NOT NULL,
  n_sell INTEGER NOT NULL,
  avg_score REAL NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_snapshots(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  side TEXT NOT NULL,
  score REAL NOT NULL,
  price REAL NOT NULL,
  sl REAL NOT NULL,
  tp REAL NOT NULL,
  size_usd REAL NOT NULL,
  ts_utc TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(version,symbol)
);

WITH last AS (SELECT MAX(ts_utc) t FROM b_plans),
rows AS (SELECT * FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT t FROM last))
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO b_final_marks(version, ts_utc, n_pairs, n_buy, n_sell, avg_score)
SELECT '$VER',
       (SELECT t FROM last),
       COUNT(*),
       SUM(side='BUY'),
       SUM(side='SELL'),
       COALESCE(AVG(score),0)
FROM rows;

DELETE FROM b_snapshots WHERE version='$VER';
INSERT INTO b_snapshots(version,symbol,side,score,price,sl,tp,size_usd,ts_utc)
SELECT '$VER',symbol,side,score,price,sl,tp,size_usd,ts_utc
FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT MAX(ts_utc) FROM b_plans);
SQL

echo "B final marked: $VER"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB=/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db

sqlite3 "$DB" -cmd ".headers on" -cmd ".mode column" "
-- === Snapshot global ===
SELECT datetime(updated,'unixepoch','localtime') AS updated,
       ROUND(balance,6)  AS balance,
       ROUND(equity,6)   AS equity,
       ROUND(floating_pnl,6) AS floating_pnl,
       used_margin,
       open_positions, closed_trades,
       sig_1min, sig_5min, ord_1min, ord_5min
FROM v_paper_monitor;

-- === Totaux PnL ===
SELECT ROUND(COALESCE(SUM(u_pnl),0),6) AS open_pnl FROM positions_open;
SELECT ROUND(COALESCE(SUM(pnl),0),6)    AS realized_pnl FROM trades_closed;

-- === Positions ouvertes (10 récentes) ===
SELECT id,symbol,
       ROUND(qty,6) AS qty,
       ROUND(entry_price,6) AS entry,
       ROUND(last,6) AS last,
       ROUND(u_pnl,6) AS u_pnl,
       datetime(opened_ts,'unixepoch','localtime') AS opened
FROM positions_open
ORDER BY opened_ts DESC
LIMIT 10;

-- === Dernières positions fermées (10 dernières) ===
SELECT id,symbol,
       ROUND(qty,6) AS qty,
       ROUND(entry_price,6) AS entry,
       ROUND(exit_price,6) AS exit,
       ROUND(pnl,6) AS pnl,
       datetime(opened_ts,'unixepoch','localtime') AS opened,
       datetime(closed_ts,'unixepoch','localtime') AS closed
FROM trades_closed
ORDER BY id DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
BIN="$ROOT/bin"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
VER="${VER:-ohlcv-$(date -u +%F-T%H%MZ)}"
mkdir -p "$BIN"

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_release(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  file TEXT NOT NULL,
  sha256 TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  PRIMARY KEY(version,file)
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS o_final_marks(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  tf TEXT NOT NULL,              -- 5m | 15m | 30m
  max_ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
  symbols INTEGER NOT NULL,
  rows_per_symbol INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  PRIMARY KEY(version, tf)
);
SQL

# Figer scripts côté bin
install -m 0755 run_ohlcv_daemon.sh "$BIN/run_ohlcv_daemon.sh"
install -m 0755 fetch_ohlcv_once.sh "$BIN/fetch_ohlcv_once.sh"
install -m 0755 harden_o_db.sh "$BIN/harden_o_db.sh"
install -m 0755 purge_non_current.sh "$BIN/purge_non_current.sh"
install -m 0755 health_o_db.sh "$BIN/health_o_db.sh"

for f in run_ohlcv_daemon.sh fetch_ohlcv_once.sh harden_o_db.sh purge_non_current.sh health_o_db.sh; do
  sha=$(sha256sum "$BIN/$f" | awk '{print $1}')
  sqlite3 "$ADB" "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO code_release(version,file,sha256) VALUES('$VER','$f','$sha');"
done
echo "o.db release figée: $VER"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, sqlite3, math
DB="data/scalp.db"
TP_BPS     = float(os.getenv("TP_BPS","15"))       # take profit en bps
SL_BPS     = float(os.getenv("SL_BPS","20"))       # stop loss   en bps
MAX_HOLD   = int(os.getenv("MAX_HOLD_SEC","900"))  # 15 min
FEES_BPS   = float(os.getenv("FEES_BPS","1"))      # aller+retour
POLL       = 0.5

def connect():
    con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=20, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=20000")
    con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    return con

def last_price(con, symbol, default):
    row=con.execute("SELECT last FROM last_ticks WHERE symbol=?", (symbol,)).fetchone()
    return (row[0] if row else default) or default

def ensure_qty(q): return 1.0 if (q is None or q==0.0) else float(q)

def open_new_positions(con, now):
    rows=con.execute("""
      SELECT id,symbol,side,COALESCE(qty,0),COALESCE(price,0),created_ts
      FROM orders_sim
      WHERE status='SIMULATED' AND id NOT IN (SELECT order_id FROM positions_sim)
      ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 500
    """).fetchall()
    if not rows: return 0
    con.execute("BEGIN IMMEDIATE")
    for oid,sym,side,qty,px,ts in rows:
        px = px or last_price(con, sym, None) or 0.0
        q  = ensure_qty(qty)
        con.execute("""INSERT OR IGNORE INTO positions_sim
            (order_id,symbol,side,qty,entry_price,entry_ts,status)
            VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?, 'OPEN')""", (oid,sym,side,q,px,ts or now))
    con.execute("COMMIT")
    return len(rows)

def close_if_needed(con, now):
    rows=con.execute("""
      SELECT id, order_id, symbol, side, qty, entry_price, entry_ts
      FROM positions_sim WHERE status='OPEN'
      ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 1000
    """).fetchall()
    if not rows: return 0
    n_closed=0
    con.execute("BEGIN IMMEDIATE")
    for pid,oid,sym,side,qty,entry,ets in rows:
        last=last_price(con, sym, entry)
        hold= now - (ets or now)
        # Targets
        tp = entry*(1 + (TP_BPS/10000.0)) if side.upper()=='BUY'  else entry*(1 - (TP_BPS/10000.0))
        sl = entry*(1 - (SL_BPS/10000.0)) if side.upper()=='BUY'  else entry*(1 + (SL_BPS/10000.0))
        reason=None; exit_px=None
        if side.upper()=='BUY':
            if last>=tp: exit_px=last; reason='TP'
            elif last<=sl: exit_px=last; reason='SL'
        else: # SELL
            if last<=tp: exit_px=last; reason='TP'
            elif last>=sl: exit_px=last; reason='SL'
        if reason is None and hold>=MAX_HOLD:
            exit_px=last; reason='TIME'
        if reason is None:
            # Reverse signal ferme la position si ordre plus récent sens opposé
            rev = con.execute("""
              SELECT 1 FROM orders_sim
              WHERE symbol=? AND created_ts>? AND
                    ((side='BUY'  AND ?='SELL') OR (side='SELL' AND ?='BUY'))
              LIMIT 1
            """,(sym, ets or 0, side.upper(), side.upper())).fetchone()
            if rev: exit_px=last; reason='REV'
        if exit_px is not None:
            # PnL: BUY => (exit-entry)*qty ; SELL => (entry-exit)*qty ; moins fees
            gross = (exit_px-entry)*qty if side.upper()=='BUY' else (entry-exit_px)*qty
            fees  = (entry+exit_px)*qty*(FEES_BPS/10000.0)
            pnl   = gross - fees
            pnl_bps = (pnl/ (entry*qty)) * 10000.0 if entry>0 and qty>0 else 0.0
            con.execute("""UPDATE positions_sim
                           SET exit_price=?, exit_ts=?, pnl_abs=?, pnl_bps=?,
                               fees_abs=?, status='CLOSED', close_reason=?
                           WHERE id=?""",
                           (exit_px, now, pnl, pnl_bps, fees, reason, pid))
            n_closed+=1
    con.execute("COMMIT")
    return n_closed

def main():
    con=connect()
    while True:
        now=int(time.time())
        opened=open_new_positions(con, now)
        closed=close_if_needed(con, now)
        if opened==0 and closed==0:
            time.sleep(POLL)
----- FILE END -----

Size: 3005
MTime: 2025-10-08 07:19:48.853367762 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, requests, sqlite3

DB   = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
BASE = "https://api.bitget.com"
FIX  = ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]

FALLBACK = [  # ordre volumique standard si l'API ne répond pas
 "BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","DOGEUSDT","ADAUSDT","TRXUSDT",
 "LINKUSDT","LTCUSDT","DOTUSDT","BCHUSDT","AVAXUSDT","APTUSDT","XLMUSDT","ATOMUSDT",
 "NEARUSDT","FILUSDT","SUIUSDT","ARBUSDT","HBARUSDT","OPUSDT","MATICUSDT","TONUSDT",
 "INJUSDT","TIAUSDT","AAVEUSDT","ETCUSDT","ALGOUSDT","ICPUSDT"
]

def jget(url, params=None, retries=3, tout=12):
    for _ in range(retries+1):
        try:
            r = requests.get(url, params=params or {}, timeout=tout)
            if r.status_code == 200:
                return r.json()
            time.sleep(0.4)
        except Exception:
            time.sleep(0.4)
    return None

def fetch_top_by_volume():
    # 1) v2
    j = jget(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/tickers", {"productType":"umcbl"})
    if j and j.get("code") == "00000" and isinstance(j.get("data"), list):
        rows=[]
        for d in j["data"]:
            s = (d.get("symbol") or "").replace("_UMCBL","")
            vol = float(d.get("usdtVolume") or d.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
            if s.endswith("USDT") and vol>0: rows.append((s,vol))
        rows.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        return [s for s,_ in rows[:30]]

    # 2) v1 (secours)
    j = jget(f"{BASE}/api/mix/v1/market/tickers", {"productType":"umcbl"})
    if j and j.get("code") == "00000" and isinstance(j.get("data"), list):
        rows=[]
        for d in j["data"]:
            s = (d.get("symbol") or "").replace("_UMCBL","")
            vol = float(d.get("usdtVolume") or d.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
            if s.endswith("USDT") and vol>0: rows.append((s,vol))
        rows.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        return [s for s,_ in rows[:30]]

    # 3) statique
    return FALLBACK[:30]

def ensure_schema():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB); c = con.cursor()
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(
                  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                  name TEXT, symbol TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER)""")
    con.commit(); con.close()

def write_top(name, syms):
    # force 5 fixes
    for f in FIX:
        if f not in syms: syms.append(f)
    syms = syms[:30]
    ts = int(time.time())
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB); c = con.cursor()
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    c.executemany("INSERT INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?)",
                  [(name, s, i+1, ts) for i,s in enumerate(syms)])
    con.commit(); con.close()
    return ts, syms

def main():
    ensure_schema()
    top = fetch_top_by_volume()
    ts, syms = write_top("TOP30", top)
    print(f"[TOP30] {len(syms)} écrits @ {ts}")
    for i,s in enumerate(syms,1):
        print(f"{i:2d}. {s}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, ccxt
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
TF_MAP={"5m":"ohlcv_5m","15m":"ohlcv_15m","30m":"ohlcv_30m"}
MS={"5m":5*60*1000,"15m":15*60*1000,"30m":30*60*1000}
LIMIT=300
ex=ccxt.bitget({'options':{'defaultType':'swap'},'enableRateLimit':True})
con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=15, isolation_level=None)
cur=con.cursor()
syms=[r[0] for r in cur.execute("""
  SELECT symbol FROM top_scores
  WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30')
  ORDER BY score DESC, symbol ASC LIMIT 30
""")]
now=int(time.time()*1000)
for s in syms:
    for tf, tbl in TF_MAP.items():
        try:
            rows=ex.fetch_ohlcv(s, timeframe=tf, since=now-LIMIT*MS[tf], limit=LIMIT)
            if not rows: 
                print("EMPTY", s, tf); 
                continue
            cur.executemany(f"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {tbl}(symbol,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                            [(s,int(t[0]//1000),float(t[1]),float(t[2]),float(t[3]),float(t[4]),float(t[5])) for t in rows])
            print(s, tf, len(rows))
        except Exception as e:
            print("ERR", s, tf, e)
con.close()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, random, sqlite3
IN="/opt/scalp/project/data/analyse_A_out.json"
OUT="/opt/scalp/project/data/signals_B.json"
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

with open(IN) as f:
    ctx=json.load(f)

signals=[]
for sym,data in ctx.items():
    # score basé sur strength et trend
    strength=data["strength"]
    bias=1 if data["trend"]=="bull" else -1
    r=random.uniform(-0.3,0.3)
    signal_strength=strength*(1+r)
    if abs(signal_strength)>0.3:
        signals.append({
            "symbol":sym,
            "side":"buy" if bias>0 else "sell",
            "score":round(signal_strength,4),
            "reason":"ctx_strength",
            "created_ts":int(time.time())
        })

# écriture JSON
with open(OUT,"w") as f: json.dump(signals,f,indent=2)
print(f"[AnalyseB] {len(signals)} signaux raffinés -> {OUT}")

# insertion DB
con=sqlite3.connect(DB)
con.execute("""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
 symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
)
""")
for s in signals:
    con.execute("INSERT INTO signals_B(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)",
                (s["symbol"], s["side"], 0.0, s["reason"], s["created_ts"]))
con.commit()
con.close()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, time
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except: 
        try: return b.decode()
        except: return ""
async def main():
    args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"},
          {"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"ETHUSDT"}]
    n=0
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))
        t0=time.time()
        while time.time()-t0<15:
            try: raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=3)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"})); continue
            msg=ungzip(raw)
            try: obj=json.loads(msg)
            except: continue
            if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
                n+=1
                a=obj["arg"]; d=obj["data"][0]
                print(f"{a['instId']} ts={d.get('ts')} last={d.get('lastPr') or d.get('last')}")
        print("msgs:", n)
asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, json, time
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

con=sqlite3.connect(DB)
cur=con.cursor()

cur.execute("""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tops(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  name TEXT, symbol TEXT, vol REAL, vola REAL,
  turnover REAL, spread REAL, ts INTEGER
);
""")

# Simule la récupération des coins avec indicateurs (vol24h, turnover, volatilité)
symbols = [
    ("BTCUSDT", 1.0, 0.9, 1.0, 0.01),
    ("ETHUSDT", 0.8, 0.7, 0.8, 0.015),
    ("BNBUSDT", 0.7, 0.6, 0.7, 0.02),
    ("SOLUSDT", 0.6, 0.5, 0.6, 0.025),
    ("XRPUSDT", 0.5, 0.4, 0.5, 0.03)
]
# Ajoute 30 symboles factices pour simuler le tri
for i in range(30):
    symbols.append((f"ALT{i}USDT", 0.1+i*0.02, 0.1+i*0.015, 0.2+i*0.01, 0.05))

# Sélection par volatilité × volume
symbols.sort(key=lambda x: x[1]*x[2]*x[3]/x[4], reverse=True)
top35 = symbols[:35]
ts = int(time.time())

for sym in top35:
    cur.execute("INSERT INTO tops(name,symbol,vol,vola,turnover,spread,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                ("TOP35", sym[0], sym[1], sym[2], sym[3], sym[4], ts))
con.commit()
print(f"[TOP35] Enregistrés {len(top35)} paires à {ts}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
FIX=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]

con=sqlite3.connect(DB); c=con.cursor()
ts=c.execute("SELECT MAX(ts) FROM tops").fetchone()[0]
if ts is None:
    print("tops vide"); exit(0)

rows=c.execute("""
SELECT symbol, (vol*vola*turnover)/(CASE WHEN spread=0 THEN 1e-9 ELSE spread END) AS score
FROM tops WHERE ts=? ORDER BY score DESC
""",(ts,)).fetchall()

seen=set(); sel=[]
for sym,sc in rows:
    s = sym if sym.endswith("USDT") else sym+"USDT"
    if s not in seen:
        sel.append((s, float(sc))); seen.add(s)
for f in FIX:
    if f not in seen:
        sel.append((f, 0.0)); seen.add(f)
sel=sel[:30]

now=int(time.time())
c.executemany("INSERT INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES('TOP30',?,?,?)",
              [(s,sc,now) for s,sc in sel])
con.commit(); con.close()
print(f"TOP30 écrit: {len(sel)}")

m = ex.load_markets()
rows=[]
for s,x in m.items():
    if x.get('swap') and x.get('quote')=='USDT':

        try: rows.append((s.replace(':USDT','').replace('/','').upper(), float(v or 0)))
        except: pass
rows.sort(key=lambda t:t[1], reverse=True)
for sym,vol in rows[:150]:
    print(f"{sym}|{vol:.0f}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, sqlite3, ccxt

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
FIX = ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]

def instid(s):  # "BTC/USDT:USDT" -> "BTCUSDT"
    return s.replace(":USDT","").replace("/","").upper()

def has_90d_history(ex, sym):
    """
    Test léger: demande des bougies 1D autour de J-90.
    Critère: on a au moins une bougie ≤ (now-88j).
    """
    now_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
    since = now_ms - 95*24*3600*1000
    try:
        rows = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe='1d', since=since, limit=10)
    except Exception:
        return False
    if not rows:
        return False
    # une bougie assez ancienne?
    threshold = now_ms - 88*24*3600*1000
    return any(r[0] <= threshold for r in rows)

def quote_volume(ex, sym):
    """
    Récupère le volume quote du ticker si dispo.
    Fallback sur baseVolume sinon.
    """
    try:
        t = ex.fetch_ticker(sym)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0
    for k in ("quoteVolume","quoteVolume24h","info"):
        if k in t and t[k]:
            if k=="info":
                # Bitget renvoie souvent 'baseVolume' ou 'quoteVolume' dans info
                v = t["info"].get("quoteVolume") or t["info"].get("baseVolume")
            else:
                v = t[k]
            try:
                return float(v)
            except Exception:
                pass
    # fallback très faible
    try:
        return float(t.get("baseVolume") or 0.0)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def main():
    ex = ccxt.bitget({'options': {'defaultType':'swap'}, 'enableRateLimit': True})
    markets = ex.load_markets()

    # 1) candidats USDT-SWAP
    cands = [s for s,m in markets.items() if m.get('swap') and m.get('quote')=='USDT']

    # 2) filtre 90j
    keep = []
    for s in cands:
        if has_90d_history(ex, s):
            keep.append(s)
        # throttle léger
        time.sleep(0.03)

    # 3) scoring volume
    scored = []
    for s in keep:
        volq = quote_volume(ex, s)
        scored.append((instid(s), volq))
        time.sleep(0.03)

    # tri décroissant volume
    scored.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)

    # 4) top30 réel + 5 fixes garantis
    seen=set()
    sel=[]
    for sym,sc in scored:
        if sym not in seen:
            sel.append((sym, float(sc)))
            seen.add(sym)
        if len(sel) >= 25:
            break
    for f in FIX:
        if f not in seen:
            sel.append((f, 0.0))
            seen.add(f)
    sel = sel[:30]

    # 5) enregistrement dans top_scores
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB); c = con.cursor()
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      name TEXT, symbol TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER
    )""")
    now = int(time.time())
    c.executemany("INSERT INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES('TOP30',?,?,?)",
                  [(s,sc,now) for s,sc in sel])
    con.commit(); con.close()

    print(f"[TOP30 REAL] kept={len(keep)} sel={len(sel)} @ {now}")
    for s,sc in sel[:10]:
        print(s, sc)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, requests, sys, json

BASE="https://api.bitget.com"
sym = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv)>1 else "BTCUSDT"
now=int(time.time())
sixm=int(30.44*6*24*3600)
slack=3*24*3600
lo,hi = (now-sixm-slack)*1000, (now-sixm+slack)*1000  # ms

tests = [
  ("v2 mix candles (symbol+suffix)", f"/api/v2/mix/market/candles", {"symbol":f"{sym}_UMCBL","granularity":86400,"limit":200}),
  ("v2 mix candles (productType+symbol)", f"/api/v2/mix/market/candles", {"productType":"USDT-FUTURES","symbol":sym,"granularity":86400,"limit":200}),
  ("v1 mix candles", f"/api/mix/v1/market/candles", {"symbol":f"{sym}_UMCBL","granularity":"1day","limit":200}),
  ("v1 mix history-candles (windowed)", f"/api/mix/v1/market/history-candles", {"symbol":f"{sym}_UMCBL","period":"1day","startTime":lo,"endTime":hi,"limit":200}),
]

def has_in_window(data):
    try:
        ts=[int(int(k[0])//1000) for k in data]
        target_low=(lo//1000); target_high=(hi//1000)
        return any(target_low<=t<=target_high for t in ts), len(ts)
    except: return False,0

sess=requests.Session()
for name,path,params in tests:
    ok=False; n=0; status=None; code=None; msg=None
    try:
        r=sess.get(BASE+path, params=params, timeout=8)
        status=r.status_code
        j=r.json() if r.headers.get("content-type","").startswith("application/json") else {}
        code=j.get("code"); msg=j.get("msg")
        data=j.get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else []
        ok,n = has_in_window(data)
    except Exception as e:
        msg=str(e)
    print(json.dumps({
        "test":name,"status":status,"code":code,"count":n,"ok_in_window":ok,"first_item":str(data[0])[:80] if n else None
    }, ensure_ascii=False))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
NOW=int(time.time())

con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
c=con.cursor()
c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")

c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_refined(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
)""")

# symboles avec contexte non nul
syms=[r[0] for r in c.execute("SELECT symbol FROM contexts_A WHERE ctx IS NOT NULL AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM contexts_A);").fetchall()]

inserted=0
for s in syms:
  rows=c.execute("SELECT ts,close FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 30;", (s,)).fetchall()
  if len(rows)<20: continue
  rows=rows[::-1]
  closes=[x[1] for x in rows]
  last=closes[-1]
  sma30=sum(closes)/len(closes)
  side= "buy" if last>sma30 else "sell"
  c.execute("""INSERT INTO signals_B_refined(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts)
               VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)""",(s,side,float(last),"A:sma30",NOW))
  inserted+=1

print(f"[AnalyseB] refined={inserted} ts={NOW}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, sqlite3, ccxt
from pathlib import Path

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
TF={"5m":"ohlcv_5m","15m":"ohlcv_15m","30m":"ohlcv_30m"}

DDL = """
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {t}(
  symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
  open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL
);
"""

def ensure(con):
    for tbl in TF.values():
        con.execute(DDL.format(t=tbl))

def main():
    bases = []
    p = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/top90_active.json")
    if p.exists(): bases = json.loads(p.read_text())
    if not bases: return
    ex = ccxt.bitget({'options': {'defaultType':'swap'}, 'enableRateLimit': True})
    ex.load_markets()
    mkt = {m['base']: s for s,m in ex.markets.items() if m.get('swap') and m.get('quote')=='USDT'}
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=10)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    ensure(con)
    for base in bases:
        sym = mkt.get(base)
        if not sym: continue
        for tf, table in TF.items():
            try:
                rows = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe=tf, limit=200)
                con.executemany(
                    f"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table}(symbol,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                    [(base, int(t[0]/1000), t[1], t[2], t[3], t[4], t[5]) for t in rows]
                )
                con.commit()
            except Exception:
                pass
    con.close()
    print("OHLCV fetched")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import json,time,sqlite3,asyncio,websockets
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
SUB={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"mc","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"}]}

async def main():
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, close_timeout=2) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(SUB))
        t0=time.time()
        while time.time()-t0<12:    # attend jusqu'à 12s
            msg=json.loads(await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=6))
            if "data" in msg:
                d=msg["data"][0]
                ts=int(d.get("systemTime", time.time()*1000))//1000
                row=("BTCUSDT", ts, float(d["last"]), float(d["bestBid"]), float(d["bestAsk"]))
                con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
                con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
                con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
                con.execute("INSERT INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?)", row)
                print("WROTE", *row); return
        print("TIMEOUT")
asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, sqlite3, time, websockets

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"
SUB={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"channel":"ticker","instType":"mc","instId":"BTCUSDT"}]}

def db():
    c=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
    )""")
    c.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sig_cts ON signals_B(created_ts)")
    return c

def price(it):
    for k in ("last","lastPr","price","close"):
        v=it.get(k)
        if v is None: continue
        try: return float(v)
        except: pass
    return None

async def run():
    con=db()
    last_emit_sec = -1
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20, close_timeout=5) as ws:
                await ws.send(json.dumps(SUB))
                print("MODE=OLD")
                while True:
                    raw=await ws.recv()
                    if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)): raw=raw.decode(errors="ignore")
                    try: msg=json.loads(raw)
                    except: continue
                    data=msg.get("data") or []
                    now=int(time.time())
                    for it in data:
                        p=price(it)
                        if not p: continue
                        # déduplication: max 1 tick inséré par seconde
                        if now==last_emit_sec: continue
                        con.execute("INSERT INTO signals_B(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)",
                                    ("BTCUSDT","buy",p,"mc_ticker",now))
                        last_emit_sec = now
        except Exception as e:
            print("WS FAIL", type(e).__name__, e)
            await asyncio.sleep(2)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Paper trader minimal :
- consomme /opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db
- lit orders_sim (id, signal_id, symbol, side, qty, price, ts, created_ts)
- tient positions_open (netting par symbole) et trades_closed
- met à jour account_sim (balance, equity, used_margin, updated_ts)
"""

import sqlite3, time, math, pathlib, os

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
LOOP_SEC = 2

SCHEMA = """
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS account_sim(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK(id=1),
  balance REAL NOT NULL,
  equity  REAL NOT NULL,
  used_margin REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  updated_ts INTEGER NOT NULL
);

INSERT OR IGNORE INTO account_sim(id,balance,equity,used_margin,updated_ts)
VALUES(1,100.0,100.0,0,CAST(strftime('%s','now') AS INTEGER));

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS positions_open(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  qty    REAL NOT NULL,             -- qty signée (>0 long, <0 short)
  entry_price REAL NOT NULL,
  last   REAL NOT NULL,
  u_pnl  REAL NOT NULL,
  opened_ts INTEGER NOT NULL
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_pos_symbol ON positions_open(symbol);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS trades_closed(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  qty    REAL NOT NULL,
  entry_price REAL NOT NULL,
  exit_price  REAL NOT NULL,
  pnl   REAL NOT NULL,
  opened_ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
  closed_ts INTEGER NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS paper_state(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK(id=1),
  last_ord_id INTEGER NOT NULL
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO paper_state(id,last_ord_id) VALUES(1,0);
"""

def qrow(cur, q, args=()):
    cur.execute(q, args); r=cur.fetchone(); return r

def qval(cur, q, args=(), default=None):
    r=qrow(cur,q,args); return r[0] if r and r[0] is not None else default

def mark_last_id(cur, last_id):
    cur.execute("UPDATE paper_state SET last_ord_id=? WHERE id=1", (last_id,))

def load_last_id(cur):
    return qval(cur,"SELECT last_ord_id FROM paper_state WHERE id=1",(),0)

def up_equity(cur):
    bal = qval(cur,"SELECT balance FROM account_sim WHERE id=1",(),0.0)
    upnl = qval(cur,"SELECT COALESCE(SUM(u_pnl),0) FROM positions_open",(),0.0)
    now = int(time.time())
    cur.execute("UPDATE account_sim SET equity=?, updated_ts=? WHERE id=1",
                (bal+upnl, now))

def realize(cur, sym, qty_to_close, price, now):
    """Ferme contre la position existante (FIFO simple)."""
    # Une seule ligne par symbole (netting), donc qty_signée suffit
    row = qrow(cur, "SELECT id, qty, entry_price, opened_ts FROM positions_open WHERE symbol=?", (sym,))
    if not row: return 0.0
    pid, pos_qty, entry, opened_ts = row
    # sens inverse pour fermer
    remain = pos_qty + qty_to_close  # qty_to_close est signée (opposée)
    # PnL réalisé sur la portion fermée = (prix_sortie - prix_entree) * qty_signée_initiale_fermée
    closed_qty = -qty_to_close if pos_qty*qty_to_close < 0 else 0.0
    if closed_qty == 0.0:  # rien à fermer
        return 0.0
    pnl = (price - entry) * (closed_qty if pos_qty>0 else -closed_qty)
    # balance++
    bal = qval(cur,"SELECT balance FROM account_sim WHERE id=1",(),0.0)
    cur.execute("UPDATE account_sim SET balance=? WHERE id=1", (bal+pnl,))
    # trade
    cur.execute("""INSERT INTO trades_closed(symbol,qty,entry_price,exit_price,pnl,opened_ts,closed_ts)
                   VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)""",
                (sym, closed_qty if pos_qty>0 else -closed_qty, entry, price, pnl, opened_ts, now))
    # position restante (si 0 => on efface)
    if abs(remain) < 1e-12:
        cur.execute("DELETE FROM positions_open WHERE id=?", (pid,))
    else:
        # Si on a inversé, on ouvre à ce nouveau prix
        if pos_qty*remain < 0:
            cur.execute("""UPDATE positions_open
                           SET qty=?, entry_price=?, last=?, u_pnl=0, opened_ts=?
                           WHERE id=?""",
                        (remain, price, price, now, pid))
        else:
            cur.execute("""UPDATE positions_open
                           SET qty=?, last=?, u_pnl=(? - entry_price)*CASE WHEN qty>0 THEN qty ELSE -qty END
                           WHERE id=?""",
                        (remain, price, price, pid))
    return pnl

def apply_order(cur, sym, side, qty, price, ts):
    if qty is None: qty = 0.0
    if qty == 0.0:  # rien à faire
        return
    now = int(time.time())
    signed = qty if side=="buy" else -qty
    # existe ?
    row = qrow(cur,"SELECT id, qty, entry_price FROM positions_open WHERE symbol=?", (sym,))
    if not row:
        # ouverture directe si même sens, sinon c'est un short/long selon signed
        cur.execute("""INSERT INTO positions_open(symbol,qty,entry_price,last,u_pnl,opened_ts)
                       VALUES(?,?,?,?,0,?)""",
                    (sym, signed, price, price, now))
        return
    # position existe : fermer partiellement si sens inverse
    pid, pos_qty, entry = row
    if pos_qty * signed < 0:
        # on ferme jusqu'à min(|pos|, |signed|)
        close_part = -math.copysign(min(abs(pos_qty),abs(signed)), signed)  # opposé à la position
        realize(cur, sym, close_part, price, now)
        signed_after = pos_qty + signed
        # si il reste du sens de l'ordre -> se retrouve dans apply suivant
        row2 = qrow(cur,"SELECT id, qty, entry_price FROM positions_open WHERE symbol=?", (sym,))
        if row2:
            pid2, qty2, entry2 = row2
            cur.execute("""UPDATE positions_open
                           SET last=?, u_pnl=(? - entry_price)*CASE WHEN qty>0 THEN qty ELSE -qty END
                           WHERE id=?""",
                        (price, price, pid2))
        else:
            if abs(signed_after) > 1e-12:
                cur.execute("""INSERT INTO positions_open(symbol,qty,entry_price,last,u_pnl,opened_ts)
                               VALUES(?,?,?,?,0,?)""",
                            (sym, signed_after, price, price, now))
    else:
        # même sens : on moyenne le prix d'entrée
        new_qty = pos_qty + signed
        if abs(new_qty) < 1e-12:
            # s'annule exactement -> trade clos
            realize(cur, sym, -signed, price, now)
        else:
            new_entry = (pos_qty*entry + signed*price)/new_qty
            cur.execute("""UPDATE positions_open
                           SET qty=?, entry_price=?, last=?, u_pnl=(? - ?)*CASE WHEN ?>0 THEN ? ELSE -? END
                           WHERE id=?""",
                        (new_qty, new_entry, price, price, new_entry, new_qty, new_qty, new_qty, pid))

def main():
    pathlib.Path("/opt/scalp/project/scripts").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    with sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5) as con:
        con.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys=ON;")
        con.executescript(SCHEMA)
        con.commit()

        while True:
            cur = con.cursor()
            last_id = load_last_id(cur)
            rows = cur.execute(
                "SELECT id, symbol, side, COALESCE(qty,0.0), price, ts FROM orders_sim WHERE id>? ORDER BY id ASC",
                (last_id,)
            ).fetchall()

            for (oid, sym, side, qty, price, ts) in rows:
                try:
                    apply_order(cur, sym, side, float(qty), float(price), int(ts or time.time()))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                mark_last_id(cur, oid)

            # recalcul u_pnl avec dernier prix connu en base (ici: last dans positions_open)
            cur.execute("""UPDATE positions_open
                           SET u_pnl=(last - entry_price)*CASE WHEN qty>0 THEN qty ELSE -qty END""")
            up_equity(cur)
            con.commit()

            # petit résumé console (optionnel)
            acc = qrow(cur,"SELECT balance, equity, updated_ts FROM account_sim WHERE id=1")
            if acc:
                bal, eq, uts = acc
                print(f"updated {time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}  balance={bal:.2f}  equity={eq:.2f}")

            time.sleep(LOOP_SEC)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, sqlite3, math
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
CFG="/opt/scalp/project/config.env"
def load_env():
    if os.path.exists(CFG):
        for line in open(CFG):
            s=line.strip()
            if not s or s.startswith("#") or "=" not in s: continue
            k,v=s.split("=",1)
            os.environ[k]=v.split("#",1)[0].strip()
load_env()
def envf(k,d):
    try: return float(os.environ.get(k,str(d)))
    except: return float(d)
TP_PCT=envf("TP_PCT",0.002)
SL_PCT=envf("SL_PCT",0.002)
def q(c,s,p=()): return c.execute(s,p)
def lev(c):
    r=q(c,"SELECT COALESCE(leverage,50) FROM account_sim LIMIT 1").fetchone()
    return float(r[0]) if r else 50.0
def last_price(c):
    r=q(c,"SELECT price FROM signals_B ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1").fetchone()
    return float(r[0]) if r else None
def pnl(entry,last,qty): return round((last-entry)*qty,6)
def main():
    con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    q(con,"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); q(con,"PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    while True:
        L=lev(con)
        pos=q(con,"SELECT id,symbol,qty,entry_price,opened_ts FROM positions_open").fetchall()
        if not pos: time.sleep(0.3); continue
        now=math.trunc(time.time())
        lp=last_price(con)
        if not lp: time.sleep(0.3); continue
        for pid,sym,qty,entry,opened_ts in pos:
            up=pnl(entry,lp,qty); q(con,"UPDATE positions_open SET last=?, u_pnl=? WHERE id=?",(lp,up,pid))
            move=(lp-entry)/entry
            if move>=TP_PCT or move<=-SL_PCT:
                realized=pnl(entry,lp,qty)
                q(con,"INSERT INTO trades_closed(symbol,side,qty,entry_price,exit_price,pnl,opened_ts,closed_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,strftime('%s','now'))",
                  (sym,"buy",qty,entry,lp,realized,opened_ts))
                q(con,"DELETE FROM positions_open WHERE id=?",(pid,))
                eq=q(con,"SELECT equity FROM account_sim LIMIT 1").fetchone()
                eq=float(eq[0]) if eq else 300.0
                q(con,"UPDATE account_sim SET equity=?, used_margin=(SELECT COALESCE(SUM(qty*entry_price/?),0) FROM positions_open), updated=strftime('%s','now')",
                  (round(eq+realized,6), L))
        time.sleep(0.3)
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, sqlite3, time
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
BATCH=5
RUN_SECS=25

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except Exception:
        try: return b.decode()
        except Exception: return ""

def load_syms():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    rows=con.execute("SELECT symbol FROM u_syms_futures").fetchall()
    con.close()
    return [r[0] for r in rows]

async def subscribe_chunk(ws, chunk):
    args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in chunk]
    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))
    await asyncio.sleep(0.2)

async def main():
    syms=load_syms()
    if not syms:
        print("⚠️  u_syms_futures vide"); return
    print(f"USDT-FUTURES top={len(syms)}:", syms)

    counts={s:0 for s in syms}
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        for i in range(0,len(syms),BATCH):
            await subscribe_chunk(ws, syms[i:i+BATCH])

        start=time.time()
        while time.time()-start < RUN_SECS:
            try:
                raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=3)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"}))
                continue
            msg=ungzip(raw)
            try: obj=json.loads(msg)
            except Exception: continue
            if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
                inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
                if inst in counts: counts[inst]+=1

    total=sum(counts.values())
    got=[(k,v) for k,v in counts.items() if v>0]
    miss=[k for k,v in counts.items() if v==0]
    print("\n=== RÉSUMÉ ===")
    print("messages_total =", total)
    print("symbols_ok     =", len(got))
    for k,v in sorted(got,key=lambda x:-x[1])[:10]:
        print(f"{k}: {v} msgs")
    if miss:
        print("aucun flux pour:", ", ".join(miss))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, time, sys, sqlite3, os, websockets

URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
BDB=os.getenv("BDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db")
SYMS=sys.argv[1].split(",") if len(sys.argv)>1 else ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]

def ensure_db():
    con=sqlite3.connect(BDB, timeout=8, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
        symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, best_bid REAL, best_ask REAL,
        PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))""")
    con.close()

def write_rows(rows):
    if not rows: return
    con=sqlite3.connect(BDB, timeout=8, isolation_level=None)
    con.executemany("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.close()

async def run():
    ensure_db()
    sub={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in SYMS]}
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20, close_timeout=5, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
        want=set(SYMS)
        while True:
            raw=await ws.recv()
            if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)): raw=raw.decode(errors="ignore")
            try: msg=json.loads(raw)
            except: continue
            if "event" in msg:  # acks/errors
                print("EVT", msg); continue
            if "data" not in msg: continue
            rows=[]
            ts=int(time.time())
            for d in msg["data"]:
                inst=d.get("instId") or d.get("symbol")
                if not inst or inst not in want: continue
                # v2 keys
                last = d.get("lastPr") or d.get("last") or d.get("lastPrice")
                bid  = d.get("bidPr")  or d.get("bestBid")
                ask  = d.get("askPr")  or d.get("bestAsk")
                try:
                    p=float(last); b=float(bid or last); a=float(ask or last)
                    t=int((int(d.get("ts") or 0))//1000) or ts
                except: 
                    continue
                rows.append((inst,t,p,b,a))
            write_rows(rows)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json,time,sqlite3,ccxt
from pathlib import Path
DB="data/scalp.db"; bases=json.loads(Path("data/top90_active.json").read_text())
ex=ccxt.bitget({'options': {'defaultType':'swap'}, 'enableRateLimit': True}); ex.load_markets()
mkt={m['base']:s for s,m in ex.markets.items() if m.get('swap') and m.get('quote')=='USDT'}
rows=[]
def spread_bps(sym):
    try:
        ob=ex.fetch_order_book(sym,limit=5)
        bid=ob['bids'][0][0]; ask=ob['asks'][0][0]; mid=(bid+ask)/2
        return (ask-bid)/mid*10000.0
    except Exception: return 100.0
for b in bases[:120]:
    sym=mkt.get(b); 
    if not sym: continue
    try:
        h=ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym,'1h',limit=24)
        vol=sum(c*v for _,_,_,_,c,v in h[-24:]) if h else 0
        sp=spread_bps(sym)
        score=max(0, vol/1e7) - min(1.0, sp/100.0)
        rows.append((b,score,None,sp,vol,None,None,"ok",int(time.time())))
    except Exception:
        rows.append((b,None,None,None,None,None,None,"error",int(time.time())))
con=sqlite3.connect(DB)
with con:
    con.execute("DELETE FROM top_scores")
    con.executemany("""INSERT INTO top_scores(symbol,score,rank,spread_bps,vol24,turn7,vola7,status,updated_ts)
                       VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)""",rows)
print("scores:",len(rows))

import asyncio, json, sqlite3, time, websockets, sys
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
SYMS=sys.argv[1:] or ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]

def con():

    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
        symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, best_bid REAL, best_ask REAL, volume REAL,
        PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))""")
    c.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_ts ON ticks(ts)")
    return c

async def run():

            async with websockets.connect(uri, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20) as ws:

                while True:

                    bb=float(d.get("bestBid") or 0.0); ba=float(d.get("bestAsk") or 0.0)
                    vol=float(d.get("tradeTurnover","0") or 0.0)

                    db.execute("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask,volume) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                               (sym, now, pr, bb, ba, vol))
        except Exception:
            await asyncio.sleep(1)  # retry loop
asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, sqlite3, time, websockets
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"; URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"

def db():
    c=sqlite3.connect(DB,timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER)""")
    c.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sig_cts ON signals_B(created_ts)")
    return c

def top_symbols(con):
    r=con.execute("""SELECT symbol FROM top_scores
      WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30')
      ORDER BY score DESC, symbol ASC LIMIT 30""").fetchall()
    syms=[x[0] for x in r]
    for f in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"):
        if f not in syms: syms.append(f)
    return syms[:30]

def price_of(it):
    for k in ("last","lastPr","price","close"):
        v=it.get(k)
        if v is None: continue
        try: return float(v)
        except: pass
    return None

async def worker(sym, con):
    sub={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"channel":"ticker","instType":"mc","instId":sym}]}
    backoff=1
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20, close_timeout=5) as ws:
                await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
                print("SUB", sym, flush=True)
                last=-1
                while True:
                    raw=await ws.recv()
                    if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)): raw=raw.decode(errors="ignore")
                    try: msg=json.loads(raw)
                    except: continue
                    data=msg.get("data") or []
                    now=int(time.time())
                    for it in data:
                        p=price_of(it)
                        if not p: continue
                        if last==now: continue
                        con.execute("INSERT INTO signals_B(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)",
                                    (sym,"buy",p,"ctx_ws",now))
                        last=now
            backoff=1
        except Exception as e:
            print("WS FAIL", sym, type(e).__name__, flush=True)
            await asyncio.sleep(backoff); backoff=min(30, backoff*2)

async def main():
    con=db()
    tasks=[asyncio.create_task(worker(s, con)) for s in top_symbols(con)]
    await asyncio.gather(*tasks)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, sqlite3, time, sys, os
os.environ["PYTHONUNBUFFERED"]="1"
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"; URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
BATCH=5; RUN_SECS=20; ACK_TIMEOUT=5

def log(*a): print(*a, flush=True)
def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except: 
        try: return b.decode()
        except: return ""

def load_syms():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    cur=con.cursor()
    has_fut=cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='u_syms_futures'").fetchone()
    u=cur.execute("SELECT symbol FROM u_syms").fetchall()
    uf=cur.execute("SELECT symbol FROM u_syms_futures").fetchall() if has_fut else []
    con.close()
    u=[r[0] for r in u if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT")]
    uf=[r[0] for r in uf if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT")]
    src="u_syms_futures" if uf else "u_syms"
    syms=uf if uf else u
    return src, syms[:35]

async def subscribe_chunk(ws, chunk):
    args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in chunk]
    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))
    acks=set(); t0=time.time()
    while time.time()-t0<ACK_TIMEOUT and len(acks)<len(chunk):
        try: raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=ACK_TIMEOUT)
        except asyncio.TimeoutError: break
        msg=ungzip(raw)
        try: obj=json.loads(msg)
        except: continue
        if obj.get("event")=="subscribe":
            inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId"); 
            if inst in chunk: acks.add(inst); log("ACK", inst)
        elif obj.get("event")=="error":
            log("ERR", obj)
        elif obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
            # premier snapshot reçu pendant ACK
            inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
            if inst in chunk: acks.add(inst)
    missing=[s for s in chunk if s not in acks]
    if missing: log("ACK missing:", missing)

async def main():
    src, syms = load_syms()
    log(f"source={src} count={len(syms)}")
    log("syms:", syms)
    if not syms: 
        log("LISTE VIDE → rien à souscrire"); return
    counts={s:0 for s in syms}
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        for i in range(0,len(syms),BATCH):
            chunk=syms[i:i+BATCH]
            log("SUB", chunk)
            await subscribe_chunk(ws, chunk)
            await asyncio.sleep(0.2)
        t0=time.time()
        while time.time()-t0<RUN_SECS:
            try: raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=3)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"})); continue
            msg=ungzip(raw)
            try: obj=json.loads(msg)
            except: continue
            if obj.get("event")=="error": log("ERR", obj); continue
            if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
                inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
                if inst in counts: counts[inst]+=1
        total=sum(counts.values()); ok=[(k,v) for k,v in counts.items() if v>0]
        ok.sort(key=lambda x:-x[1]); miss=[k for k,v in counts.items() if v==0]
        log("\n=== RESUME ==="); log("msgs_total", total, "syms_ok", len(ok))
        for k,v in ok[:10]: log(f"{k}: {v} msgs")
        if miss: log("aucun flux:", ", ".join(miss))
if __name__=="__main__": asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, time, json, websockets
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"
CANDS=[
  {"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"},
  {"instType":"MC","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"},
  {"instType":"UMCBL","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"} # legacy
]
async def main():
  async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20, close_timeout=5, max_size=2**20) as ws:
    await asyncio.sleep(1)
    for a in CANDS: await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":[a]}))
    start=time.time()
    while time.time()-start<20:
      msg=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=20)
      if isinstance(msg,(bytes,bytearray)): msg=msg.decode("utf-8","ignore")
      try: d=json.loads(msg)
      except: continue
      if d.get("event") in ("subscribe","subscribed") or d.get("code")==0:
        print("ACK:", d)
      if "data" in d and "arg" in d:
        print("DATA_OK:", d["arg"]); return
    print("FAIL: no data"); raise SystemExit(1)
asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

SQL_FETCH = """
SELECT id, symbol, side, COALESCE(price,0.0) AS price, created_ts
FROM signals_B
WHERE id > ?
ORDER BY id ASC
LIMIT 100;
"""

SQL_INSERT_ORD = """
INSERT INTO orders_sim(signal_id, symbol, side, qty, price, ts)
VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,strftime('%s','now'));
"""

def route_once(con, last_id):
    cur = con.cursor()
    rows = cur.execute(SQL_FETCH, (last_id,)).fetchall()
    n = 0
    for sid, sym, side, price, _ in rows:
        cur.execute(SQL_INSERT_ORD, (sid, sym, side, 0.0, float(price or 0.0)))
        last_id = sid
        n += 1
    con.commit()
    return n, last_id

def main():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    con.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys=ON;")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS orders_sim(
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        signal_id INTEGER REFERENCES signals_B(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        symbol TEXT NOT NULL, side TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(side IN ('buy','sell')),
        qty REAL DEFAULT 0, price REAL NOT NULL, ts INTEGER NOT NULL
    );""")
    last_id = 0
    print("== Router dry-run started (signals_B -> orders_sim) ==")
    total = 0
    for _ in range(10):
        n, last_id = route_once(con, last_id)
        if n == 0: break
        total += n
        time.sleep(0.2)
    print(f"routed {total} order(s)")
    con.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, sqlite3

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
CFG="/opt/scalp/project/config.env"

def load_env():
    if os.path.exists(CFG):
        for line in open(CFG):
            s=line.strip()
            if not s or s.startswith("#") or "=" not in s: continue
            k,v=s.split("=",1)
            os.environ[k]=v.split("#",1)[0].strip()
load_env()

def envf(k,d): 
    try: return float(os.environ.get(k,str(d)))
    except: return float(d)

RISK_PCT   = envf("RISK_PCT",0.005)
MAX_OPEN   = int(envf("MAX_OPEN",200))
COOLDOWN_MS= int(envf("COOLDOWN_MS",150))
MAX_MARGIN = envf("MAX_MARGIN_PCT",0.95)
DEF_LEV    = envf("LEVERAGE",50)

def q(c,s,p=()): return c.execute(s,p)
def ensure(c):
    q(c,"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); q(c,"PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    q(c,"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS router_state(k TEXT PRIMARY KEY, v INTEGER)")
    q(c,"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO router_state(k,v) VALUES('last_signal_id',0)")
    q(c,"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS positions_open(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      order_id INTEGER, symbol TEXT, side TEXT,
      qty REAL, entry_price REAL, last REAL, u_pnl REAL, opened_ts INTEGER)""")
    q(c,"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS orders_sim(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      signal_id INTEGER, symbol TEXT, side TEXT,
      qty REAL, price REAL, used_margin REAL, created_ts INTEGER, ts INTEGER)""")

def has_col(c,t,col): return any(r[1]==col for r in q(c,f"PRAGMA table_info({t})"))
def acct(c):
    r=q(c,"SELECT equity,COALESCE(leverage,?),COALESCE(used_margin,0) FROM account_sim LIMIT 1",(DEF_LEV,)).fetchone()
    return (float(r[0]),float(r[1]),float(r[2])) if r else (300.0,DEF_LEV,0.0)
def load_last(c):
    last=q(c,"SELECT v FROM router_state WHERE k='last_signal_id'").fetchone()[0]
    mx=q(c,"SELECT COALESCE(MAX(id),0) FROM signals_B").fetchone()[0] or 0
    if last==0 or last>mx: last=max(0,mx-100); q(c,"UPDATE router_state SET v=? WHERE k='last_signal_id'",(last,))
    return last
def save_last(c,v): q(c,"UPDATE router_state SET v=? WHERE k='last_signal_id'",(v,))
def open_cnt(c): return q(c,"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM positions_open").fetchone()[0] or 0
def last_ord_ms(c): return int((q(c,"SELECT COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) FROM orders_sim").fetchone()[0] or 0)*1000)

def main():
    con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None); ensure(con)
    use_ts=has_col(con,"orders_sim","ts")
    last=load_last(con)
    while True:
        eq,lev,used=acct(con)
        if used > MAX_MARGIN*eq or open_cnt(con) >= MAX_OPEN:
            time.sleep(0.2); last=load_last(con); continue
        rows=q(con,"SELECT id,symbol,price,created_ts FROM signals_B WHERE id>? ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 200",(last,)).fetchall()
        if not rows: time.sleep(0.2); continue
        for sid,sym,price,cts in rows:
            if int(time.time()*1000)-last_ord_ms(con) < COOLDOWN_MS: last=sid; continue
            if not price or price<=0: last=sid; continue
            qty  = round((eq*RISK_PCT*lev)/float(price), 6)
            if qty<=0: last=sid; continue
            used_m = round(qty*float(price)/lev, 6)
            if use_ts:
                q(con,"INSERT INTO orders_sim(signal_id,symbol,side,qty,price,used_margin,created_ts,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                  (sid,sym,"buy",qty,float(price),used_m,int(cts),int(cts)))
            else:
                q(con,"INSERT INTO orders_sim(signal_id,symbol,side,qty,price,used_margin,created_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                  (sid,sym,"buy",qty,float(price),used_m,int(cts)))
            oid=q(con,"SELECT last_insert_rowid()").fetchone()[0]
            q(con,"INSERT INTO positions_open(order_id,symbol,side,qty,entry_price,last,u_pnl,opened_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
              (oid,sym,"buy",qty,float(price),float(price),0.0,int(cts)))
            last=sid
        save_last(con,last)
        try:
            tot=q(con,"SELECT COALESCE(SUM(qty*entry_price/?),0) FROM positions_open",(lev,)).fetchone()[0] or 0.0
            q(con,"UPDATE account_sim SET used_margin=?, updated=strftime('%s','now')",(round(tot,6),))
        except sqlite3.OperationalError: pass

if __name__=="__main__": main()
