#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
TF=({"name":"5m","secs":300},{"name":"15m","secs":900},{"name":"30m","secs":1800})
VIEW=lambda tf: f"v_indic_{tf}"
TBL =lambda tf: f"indic_{tf}"
WARMUP_BARS=100  # recalcule 100 barres avant le max ts connu (pour SMA/RSI/MACD)

con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
cur=con.cursor()
cur.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); cur.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")

# symbols à maintenir (TOP30 courant)
syms=[r[0] for r in cur.execute("""
SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM top_scores
WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30')
LIMIT 30
""")]

for tf in TF:
    tfname=tf["name"]; secs=tf["secs"]
    view=VIEW(tfname); tbl=TBL(tfname)

    # sécurités
    cur.execute(f"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {tbl}(
      symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
      close REAL, sma20 REAL, sma50 REAL,
      macd REAL, macd_sig REAL, macd_hist REAL,
      rsi14 REAL, atr14 REAL, atr_pct REAL, obv REAL,
      PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts)
    )""")
    cur.execute(f"CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_{tbl}_sym_ts ON {tbl}(symbol,ts)")

    for s in syms:
        row=cur.execute(f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM {tbl} WHERE symbol=?",(s,)).fetchone()
        max_ts = row[0] or 0
        cutoff = max(0, max_ts - WARMUP_BARS*secs)

        # purge la zone à reconstituer
        cur.execute(f"DELETE FROM {tbl} WHERE symbol=? AND ts>=?", (s, cutoff))

        # réinsère depuis la vue récente seulement
        cur.execute(f"""
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {tbl}(symbol,ts,close,sma20,sma50,macd,macd_sig,macd_hist,rsi14,atr14,atr_pct,obv)
        SELECT symbol,ts,close,sma20,sma50,macd,macd_sig,macd_hist,rsi14,atr14,atr_pct,obv
        FROM {view}
        WHERE symbol=? AND ts>=?;
        """, (s, cutoff))

    n = cur.execute(f"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {tbl}").fetchone()[0]
    print(f"[INC] {tfname} rows={n}")

con.close()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, math, os

ADB=os.getenv("ADB","/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
UDB=os.getenv("UDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db")

TF=("5m","15m","30m")
W_TF={"5m":0.20,"15m":0.30,"30m":0.50}
TAU=0.30
LIMIT_BARS=120   # faible pour vitesse

def ema(vals,n):
    if len(vals)<n: return None
    k=2/(n+1); e=vals[0]
    for v in vals[1:]: e += (v-e)*k
    return e
def macd(vals):
    if len(vals)<26: return 0.0
    e12=ema(vals[-26:],12); e26=ema(vals[-26:],26)
    return (e12-e26) if (e12 is not None and e26 is not None) else 0.0
def rsi(vals,n=14):
    if len(vals)<n+1: return 50.0
    g=l=0.0
    for i in range(-n-1,-1):
        d=vals[i+1]-vals[i]
        if d>0: g+=d
        else:   l-=d
    if l==0: return 100.0
    rs=(g/n)/(l/n)
    return 100.0-(100.0/(1.0+rs))
def atr(H,L,C,n=14):
    if len(C)<n+1: return 0.0
    s=0.0
    for i in range(-n,0):
        tr=max(H[i]-L[i], abs(H[i]-C[i-1]), abs(L[i]-C[i-1]))
        s+=tr
    return (s/n)/C[-1] if C[-1] else 0.0
def softmax3(b,h,s,tau):
    e=(math.exp(b/tau),math.exp(h/tau),math.exp(s/tau)); z=sum(e)
    return e[0]/z, e[1]/z, e[2]/z

def load_top(cur):
    syms=[]
    try:
        cur.execute(f"ATTACH DATABASE '{UDB}' AS udb")
        syms=[s for (s,) in cur.execute(
            "SELECT symbol FROM udb.top_scores WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM udb.top_scores WHERE name='TOP30') LIMIT 30")]
        cur.execute("DETACH DATABASE udb")
    except: pass
    for fix in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"):
        if fix not in syms: syms.append(fix)
    return syms

def fetch_ll(cur, tf, sym):
    # index requis: CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_%s_sym_ts ON ohlcv_%s(symbol,ts);
    return cur.execute(f"SELECT close,high,low FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT ?",
                       (sym, LIMIT_BARS)).fetchall()

def main():
    t0=time.time()
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, timeout=8, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    cur=con.cursor()
    cur.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contexts_A(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, pb REAL, ph REAL, ps REAL, ts INTEGER)""")
    cur.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ctxA_sym_ts ON contexts_A(symbol,ts)")
    # s'assure des index OHLCV
    for tf in TF:
        cur.execute(f"CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_{tf}_sym_ts ON ohlcv_{tf}(symbol,ts)")

    syms=load_top(cur)
    now=int(time.time()); rows=[]
    for sym in syms:
        buy_w=0.0; ok=False
        for tf in TF:
            rs=fetch_ll(cur, tf, sym)
            if len(rs)<30: continue
            C=[r[0] for r in rs][::-1]; H=[r[1] for r in rs][::-1]; L=[r[2] for r in rs][::-1]
            e9=ema(C,9) or 0.0; e21=ema(C,21) or 0.0
            s=0.35*(1.0 if e9>e21 else 0.0)
            s+=0.25*(1.0 if macd(C)>0.0 else 0.0)
            s+=0.20*(rsi(C)/100.0)
            s+=0.20*(min(atr(H,L,C)*10.0,1.0))
            buy_w+=W_TF[tf]*s; ok=True
        if not ok: continue
        hold=1.0-abs(buy_w-0.5)*2.0; sell=1.0-buy_w
        pb,ph,ps=softmax3(buy_w,hold,sell,TAU)
        ctx='buy' if pb>=0.60 else 'sell' if ps>=0.60 else 'hold' if ph>=0.45 else 'none'
        rows.append((sym,ctx,round(pb,3),round(ph,3),round(ps,3),now))

    if rows:
        cur.executemany("INSERT INTO contexts_A(symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,ts) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?)", rows)

    # vue latest
    cur.execute("DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_contexts_A_latest")
    cur.execute("""
      CREATE VIEW v_contexts_A_latest AS
      WITH m AS (SELECT symbol,MAX(ts) ts FROM contexts_A GROUP BY symbol)
      SELECT c.* FROM contexts_A c JOIN m ON c.symbol=m.symbol AND c.ts=m.ts
    """)

    # résumé sortie
    counts=dict(cur.execute("SELECT ctx,COUNT(*) FROM v_contexts_A_latest GROUP BY ctx").fetchall())
    total=sum(counts.values()) if counts else 0
    usable=total-counts.get('none',0)
    dur=round(time.time()-t0,2)
    print(f"[A] inserted={len(rows)} total={total} usable_for_B={usable} "
          f"buy={counts.get('buy',0)} hold={counts.get('hold',0)} sell={counts.get('sell',0)} none={counts.get('none',0)} "
          f"tf=5/15/30 lookback={LIMIT_BARS} dur_s={dur}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

import asyncio, json, os, time, sqlite3, websockets, aiohttp, random
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
SYM=os.environ.get("SYM","BTCUSDT")

URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
SUB_NEW={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":f"{SYM}_UMCBL"}]}
SUB_OLD={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"mc","channel":"ticker","instId":SYM}]}

def db_write(sym, ts, last, bid, ask):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None) as con:
        con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
        con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
        con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, best_bid REAL, best_ask REAL)""")
        con.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_sym_ts ON ticks(symbol,ts)")
        con.execute("INSERT INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?)",
                    (sym, ts, last, bid, ask))

async def ws_once(sub):
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, close_timeout=2) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
        t0=time.time()
        while time.time()-t0<25:  # 25s par branche
            msg=json.loads(await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=8))
            # OLD = {"action":"snapshot"/"update", "data":[...]}
            # NEW = {"event":"subscribe"} puis "data"
            d=None
            if "data" in msg:
                d=msg["data"][0]
            elif msg.get("action") in ("snapshot","update") and msg.get("data"):
                d=msg["data"][0]
            if not d: 
                continue
            last=float(d.get("last") or d.get("lastPr") or d.get("pr") or 0.0)
            bid=float(d.get("bestBid") or d.get("bidPx") or last)
            ask=float(d.get("bestAsk") or d.get("askPx") or last)
            ts=int((d.get("systemTime") or d.get("ts") or time.time()*1000)//1000)
            if last>0:
                db_write(SYM, ts, last, bid, ask)
                print("WROTE", SYM, ts, last, bid, ask)
                return True
        return False

async def rest_fallback():
    url=f"https://api.bitget.com/api/v2/mix/market/tickers?productType=umcbl"  # USDT-perp
    try:
        timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=8)
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession(timeout=timeout) as ses:
            async with ses.get(url) as r:
                j=await r.json()
        for it in j.get("data",[]):
            if it.get("symbol")==f"{SYM}_UMCBL":
                last=float(it.get("lastPr") or 0)
                bid=float(it.get("bestBid") or last)
                ask=float(it.get("bestAsk") or last)
                ts=int(time.time())
                if last>0:
                    db_write(SYM, ts, last, bid, ask)
                    print("REST_WROTE", SYM, ts, last, bid, ask)
                    return True
    except Exception as e:
        print("REST_FAIL", e)
    return False

async def main():
    # 3 tentatives avec backoff
    for attempt in range(3):
        # course NEW + OLD, on garde le premier qui écrit
        done, pending = await asyncio.wait(
            [asyncio.create_task(ws_once(SUB_NEW)), asyncio.create_task(ws_once(SUB_OLD))],
            return_when=asyncio.FIRST_COMPLETED)
        ok = any(t.result() for t in done if not t.cancelled())
        for p in pending: p.cancel()
        if ok:
            return
        # fallback REST
        if await rest_fallback():
            return
        await asyncio.sleep(1.5*(attempt+1)+random.random())
    print("TIMEOUT_ALL")
asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, sqlite3, time, websockets

DB  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"

def db():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
    )""")
    c.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sig_cts ON signals_B(created_ts)")
    return c

def top_symbols(con):
    rows = con.execute("""
      SELECT symbol FROM top_scores
      WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30')
      ORDER BY score DESC LIMIT 20
    """).fetchall()
    syms = [r[0] for r in rows]
    for f in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"):
        if f not in syms: syms.append(f)
    return syms[:20]

def price_of(item):
    for k in ("last","lastPr","price","close"):
        v = item.get(k)
        if v is None: continue
        try: return float(v)
        except: pass
    return None

async def sub_batch(ws, syms):
    args = [{"channel":"ticker","instType":"mc","instId":s} for s in syms]
    sub = {"op":"subscribe","args":args}
    await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
    print("SUB", len(syms), flush=True)

async def run():
    con = db()
    symbols = top_symbols(con)
    # group par 2 ou 3 symboles max
    groups = [symbols[i:i+3] for i in range(0,len(symbols),3)]
    print("GROUPS", len(groups), flush=True)

    while True:
        for grp in groups:
            try:
                async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20, close_timeout=5) as ws:
                    await sub_batch(ws, grp)
                    while True:
                        raw = await ws.recv()
                        if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)): raw = raw.decode(errors="ignore")
                        try: msg = json.loads(raw)
                        except: continue
                        data = msg.get("data") or []
                        arg  = msg.get("arg") or {}
                        inst = arg.get("instId") if isinstance(arg,dict) else ""
                        now = int(time.time())
                        for it in data:
                            p = price_of(it)
                            if not p: continue
                            con.execute("INSERT INTO signals_B(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)",
                                        (inst or it.get("instId"), "buy", p, "ctx_ws", now))
            except Exception as e:
                print("WS FAIL:", type(e).__name__, e, flush=True)
                await asyncio.sleep(3)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, time, sqlite3, os, websockets
ADB=os.getenv("ADB","/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
TDB=os.getenv("TDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db")
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
REFRESH_SEC=20; PING_INT=20

def load_symbols():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, timeout=5)
    rows=con.execute("""
      WITH m AS (SELECT symbol,MAX(ts) ts FROM contexts_A GROUP BY symbol)
      SELECT c.symbol FROM contexts_A c JOIN m USING(symbol,ts) WHERE c.ctx!='none'
    """).fetchall(); con.close()
    return sorted({r[0] for r in rows})

def ensure_tdb():
    con=sqlite3.connect(TDB, timeout=8, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
      symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, best_bid REAL, best_ask REAL,
      PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))"""); con.close()

def write_rows(rows):
    if not rows: return
    con=sqlite3.connect(TDB, timeout=8, isolation_level=None)
    con.executemany("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.close()

async def send(ws, op, syms):
    if not syms: return
    args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in syms]
    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":op,"args":args})); print(op.upper(), syms, flush=True)

async def run():
    ensure_tdb(); current=set()
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=PING_INT, ping_timeout=PING_INT, close_timeout=5, max_size=2**22) as ws:
                last_refresh=0
                while True:
                    now=time.time()
                    if now-last_refresh>REFRESH_SEC:
                        want=set(load_symbols()); add=list(want-current); rem=list(current-want)
                        if rem: await send(ws,"unsubscribe",rem)
                        if add: await send(ws,"subscribe",add)
                        current=want; last_refresh=now
                    try: raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=2.5)
                    except asyncio.TimeoutError: continue
                    if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)): raw=raw.decode(errors="ignore")
                    try: msg=json.loads(raw)
                    except Exception: continue
                    if "data" not in msg: continue
                    rows=[]; ts_fb=int(time.time())
                    for d in msg["data"]:
                        s=d.get("instId") or d.get("symbol")
                        if not s or s not in current: continue
                        last=d.get("lastPr") or d.get("last") or d.get("lastPrice")
                        bid=d.get("bidPr") or d.get("bestBid") or last
                        ask=d.get("askPr") or d.get("bestAsk") or last
                        try:
                            p=float(last); b=float(bid); a=float(ask)
                            ts=int((int(d.get("ts") or 0))//1000) or ts_fb
                        except Exception: continue
                        rows.append((s,ts,p,b,a))
                    write_rows(rows)
        except Exception as e:
            print("WS_RESTART", e, flush=True); await asyncio.sleep(3)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import ccxt, json
from pathlib import Path
EXCLUDE={"USDT","USDC","FDUSD","TUSD","DAI","EUR","TRY","USD"}
EX_LEV=("UP","DOWN","BULL","BEAR","3L","3S","5L","5S")
out=Path("data/top90_active.json")
ex=ccxt.bitget({'options': {'defaultType':'swap'}, 'enableRateLimit': True})
ex.load_markets()
bases=set()
for s,m in ex.markets.items():
    if m.get('swap') and m.get('quote')=='USDT':
        b=(m.get('base') or '').upper()
        if b not in EXCLUDE and not any(t in b for t in EX_LEV):
            bases.add(b)
out.write_text(json.dumps(sorted(bases), indent=2))
print("ACTIVE:", len(bases))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, json, sqlite3, ccxt, concurrent.futures as fut

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
CACHE = "/opt/scalp/project/data/top30_cache.json"
FIX = ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]

TARGET     = int(os.getenv("TARGET", "30"))
CAND_LIMIT = int(os.getenv("CAND_LIMIT", "120"))
WORKERS    = int(os.getenv("WORKERS", "6"))
BYPASS_CACHE = os.getenv("TOP30_BYPASS_CACHE", "0") == "1"
SKIP_90D     = os.getenv("SKIP_90D", "0") == "1"

def instid(s): return s.replace(":USDT","").replace("/","").upper()

def save_top(symbols_scores):
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB); c=con.cursor()
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      name TEXT, symbol TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER)""")
    now = int(time.time())
    c.executemany("INSERT INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES('TOP30',?,?,?)",
                  [(sym, float(sc), now) for sym,sc in symbols_scores[:TARGET]])
    con.commit(); con.close()
    return now

def load_cache():
    if BYPASS_CACHE: return None
    try:
        st = os.stat(CACHE)
        if time.time() - st.st_mtime < 24*3600:
            return json.load(open(CACHE))
    except Exception: pass
    return None

def save_cache(d):
    try: json.dump(d, open(CACHE,"w"))
    except Exception: pass

def has_90d_history(ex, sym):
    if SKIP_90D: return True
    now_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
    since  = now_ms - 100*24*3600*1000
    try:
        rows = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe='1w', since=since, limit=20)
        return bool(rows) and len(rows) >= 13
    except Exception:
        return False

def quote_volume_of_ticker(ex, sym):
    try:
        t = ex.fetch_ticker(sym)
        v = t.get("quoteVolume") or (t.get("info",{}) or {}).get("quoteVolume") \
            or t.get("baseVolume") or (t.get("info",{}) or {}).get("baseVolume") or 0
        return float(v or 0)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def main():
    cache = load_cache()
    if cache:
        now = save_top(cache["top"])
        print(f"[TOP30 FAST] cache {len(cache['top'])} @ {now}"); return

    ex = ccxt.bitget({'options': {'defaultType':'swap'}, 'enableRateLimit': True})
    markets = ex.load_markets()

    vols = []
    for s,m in markets.items():
        if not m.get('swap') or m.get('quote')!='USDT': continue
        raw = (m.get('info',{}) or {}).get('baseVolume') or m.get('volume') or 0
        try: vol = float(raw or 0)
        except: vol = 0.0
        vols.append((s, vol))
    vols.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
    cands = [s for s,_ in vols[:CAND_LIMIT]]

    def check(sym):
        exi = ccxt.bitget({'options': {'defaultType':'swap'}, 'enableRateLimit': True})
        if not has_90d_history(exi, sym): return None
        vq = quote_volume_of_ticker(exi, sym)
        return (instid(sym), vq)

    results = []
    with fut.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS) as pool:
        for r in pool.map(check, cands):
            if r: results.append(r)

    results.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
    seen=set(); top=[]
    for sym,sc in results:
        if sym not in seen:
            top.append((sym, sc)); seen.add(sym)
        if len(top) >= TARGET-5: break
    for f in FIX:
        if f not in seen:
            top.append((f, 0.0)); seen.add(f)
    top = top[:TARGET]

    now = save_top(top)
    save_cache({"top": top, "ts": now})
    print(f"[TOP30 FAST] kept={len(results)} sel={len(top)} @ {now}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, requests, sqlite3

UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
BASE="https://api.bitget.com"

NOW=int(time.time())
SIXM=int(30.44*6*24*3600)
SLACK=3*24*3600
T_LOW = NOW - SIXM - SLACK
T_HIGH= NOW - SIXM + SLACK

def get_tickers_top100():
    r=requests.get(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/tickers",
                   params={"productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}, timeout=10)
    r.raise_for_status()
    data=r.json().get("data",[]) or []
    rows=[]
    for d in data:
        s=(d.get("symbol") or "").replace("_UMCBL","")
        if not s: continue
        try:
            usdt=float(d.get("usdtVolume") or d.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
            if usdt==0:
                last=float(d.get("lastPr") or 0.0)
                base=float(d.get("baseVolume") or 0.0)
                usdt=last*base
        except: usdt=0.0
        rows.append((s,usdt))
    rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)
    return rows[:100]

def daily_has_6m(sym):
    sess=requests.Session()
    # Try v2 (suffix)
    try:
        p={"symbol":f"{sym}_UMCBL","granularity":86400,"limit":200}
        j=sess.get(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/candles", params=p, timeout=8).json()
        data=j.get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else []
        if data:
            ts=[int(int(k[0])//1000) for k in data]
            return any(T_LOW<=t<=T_HIGH for t in ts)
    except: pass
    # Try v2 (productType + sans suffixe)
    try:
        p={"productType":"USDT-FUTURES","symbol":sym,"granularity":86400,"limit":200}
        j=sess.get(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/candles", params=p, timeout=8).json()
        data=j.get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else []
        if data:
            ts=[int(int(k[0])//1000) for k in data]
            return any(T_LOW<=t<=T_HIGH for t in ts)
    except: pass
    # Try v1
    try:
        p={"symbol":f"{sym}_UMCBL","granularity":"1day","limit":200}
        j=sess.get(f"{BASE}/api/mix/v1/market/candles", params=p, timeout=8).json()
        data=j.get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else []
        if data:
            ts=[int(int(k[0])//1000) for k in data]
            return any(T_LOW<=t<=T_HIGH for t in ts)
    except: pass
    return False

def cache_age_whitelist(symbols):
    con=sqlite3.connect(UDB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    cur=con.cursor()
    cur.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS age_whitelist(
      symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ok INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, first_ok_ts INTEGER)""")
    known={s:o for (s,o) in cur.execute("SELECT symbol,ok FROM age_whitelist")}
    now=int(time.time())
    for s in symbols:
        if known.get(s,0)==1: continue
        ok = 1 if daily_has_6m(s) else 0
        cur.execute("""INSERT INTO age_whitelist(symbol,ok,first_ok_ts)
                       VALUES(?,?,?)
                       ON CONFLICT(symbol) DO UPDATE SET ok=excluded.ok,
                         first_ok_ts=COALESCE(age_whitelist.first_ok_ts, excluded.first_ok_ts)""",
                    (s,ok, now if ok else None))
    con.close()

def write_top(name, pairs):
    con=sqlite3.connect(UDB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    ts=int(time.time())
    con.executemany("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?)",
                    [(name,s,float(sc),ts) for s,sc in pairs])
    con.close()
    return ts

def main():
    top100 = get_tickers_top100()
    cache_age_whitelist([s for s,_ in top100])

    con=sqlite3.connect(UDB, timeout=8)
    ok_age={s for (s,) in con.execute("SELECT symbol FROM age_whitelist WHERE ok=1")}
    con.close()

    top100_age=[(s,v) for s,v in top100 if s in ok_age]
    ts1=write_top("TOP100_VOL", top100)
    top30=top100_age[:30]
    ts2=write_top("TOP30", top30)

    # +5 fixes
    FIX=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]
    fix_to_add=[f for f in FIX if f not in [s for s,_ in top30]]
    if fix_to_add:
        write_top("TOP30", top30 + [(s,9e9) for s in fix_to_add])

    print(f"[UNIVERSE] top100={len(top100)} top100_age={len(top100_age)} top30_written={len(top30)} ts={ts2}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os,time,sqlite3,requests

BDB=os.getenv("BDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db")
UDB=os.getenv("UDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db")
FIX=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]
PERIOD=2.0
S="https://api.bitget.com"

def get_syms():
    try:
        con=sqlite3.connect(UDB,timeout=3)
        syms=[r[0] for r in con.execute(
            "SELECT symbol FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30') LIMIT 30")]
        con.close()
        if not syms: return FIX
        for f in FIX:
            if f not in syms: syms.append(f)
        return syms[:35]
    except: return FIX

def ensure_db():
    con=sqlite3.connect(BDB,timeout=8,isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
        symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, best_bid REAL, best_ask REAL,
        PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))""")
    con.close()

def write_batch(rows):
    if not rows: return
    con=sqlite3.connect(BDB,timeout=8,isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    con.executemany("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.close()

def loop():
    ensure_db()
    sess=requests.Session()
    last_ok=0
    while True:
        try:
            want=set(get_syms())
            # v2 mix tickers
            r=sess.get(f"{S}/api/v2/mix/market/tickers", params={"productType":"umcbl"}, timeout=6)
            data=r.json().get("data",[]) if r.status_code==200 else []
            m={}
            for d in data:
                sym=(d.get("symbol") or "").replace("_UMCBL","")
                if not sym or sym not in want: continue
                ts=int((int(d.get("ts") or 0))//1000) or int(time.time())
                last=float(d.get("lastPr") or 0.0)
                bid=float(d.get("bestBid") or last)
                ask=float(d.get("bestAsk") or last)
                if last>0: m[sym]=(sym,ts,last,bid,ask)
            # fallback spot tickers (rarement utile) + v1 si m vide
            if not m:
                r=sess.get(f"{S}/api/mix/v1/market/tickers", params={"productType":"umcbl"}, timeout=6)
                j=r.json()
                data=j.get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else []
                for d in data:
                    sym=(d.get("symbol") or "").replace("_UMCBL","")
                    if not sym or sym not in want: continue
                    ts=int(time.time())
                    last=float(d.get("lastPr") or 0.0)
                    bid=float(d.get("bestBid") or last)
                    ask=float(d.get("bestAsk") or last)
                    if last>0: m[sym]=(sym,ts,last,bid,ask)
            if m:
                write_batch(list(m.values()))
                last_ok=time.time()
        except Exception:
            pass
        time.sleep(PERIOD)

if __name__=="__main__":
    loop()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, ccxt
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

def load_top35():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    syms=[r[0] for r in con.execute("SELECT symbol FROM u_syms").fetchall()]
    con.close()
    return [s for s in syms if isinstance(s,str) and s.endswith("USDT")][:35]

def futures_instids(top):
    ex=ccxt.bitget({'enableRateLimit': True})
    ex.load_markets()
    out=[]
    for m in ex.markets.values():
        if m.get('swap') and m.get('quote')=='USDT':
            inst = f"{m['base']}USDT"  # format WS v2
            out.append(inst)
    avail=set(out)
    top_set=set(top)
    ok=sorted(top_set & avail)
    miss=sorted(top_set - avail)
    return ok, miss

if __name__=="__main__":
    top=load_top35()
    ok,miss=futures_instids(top)
    print("FUTURES_OK:", len(ok), ok)
    print("NO_FUTURES:", len(miss), miss)
    # persist pour les probes / writer
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    con.execute("CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS u_syms_futures(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY)")
    con.execute("DELETE FROM u_syms_futures")
    con.executemany("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO u_syms_futures(symbol) VALUES(?)", [(s,) for s in ok])
    con.close()

import asyncio, json, os, time, sqlite3, websockets

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
SYMS=os.environ.get("SYMS","BTCUSDT,ETHUSDT,BNBUSDT,SOLUSDT,XRPUSDT").split(",")

def db():
    con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=12, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, best_bid REAL, best_ask REAL)""")
    con.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_sym_ts ON ticks(symbol,ts)")
    return con

def parse_msg(msg):
    # Retourne liste [(symbol, ts, last, bid, ask)]
    out=[]
    # Format "OLD": {"action":"snapshot"/"update", "arg":{instType:"mc"...}, "data":[{instId,last,bestBid,bestAsk,systemTime}]}
    act=msg.get("action")
    if act in ("snapshot","update") and isinstance(msg.get("data"),list):
        for d in msg["data"]:
            sym=d.get("instId"); last=d.get("last"); bid=d.get("bestBid"); ask=d.get("bestAsk")
            ts=int((d.get("systemTime") or time.time()*1000)//1000)
            if sym and last:
                out.append((sym, ts, float(last), float(bid or last), float(ask or last)))
        return out
    # Format "NEW mix": {"arg":{instType:"USDT-FUTURES",instId:"BTCUSDT_UMCBL"}, "data":[{lastPr,bestBid,bestAsk,ts}]}
    if isinstance(msg.get("data"),list) and isinstance(msg.get("arg"),dict):
        sym=msg["arg"].get("instId","").replace("_UMCBL","")
        for d in msg["data"]:
            last=d.get("lastPr") or d.get("pr")
            bid=d.get("bestBid") or d.get("bidPx") or last
            ask=d.get("bestAsk") or d.get("askPx") or last
            ts=int((d.get("ts") or time.time()*1000)//1000)
            if sym and last:
                out.append((sym, ts, float(last), float(bid), float(ask)))
        return out
    return out

async def run():
    # Prépare deux listes d’abonnements
    sub_old={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"mc","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in SYMS]}
    sub_new={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":f"{s}_UMCBL"} for s in SYMS]}
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20, close_timeout=5) as ws, db() as con:
                # Envoie les deux abonnements. Celui qui parle sera pris en compte.
                await ws.send(json.dumps(sub_old))
                await ws.send(json.dumps(sub_new))
                last_write=time.time()
                while True:
                    try:
                        raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=30)
                    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                        # ping keep-alive par re-subscribe léger
                        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":[{"channel":"ping"}]}))
                        continue
                    try:
                        msg=json.loads(raw)
                    except Exception:
                        continue
                    rows=parse_msg(msg)
                    if not rows:
                        continue
                    for sym,ts,pr,bid,ask in rows:
                        # normalise sym: OLD renvoie déjà BTCUSDT, NEW on a retiré _UMCBL
                        con.execute("INSERT INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,best_bid,best_ask) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)",(sym,ts,pr,bid,ask))
                    last_write=time.time()
        except Exception as e:
            await asyncio.sleep(2)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

    FROM {view};

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, requests, sqlite3

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
BASE = "https://api.bitget.com"

VOL_MIN = 300_000_000.0
DEPTH_MIN = 1_000_000.0
AGE_DAYS = 85
FIX = ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]

def sql_exec(q, params=()):
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB); con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    try: rows = con.execute(q, params).fetchall()
    finally: con.close()
    return rows

def execmany(q, data):
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB); con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    try: con.executemany(q, data); con.commit()
    finally: con.close()

def ensure_schema():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB); c = con.cursor()
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(
                  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                  name TEXT, symbol TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER)""")
    con.commit(); con.close()

def _get_json(url, params=None, timeout=10, retries=2, sleep=0.6):
    for _ in range(retries+1):
        try:
            r = requests.get(url, params=params or {}, timeout=timeout)
            if r.status_code != 200:
                print(f"[HTTP] {url} {r.status_code} {r.text[:160]}"); time.sleep(sleep); continue
            j = r.json()
            code = j.get("code") or j.get("status") or ""
            if code not in ("00000", "success", 200):
                print(f"[API] {url} code={code} msg={j.get('msg') or j.get('message')}")
                time.sleep(sleep); continue
            return j
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[EXC] {url} {type(e).__name__}: {e}"); time.sleep(sleep)
    return None

def top_tickers():
    j = _get_json(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/tickers", {"productType":"umcbl"}, timeout=12, retries=3)
    if not j or not isinstance(j.get("data"), list):
        print("[TOP] empty/invalid response, fallback=empty list"); return []
    rows=[]
    for d in j["data"]:
        s=d.get("symbol","")
        if not s.endswith("_UMCBL"): continue
        base=s.replace("_UMCBL","")
        v=float(d.get("usdtVolume") or d.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        rows.append((base,v))
    rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)
    return rows[:50]

def age_ok(sym):
    j=_get_json(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/candles",
                {"productType":"umcbl","symbol":f"{sym}_UMCBL","granularity":"1day","limit":100})
    try:
        data=(j or {}).get("data") or []
        if not data: print(f"[AGE] {sym} no data"); return False
        oldest=int(data[-1][0]); days=(time.time()*1000-oldest)/1000/86400
        ok=days>=85
        print(f"[AGE] {sym} {'OK' if ok else 'old'} ({int(days)}d)"); return ok
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[AGE_ERR] {sym}: {e}"); return False

def depth_1pct(sym,last):
    try:
        if last<=0: return 0.0
        j=_get_json(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/depth", {"symbol":f"{sym}_UMCBL","limit":200}, timeout=8, retries=2)
        data=(j or {}).get("data") or {}
        bids=data.get("bids") or []; asks=data.get("asks") or []
        lo,hi=last*0.99,last*1.01; tot=0.0
        for p,q in bids:
            try:
                fp,fq=float(p),float(q)
                if fp>=lo: tot+=fp*fq
            except: pass
        for p,q in asks:
            try:
                fp,fq=float(p),float(q)
                if fp<=hi: tot+=fp*fq
            except: pass
        return tot
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[DEPTH_ERR] {sym}: {e}"); return 0.0

def main():
    ensure_schema()
    top=top_tickers()
    if not top:
        print("[UNIVERSE] top50=0 age_ok=0 pass=0 top30_written=0 ts=%d" % int(time.time())); return
    age_ok_list=[(s,v) for s,v in top if age_ok(s)]
    print(f"[INFO] age OK: {len(age_ok_list)}/{len(top)}")
    out=[]
    for s,v in age_ok_list:
        j=_get_json(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/ticker", {"symbol":f"{s}_UMCBL"}, timeout=6, retries=2)
        last=0.0
        try: last=float(((j or {}).get("data") or {}).get("lastPr") or 0)
        except: pass
        d=depth_1pct(s,last)
        ok=(v>=VOL_MIN and d>=DEPTH_MIN)
        print(f"[TEST] {s:<8} vol={v/1e6:7.1f}M depth={d/1e6:6.2}M {'OK' if ok else 'FAIL'}")
        if ok: out.append((s,v,d))
    out.sort(key=lambda x:(x[2],x[1]), reverse=True)
    top30=[s for s,_,_ in out][:25]
    for f in FIX:
        if f not in top30: top30.append(f)
    top30=top30[:30]; ts=int(time.time())
    if top30:
        execmany("INSERT INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES('TOP30',?,?,?)",
                 [(s,i+1,ts) for i,s in enumerate(top30)])
    print(f"[UNIVERSE] top50={len(top)} age_ok={len(age_ok_list)} pass={len(out)} top30_written={len(top30)} ts={ts}")
    for i,s in enumerate(top30,1): print(f"{i:2d}. {s}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

TF_USED=["5m","15m","30m"]
W_TF={"5m":0.20,"15m":0.30,"30m":0.50}
TAU={"5m":0.25,"15m":0.30,"30m":0.35}
ATR_GATE={"5m":0.12,"15m":0.18,"30m":0.25}  # en %

def smx(pos,neg,t):
    import math
    b=math.exp(max(pos,0)/max(t,1e-6))
    s=math.exp(max(neg,0)/max(t,1e-6))
    h=1.0
    z=b+s+h
    return b/z, s/z, h/z

def con():
    c=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contexts_A(
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, pb REAL, ps REAL, ph REAL, score REAL, ts INTEGER)""")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contexts_A_state(
      symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, last_ctx TEXT, persist INT, since_ts INT)""")
    c.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ctxA_symbol_ts ON contexts_A(symbol,ts)")
    return c

def top30(c):
    return [r[0] for r in c.execute("""
      SELECT symbol FROM v_universe ORDER BY symbol LIMIT 35
    """)]

def last_row(c, tf, sym):
    view={"5m":"indic_5m","15m":"indic_15m","30m":"indic_30m"}[tf]
    q=f"""SELECT close, sma20, sma50, macd, macd_sig, macd_hist, rsi14, atr_pct, obv
          FROM {view}
          WHERE symbol=?
          ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1"""
    r=c.execute(q,(sym,)).fetchone()
    return r

def main():
    c=con(); now=int(time.time())
    syms=top30(c)
    ins=0; with_ctx=0
    for s in syms:
        agg_score=agg_pb=agg_ps=agg_ph=0.0; wsum=0.0; seen=False
        for tf in TF_USED:
            r=last_row(c,tf,s)
            if not r: continue
            seen=True
            close,sma20,sma50,macd,sig,hist,rsi,atr_pct,obv=r
            # scores élémentaires sur signaux SQL
            s_ema = 0.0 if sma20 is None or sma50 is None or close is None else ( (sma20 - sma50) / (close*0.01 + 1e-12) )
            s_macd = 0.0 if macd is None or sig is None else ( (macd - sig) / (abs(macd)+1e-9) )
            s_rsi = 0.0 if rsi is None else ((rsi-50.0)/50.0)
            s_obv = 0.0 if obv is None else max(-1.0, min(1.0, obv / 1e9))
            # simple proxy ADX via amplitude MACD hist
            s_adx = 0.0 if hist is None else max(-1.0, min(1.0, abs(hist)/ (abs(macd)+1e-9) ))
            score_raw = 0.35*s_ema + 0.25*s_macd + 0.20*s_rsi + 0.10*s_adx + 0.10*s_obv
            score_raw = max(-1.0, min(1.0, score_raw))
            gate = 1.0 if (atr_pct or 0.0) >= ATR_GATE[tf] else 0.0
            score = gate * score_raw
            pb,ps,ph = smx(max(score,0), max(-score,0), TAU[tf])
            w=W_TF[tf]; wsum+=w
            agg_score += w*score; agg_pb += w*pb; agg_ps += w*ps; agg_ph += w*ph
        if not seen or wsum==0:
            c.execute("INSERT INTO contexts_A(symbol,ctx,pb,ps,ph,score,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                      (s,"none",0.0,0.0,1.0,0.0,now)); ins+=1; continue
        agg_score/=wsum; agg_pb/=wsum; agg_ps/=wsum; agg_ph/=wsum
        # hysteresis minimale
        row=c.execute("SELECT last_ctx,persist FROM contexts_A_state WHERE symbol=?",(s,)).fetchone()
        prev,pers=(row[0],row[1]) if row else ("none",0)
        ctx = "buy" if agg_pb>=0.60 and agg_pb>agg_ps else ("sell" if agg_ps>=0.60 and agg_ps>agg_pb else ("hold" if agg_ph>=max(agg_pb,agg_ps) else "hold"))
        if prev in("buy","sell") and ctx!=prev and max(agg_pb,agg_ps)<0.45: ctx=prev
        pers = (pers+1) if ctx==prev else 1
        if ctx!=prev and pers<2: ctx=prev
        c.execute("INSERT INTO contexts_A(symbol,ctx,pb,ps,ph,score,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                  (s,ctx,agg_pb,agg_ps,agg_ph,agg_score,now))
        c.execute("INSERT INTO contexts_A_state(symbol,last_ctx,persist,since_ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?) \
                   ON CONFLICT(symbol) DO UPDATE SET last_ctx=excluded.last_ctx,persist=excluded.persist,since_ts=excluded.since_ts",
                  (s,ctx,pers,now))
        ins+=1; with_ctx+= int(ctx!='none')
    print(f"[AnalyseA] inserted={ins} with_ctx={with_ctx} ts={now}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, requests, sqlite3

ADB=os.getenv("ADB","/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
SYMS=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]
TF_MAP={60:("ohlcv_1m","1min"),300:("ohlcv_5m","5min"),900:("ohlcv_15m","15min"),1800:("ohlcv_30m","30min")}
LIMIT=300

S_BASE="https://api.bitget.com"

def fetch_v2(sym, gran):
    url=f"{S_BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/candles"
    p={"productType":"umcbl","symbol":sym,"granularity":gran,"limit":LIMIT}
    r=requests.get(url, params=p, timeout=10)
    if r.status_code!=200: raise RuntimeError(f"v2 {r.status_code}")
    j=r.json()
    if j.get("code") not in ("00000","0000",0,None): raise RuntimeError(f"v2 code {j.get('code')}")
    return j.get("data",[])

def fetch_v1(sym_umcbl, gran_str):
    url=f"{S_BASE}/api/mix/v1/market/candles"
    p={"symbol":sym_umcbl,"granularity":gran_str,"limit":LIMIT}
    r=requests.get(url, params=p, timeout=10)
    if r.status_code!=200: raise RuntimeError(f"v1 {r.status_code}")
    j=r.json()
    # v1 répond sans 'code' uniforme parfois; on vérifie présence 'data'
    if "data" not in j: raise RuntimeError("v1 no data")
    return j["data"]

def to_rows(sym, data):
    out=[]
    for k in data:
        # Format: [ts, open, high, low, close, volume, ...] ts en ms
        ts=int(int(k[0])//1000)
        o,h,l,c,vol=map(float,[k[1],k[2],k[3],k[4],k[5]])
        out.append((sym,ts,o,h,l,c,vol))
    return out

def upsert(tbl, rows):
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute(f"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {tbl}(
        symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
        open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
        PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))""")
    con.execute(f"CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_{tbl}_sym_ts ON {tbl}(symbol,ts)")
    con.executemany(f"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO {tbl}(symbol,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.close()

def main():
    ok=err=0
    for gran,(tbl,gran_str) in TF_MAP.items():
        for s in SYMS:
            try:
                # v2 priorité
                data=fetch_v2(s, gran)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    data=fetch_v1(f"{s}_UMCBL", gran_str)
                except Exception as e2:
                    print(f"ERR {s} {gran} {e2}")
                    err+=1
                    continue
            rows=to_rows(s,data)
            if rows:
                upsert(tbl, rows)
                print(f"{s} {gran}s -> {tbl} +{len(rows)}")
                ok+=1
            time.sleep(0.25)
        time.sleep(0.5)
    print(f"DONE ok={ok} err={err}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, os
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
SRC="/opt/scalp/project/data/top_candidates.txt"
FIX=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]
TARGET=int(os.getenv("TARGET","30"))

pairs=[]
for line in open(SRC):
    line=line.strip()
    if not line or '|' not in line: continue
    sym,vol=line.split('|',1)
    try: pairs.append((sym.strip().upper(), float(vol)))
    except: pass
pairs.sort(key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)

seen=set(); sel=[]
for sym,sc in pairs:
    if sym not in seen:
        sel.append((sym, float(sc))); seen.add(sym)
    if len(sel) >= max(0,TARGET-5): break
for f in FIX:
    if f not in seen:
        sel.append((f, 0.0)); seen.add(f)
while len(sel) < TARGET:  # si pool <25, complète avec fixes en double score 0
    for f in FIX:
        if len(sel) >= TARGET: break
        sel.append((f, 0.0))

con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
c=con.cursor()
c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  name TEXT, symbol TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER
)""")
now=int(time.time())
c.executemany("INSERT INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES('TOP30',?,?,?)",
              [(s,sc,now) for s,sc in sel[:TARGET]])
print(f"[TOP30] {len(sel[:TARGET])} écrits @ {now}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, math

ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

# Paramètres
ATR_MIN_PCT=0.10
SCORE_TRIGGER=0.60
COOLDOWN_S=300          # 5 min

def main():
    now=int(time.time())
    adb=sqlite3.connect(ADB, timeout=8, isolation_level=None)
    adb.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    bdb=sqlite3.connect(BDB, timeout=8, isolation_level=None)
    bdb.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000"); bdb.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    bc=bdb.cursor()
    bc.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_plan(
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, side TEXT, score REAL,
        entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL, ts INTEGER)""")
    bc.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_state(
        symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, last_side TEXT, last_ts INTEGER)""")

    # Contextes utilisables
    rows = adb.execute("""
      WITH m AS (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) ts FROM contexts_A GROUP BY symbol)
      SELECT c.symbol, c.ctx, c.pb, c.ps, c.ts
      FROM contexts_A c JOIN m ON c.symbol=m.symbol AND c.ts=m.ts
      WHERE c.ctx!='none'
    """).fetchall()
    if not rows:
        print("[B] 0 contextes utilisables"); return

    # Dernier tick et vol basique (spread proxy)
    ticks = dict(bdb.execute("""
      SELECT symbol, price, best_bid, best_ask, MAX(ts)
      FROM ticks WHERE ts>=strftime('%s','now')-60 GROUP BY symbol
    """).fetchall())

    inserted=0
    for sym,ctx,pb,ps,cts in rows:
        if sym not in ticks: continue
        price,bid,ask,_ = ticks[sym]
        spread = 0 if price==0 else abs((ask-bid)/price)*100
        # score simple: si ctx buy → score=pb ; ctx sell → score=ps
        score = pb if ctx=='buy' else ps if ctx=='sell' else 0.5
        if score < SCORE_TRIGGER: continue
        if spread > 1.0: continue  # SPREAD_MAX_PCT=1%

        # cooldown
        bs = bc.execute("SELECT last_ts FROM b_state WHERE symbol=?",(sym,)).fetchone()
        if bs and bs[0] and bs[0] > now-COOLDOWN_S: continue

        # ATR% proxy à partir de ticks (fallback 0.15) — à remplacer si dispo
        atr_pct = 0.15
        side = 'buy' if ctx=='buy' else 'sell'
        entry = price
        sl = entry*(1-0.012) if side=='buy' else entry*(1+0.012)
        tp = entry*(1+0.018) if side=='buy' else entry*(1-0.018)

        if atr_pct < ATR_MIN_PCT: pass  # garde quand même avec proxy

        bc.execute("""INSERT INTO signals_B_plan(symbol,ctx,side,score,entry,sl,tp,ts)
                      VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)""",(sym,ctx,side,round(score,3),entry,sl,tp,now))
        bc.execute("""INSERT INTO b_state(symbol,last_side,last_ts)
                      VALUES(?,?,?)
                      ON CONFLICT(symbol) DO UPDATE SET last_side=excluded.last_side,last_ts=excluded.last_ts
                   """,(sym,side,now))
        inserted+=1

    print(f"[B] inserted={inserted} ctx_used={len(rows)} ts={now}")
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, websockets, time
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"
SUB={"op":"subscribe","args":[{"channel":"ticker","instType":"mc","instId":"BTCUSDT"}]}
def price_of(it):
    for k in ("last","lastPr","price","close"):
        v=it.get(k)
        if v is None: continue
        try: return float(v)
        except: pass
    return None
async def main():
    n=0
    async with websockets.connect(URI,ping_interval=20,ping_timeout=20,close_timeout=5) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(SUB))
        while n<5:
            raw=await ws.recv()
            if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)): raw=raw.decode()
            try: msg=json.loads(raw)
            except: continue
            for it in msg.get("data") or []:
                p=price_of(it)
                if p is not None:
                    n+=1
                    print("TICK", n, p, int(time.time()))
asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Route les nouveaux signaux vers orders_sim (qty=0.0, price=signal.price)
import sqlite3, time, argparse

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"

def conn():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
    return con

def route_once(con):
    last_id = con.execute("SELECT COALESCE(MAX(signal_id),0) FROM orders_sim").fetchone()[0]
    rows = con.execute(
        "SELECT id,symbol,side,price,created_ts FROM signals_B WHERE id>? ORDER BY id LIMIT 1000",
        (last_id,)
    ).fetchall()
    n = 0
    now = int(time.time())
    for sig_id,symbol,side,price,sig_ts in rows:
        con.execute("""INSERT INTO orders_sim(signal_id,symbol,side,qty,price,ts,created_ts)
                       VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)""",
                    (sig_id,symbol,side,0.0,price,int(sig_ts),now))
        n += 1
    return n

def loop():
    con = conn()
    while True:
        n = route_once(con)
        if n:
            print(f"routed {n} order(s)", flush=True)
        time.sleep(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--once", action="store_true")
    args = ap.parse_args()
    if args.once:
        print(f"routed {route_once(conn())} order(s)")
    else:
        loop()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, requests, sqlite3
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
BASE="https://api.bitget.com"
FIX=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]
FALLBACK=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","DOGEUSDT","ADAUSDT","TRXUSDT",
"LINKUSDT","LTCUSDT","DOTUSDT","BCHUSDT","AVAXUSDT","APTUSDT","XLMUSDT","ATOMUSDT",
"NEARUSDT","FILUSDT","SUIUSDT","ARBUSDT","HBARUSDT","OPUSDT","MATICUSDT","TONUSDT",
"INJUSDT","TIAUSDT","AAVEUSDT","ETCUSDT","ALGOUSDT","ICPUSDT"]

def jget(url, params, retries=2, tout=10):
    for _ in range(retries+1):
        try:
            r=requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=tout)
            if r.status_code==200: return r.json()
        except Exception: pass
        time.sleep(0.4)
    return None

def top_by_volume():
    # v2 correct: productType=USDT-FUTURES
    j=jget(f"{BASE}/api/v2/mix/market/tickers", {"productType":"USDT-FUTURES"})
    if j and isinstance(j.get("data"), list):
        rows=[]
        for d in j["data"]:
            s=(d.get("symbol") or "").replace("_UMCBL","")
            if not s.endswith("USDT"): continue
            v=d.get("usdtVolume") or d.get("quoteVolume") or 0
            try: v=float(v)
            except: v=0.0
            if v>0: rows.append((s,v))
        rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)
        return rows[:60]  # on prend large puis on coupera
    # v1 secours
    j=jget(f"{BASE}/api/mix/v1/market/tickers", {"productType":"umcbl"})
    if j and isinstance(j.get("data"), list):
        rows=[]
        for d in j["data"]:
            s=(d.get("symbol") or "").replace("_UMCBL","")
            if not s.endswith("USDT"): continue
            v=d.get("usdtVolume") or d.get("quoteVolume") or 0
            try: v=float(v)
            except: v=0.0
            if v>0: rows.append((s,v))
        rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)
        return rows[:60]
    # fallback statique
    return [(s,1.0) for s in FALLBACK[:60]]

def write_top30(pairs):
    # score = volume ; fixes à 9e9 puis dédupe et tronque à 30
    scored=dict(pairs)
    for f in FIX: scored[f]=9_000_000_000.0
    top=sorted(scored.items(), key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)[:30]
    ts=int(time.time())
    con=sqlite3.connect(DB); c=con.cursor()
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000")
    c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        name TEXT, symbol TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER)""")
    c.execute("DELETE FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30'")
    c.executemany("INSERT INTO top_scores(name,symbol,score,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?)",
                  [("TOP30",s,sc,ts) for s,sc in top])
    con.commit(); con.close()
    return ts, top

def main():
    pairs=top_by_volume()
    ts, top=write_top30(pairs)
    print(f"[TOP30] {len(top)} écrits @ {ts}")
    for i,(s,sc) in enumerate(top,1):
        print(f"{i:2d}. {s} | {sc:.0f}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
TFs=("1m","5m","15m","30m")

DDL=lambda t: f"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {t}(
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
  open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
  PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts)
);"""

def has_col(c,t,col): return any(r[1]==col for r in c.execute(f"PRAGMA table_info({t})"))

con=sqlite3.connect(DB); c=con.cursor()
c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")

for tf in TFs:
  t=f"ohlcv_{tf}"
  c.execute(DDL(t))
  # migrate if old column 'base'
  if has_col(c,t,"base") and not has_col(c,t,"symbol"):
    c.execute(f"CREATE TABLE _new_{t}(symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL, PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))")
    c.execute(f"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO _new_{t}(symbol,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) SELECT base,ts,open,high,low,close,volume FROM {t}")
    c.execute(f"DROP TABLE {t}")
    c.execute(f"ALTER TABLE _new_{t} RENAME TO {t}")
  # migrate if symbol missing entirely (some stray schema)
  if not has_col(c,t,"symbol"):
    c.execute(f"ALTER TABLE {t} ADD COLUMN symbol TEXT")
con.commit(); con.close()
print("OK: OHLCV normalized for 1m/5m/15m/30m")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, json, math
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
OUT="/opt/scalp/project/data/analyse_A_out.json"

def series(con, sym, tf, n):
    return con.execute(f"SELECT close FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT ?",(sym,n)).fetchall()

def mom(v): return (v[0]-v[-1])/v[-1] if len(v)>1 and v[-1] else 0.0
def vola(v): 
    if len(v)<2: return 0.0
    m=sum(v)/len(v); return math.sqrt(sum((x-m)**2 for x in v)/len(v))/m if m else 0.0

con=sqlite3.connect(DB)
syms=[r[0] for r in con.execute("SELECT symbol FROM tops WHERE ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM tops) AND name='TOP35'")]
# normaliser les ids vers 'BASEUSDT'
norm=lambda s: s if s.endswith("USDT") else s.replace("/USDT","USDT").split(':')[0].replace('/','')
ctx={}
for s in syms:
    base = norm(s)
    v5  = [x[0] for x in series(con, base,  "5m",  60)]
    v15 = [x[0] for x in series(con, base, "15m", 60)]
    v30 = [x[0] for x in series(con, base, "30m", 60)]
    if not v5 or not v15 or not v30: 
        continue
    m5,m15,m30 = mom(v5), mom(v15), mom(v30)
    vol = 0.5*vola(v5)+0.3*vola(v15)+0.2*vola(v30)
    score = 0.5*m5 + 0.3*m15 + 0.2*m30
    trend = "bull" if score>0 else "bear"
    strength = round((abs(score)* (1+vol)),6)
    ctx[base]={"symbol":base+"USDT","trend":trend,"strength":strength,"volatility":vol}
with open(OUT,"w") as f: json.dump(ctx,f,indent=2)
print(f"[AnalyseA/OHLCV] {len(ctx)} contextes -> {OUT}")
con.close()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, json, time, statistics as st

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
OUT_JSON="/opt/scalp/project/data/analyse_A_out.json"

NOW=int(time.time())
REQ_1M=200; REQ_5M=200; REQ_15M=100; REQ_30M=60

con=sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
c=con.cursor()
c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL"); c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")

c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contexts_A(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, has_1m INT, has_5m INT, has_15m INT, has_30m INT,
  ctx TEXT, ts INTEGER
)""")

# pull TOP30
syms=[r[0] for r in c.execute("""
  SELECT symbol FROM top_scores
  WHERE ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM top_scores) AND name='TOP30'
  ORDER BY score DESC, symbol ASC LIMIT 30
""").fetchall()]

def enough(tbl, sym, need):
  row=c.execute(f"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {tbl} WHERE symbol=?;", (sym,)).fetchone()
  return (row and row[0] >= need)

contexts=[]
ts=NOW
for s in syms:
  h1=enough("ohlcv_1m", s, REQ_1M)
  h5=enough("ohlcv_5m", s, REQ_5M)
  h15=enough("ohlcv_15m", s, REQ_15M)
  h30=enough("ohlcv_30m", s, REQ_30M)

  ctx=None
  if h1:
    # mini-contexte: slope sur 1m via 50 dernières closes
    rows=c.execute("SELECT close FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 50;", (s,)).fetchall()
    closes=[r[0] for r in rows][::-1]
    if len(closes)>=20:
      sma20=sum(closes[-20:])/20.0
      sma50=sum(closes)/len(closes)
      mom=closes[-1]-closes[-5] if len(closes)>=5 else 0.0
      vol=st.pstdev(closes[-20:]) if len(closes)>=20 else 0.0
      trend="up" if sma20>sma50 else "down"
      ctx=json.dumps({"trend":trend,"mom":mom,"vol":vol}, separators=(",",":"))

  c.execute("""INSERT INTO contexts_A(symbol,has_1m,has_5m,has_15m,has_30m,ctx,ts)
               VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)""",(s,int(h1),int(h5),int(h15),int(h30),ctx,ts))
  contexts.append({"symbol":s,"has_1m":h1,"has_5m":h5,"has_15m":h15,"has_30m":h30,"ctx":json.loads(ctx) if ctx else None})

# export json
with open(OUT_JSON,"w") as f: json.dump({"ts":ts,"contexts":contexts}, f)

# print summary
total=len(contexts)
with_ctx=sum(1 for x in contexts if x["ctx"] is not None)
print(f"[AnalyseA] contexts={total} with_ctx={with_ctx} ts={ts}")

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -e
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ws.log"
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
# si pas de tick depuis 90s → restart
LAST=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) FROM signals_B;")
NOW=$(date +%s)
if [ $((NOW - LAST)) -gt 90 ]; then
  pkill -f analysis_B_ws.py 2>/dev/null || true
  nohup /opt/scalp/project/scripts/analysis_B_ws.py >"$LOG" 2>&1 &
  echo "WS_RESTART $(date -Is)" >> "$LOG"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
attempts=0; max=5
while :; do
  if sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS u_syms(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
DELETE FROM u_syms;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO u_syms(symbol) SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current;
COMMIT;
DETACH DATABASE udb;
SQL
  then exit 0; fi
  attempts=$((attempts+1)); [ $attempts -ge $max ] && exit 1
  sleep 1
done
SH

cat > "$SCR/health_o_strict.sh" <<'SH'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
retry(){ n=0; until sqlite3 -noheader "$ADB" "$1"; do n=$((n+1)); [ $n -ge 5 ] && return 1; sleep 1; done }
fail(){ echo "FAIL: $*" >&2; exit 1; }

covq=$'WITH r AS (\n SELECT \'5m\' tf, COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) sy, SUM(c) rw FROM (SELECT symbol, COUNT(*) c FROM ohlcv_5m GROUP BY symbol)\n UNION ALL\n SELECT \'15m\', COUNT(DISTINCT symbol), SUM(c) FROM (SELECT symbol, COUNT(*) c FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol)\n UNION ALL\n SELECT \'30m\', COUNT(DISTINCT symbol), SUM(c) FROM (SELECT symbol, COUNT(*) c FROM ohlcv_30m GROUP BY symbol)\n), g AS (\n SELECT \'5m\' tf, SUM(missing) ms FROM (SELECT symbol, MAX(0, ((MAX(ts)-MIN(ts))/300+1-COUNT(*))) AS missing FROM ohlcv_5m GROUP BY symbol)\n UNION ALL SELECT \'15m\', SUM(missing) FROM (SELECT symbol, MAX(0, ((MAX(ts)-MIN(ts))/900+1-COUNT(*))) AS missing FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol)\n UNION ALL SELECT \'30m\', SUM(missing) FROM (SELECT symbol, MAX(0, ((MAX(ts)-MIN(ts))/1800+1-COUNT(*))) AS missing FROM ohlcv_30m GROUP BY symbol)\n) SELECT r.tf, r.sy, r.rw, g.ms FROM r JOIN g USING(tf);'
out=$(retry "$covq") || fail locked
echo "$out" | awk '{printf "%s sy=%s rows=%s gaps=%s\n",$1,$2,$3,$4}'
echo "$out" | awk '$2!=35 || $4!=0 {bad=1} END{exit bad}' || fail "coverage/gaps"

for t in 5m 15m 30m; do
  sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT 1 FROM ohlcv_${t} GROUP BY symbol,ts HAVING COUNT(*)>1 LIMIT 1;" | grep -q . && fail "dups $t"
  sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM ohlcv_${t} GROUP BY symbol HAVING COUNT(*)!=100);" | grep -qx 0 || fail "rows!=100 $t"
done

setq=$'ATTACH DATABASE \''"$UDB"$'\'' AS udb; WITH cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol), uni AS (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)\nSELECT (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM uni)) AS extra,\n       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM uni EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur)) AS missing; DETACH DATABASE udb;'
sqlite3 -noheader "$ADB" "$setq" | grep -qx "0|0" || fail "set mismatch"

mx=$(sqlite3 -noheader "$ADB" "SELECT (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_5m),(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m),(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m);")
echo "max_ts 5m|15m|30m: $mx"
echo "$mx" | awk -F'|' '{if($1!=$2 || $1!=$3 || ($1%300)!=0) exit 1}' || fail "freshness"

echo "OK: o.db health strict"
SH
chmod +x "$SCR/health_o_strict.sh"

cat > "$SCR/run_ohlcv_daemon.sh" <<'SH'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ohlcv_daemon.log"
mkdir -p "/opt/scalp/project/logs"
STEP=300; OFFSET=1; GRACE=4; RETRY=1
align(){ n=$(date +%s); next=$(( n - (n % STEP) + STEP + OFFSET )); sleep $(( next - n )); }
run_cycle(){
  "/opt/scalp/project/scripts/fetch_ohlcv_once.sh"  >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  "/opt/scalp/project/scripts/harden_o_db.sh"       >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  "/opt/scalp/project/scripts/purge_non_current.sh" >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
}
expected_ts(){ n=$(date +%s); echo $(( n - (n % STEP) )); }
have_expected(){ exp="$1"; sqlite3 -noheader "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db" "
SELECT MIN(ok) FROM (
  SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END ok FROM ohlcv_5m
  UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END FROM ohlcv_15m
  UNION ALL SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END FROM ohlcv_30m
);"; }
while true; do
  align; exp=$(expected_ts); run_cycle; ok=$(have_expected "$exp" || echo 0)
  if [ "$ok" != "1" ] && [ "$RETRY" -gt 0 ]; then sleep "$GRACE"; run_cycle; fi
done
SH
chmod +x "$SCR/run_ohlcv_daemon.sh"

echo "[4/6] install to bin"
install -m 0755 "$SCR/run_ohlcv_daemon.sh" "$BIN/run_ohlcv_daemon.sh"

Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/fetch_ticks_bitget.py
Size: 4315
MTime: 2025-10-10 10:23:23.085729074 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, sqlite3, time, signal, ssl
from urllib.request import urlopen, Request
from urllib.parse import urlencode
import websockets

UDB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
TDB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

REST_BASE = "https://api.bitget.com"
WS_URI    = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"
PRODUCT   = "USDT-FUTURES"   # << cible unique

def http_get(path, params=None, timeout=10):
    url = REST_BASE + path
    if params: url += "?" + urlencode(params)
    req = Request(url, headers={"User-Agent":"tick-fetch/1.0"})
    with urlopen(req, timeout=timeout) as r:
        return json.loads(r.read().decode())

def get_universe():
    con = sqlite3.connect(UDB)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT symbol FROM v_universe_current LIMIT 35;")
    syms = [r[0].upper() for r in cur.fetchall()]
    con.close()
    return syms

def setup_db():
    con = sqlite3.connect(TDB)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
        symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
        instId TEXT NOT NULL,
        ts INTEGER NOT NULL,      -- ms
        price REAL NOT NULL,
        size REAL NOT NULL,
        side TEXT NOT NULL,
        PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
    );""")
    cur.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_sym_ts ON ticks(symbol, ts DESC);")
    con.commit(); con.close()

def discover_instIds_usdt_futures(target_syms):
    """
    Mappe BTCUSDT -> instId exact en USDT-FUTURES via REST:
    GET /api/v2/mix/market/contracts?productType=USDT-FUTURES
    """
    data = http_get("/api/v2/mix/market/contracts", {"productType": PRODUCT})
    insts = data.get("data", [])
    # Construire dictionnaire {BASEUSDT: instId}
    out = {}
    # normaliser entrée: 'BTCUSDT' etc.
    want = set(target_syms)
    for inst in insts:
        instId = inst.get("instId","").upper()          # ex: BTCUSDT_XXXX
        base   = inst.get("symbol","").upper()          # ex: BTCUSDT
        if base in want:
            out[base] = instId
    return out

async def subscribe(ws, instIds):
    args = [f"trade:{i}" for i in instIds]
    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))

async def run():
    setup_db()
    symbols = get_universe()              # ex: ['BTCUSDT', ...]
    inst_map = discover_instIds_usdt_futures(symbols)
    instIds = [inst_map[s] for s in symbols if s in inst_map]
    if not instIds:
        print("No instIds resolved for USDT-FUTURES. Abort.")
        return
    print(f"Subscribing {len(instIds)} instIds on {PRODUCT}:", instIds[:5], "...")
    ssl_ctx = ssl.create_default_context()
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(WS_URI, ping_interval=20, ssl=ssl_ctx) as ws:
                await subscribe(ws, instIds)
                con = sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None, timeout=10)
                cur = con.cursor()
                async for msg in ws:
                    d = json.loads(msg)
                    if "data" not in d: 
                        # log event/error minimal
                        if "event" in d: print("evt:", d)
                        continue
                    for t in d["data"]:
                        instId = t.get("instId","").upper()
                        # retrouver symbol "base USDT" à partir de instId via inverse
                        base = instId.split("_")[0] if "_" in instId else instId
                        # seulement si présent dans l'univers
                        price = float(t.get("price","0"))
                        size  = float(t.get("size","0"))
                        side  = t.get("side","")
                        ts    = int(t.get("ts", int(time.time()*1000)))
                        cur.execute(
                          "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ticks(symbol,instId,ts,price,size,side) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?);",
                          (base, instId, ts, price, size, side)
                        )
        except Exception as e:
            print("WS error:", e, "reconnect in 5s")
            await asyncio.sleep(5)

def main():
    loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
    for sig in (signal.SIGINT, signal.SIGTERM):
        try: loop.add_signal_handler(sig, loop.stop)
        except NotImplementedError: pass
    loop.run_until_complete(run())

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"

UDB="$ROOT/data/u.db"

PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
ATTACH DATABASE '$ODB' AS odb;

-- table canonique
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS universe_current(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  src TEXT,
  updated_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);

DELETE FROM universe_current;

INSERT INTO universe_current(symbol,src)
SELECT DISTINCT symbol,'a15'
FROM adb.ohlcv_15m
WHERE symbol IS NOT NULL
ORDER BY symbol
LIMIT 35;

-- vue unique utilisée partout
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_universe_current;
CREATE VIEW v_universe_current AS
SELECT symbol FROM universe_current ORDER BY symbol;

DETACH DATABASE adb;
DETACH DATABASE odb;
SQL

echo "Universe rebuilt from a.db (ohlcv_15m)"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
BASE="/opt/scalp/project"
LOG="$BASE/logs"; mkdir -p "$LOG"

echo "[1] stop writers"
systemctl stop scalp-ws.service 2>/dev/null || true
systemctl stop scalp-router.service 2>/dev/null || true
systemctl stop scalp-closer.service 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f ws_ctx_ticks 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f router_simple.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f closer_tp_sl.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f analysis_B_ws.py 2>/dev/null || true
sleep 1

echo "[2] kill handles if any"
command -v fuser >/dev/null && fuser -k "$DB" 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[3] clean WAL files"
rm -f "${DB}-wal" "${DB}-shm"

echo "[4] quick integrity check"
IC=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000; PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL; PRAGMA integrity_check;")
echo "integrity_check=$IC"

if [ "$IC" != "ok" ]; then
  echo "[5] dump+restore"
  cp -f "$DB" "${DB}.bak.$(date +%s)"
  sqlite3 "$DB" ".timeout 8000" ".mode insert" ".output $DB.recover.sql" ".dump"
  mv "$DB" "${DB}.corrupt.$(date +%s)"
  sqlite3 "$DB" < "$DB.recover.sql"
  rm -f "$DB.recover.sql"
  echo "[6] post-restore check"
  sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA integrity_check;"
fi

echo "[7] vacuum"
sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000; VACUUM;"

echo "[8] ensure required tables"
sqlite3 "$DB" "
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS top_scores(id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,name TEXT,symbol TEXT,score REAL,ts INTEGER);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,symbol TEXT,side TEXT,price REAL,reason TEXT,created_ts INTEGER);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sig_cts ON signals_B(created_ts);
"

echo "[9] regenerate TOP30 from candidates"
python3 "$BASE/scripts/top30_from_candidates.py"

echo "[10] restart WS single-per-symbol"
nohup "$BASE/scripts/ws_ctx_ticks_single.py" >"$LOG/ws_ctx_ticks.log" 2>&1 &
sleep 3
sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT * FROM v_health;" | sed -n '1,1p'
tail -n 30 "$LOG/ws_ctx_ticks.log" || true

#!/usr/bin/env bash

PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

-- Tables OHLCV (ts en secondes UNIX)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_5m(
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  ts     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  open   REAL NOT NULL,
  high   REAL NOT NULL,
  low    REAL NOT NULL,
  close  REAL NOT NULL,
  volume REAL NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(symbol, ts)
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_5m_symbol_ts ON ohlcv_5m(symbol, ts DESC);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_15m(
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  ts     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  open   REAL NOT NULL,
  high   REAL NOT NULL,
  low    REAL NOT NULL,
  close  REAL NOT NULL,
  volume REAL NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(symbol, ts)
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_15m_symbol_ts ON ohlcv_15m(symbol, ts DESC);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_30m(
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  ts     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  open   REAL NOT NULL,
  high   REAL NOT NULL,
  low    REAL NOT NULL,
  close  REAL NOT NULL,
  volume REAL NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(symbol, ts)
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_30m_symbol_ts ON ohlcv_30m(symbol, ts DESC);
SQL

echo "o.db schema ready at $ODB"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, os
BDB=os.getenv("BDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db")
ADB=os.getenv("ADB","/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
TDB=os.getenv("TDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db")

SQL = f"""
ATTACH '{ADB.replace("'","''")}' AS A;
ATTACH '{TDB.replace("'","''")}' AS T;
PRAGMA main.journal_mode=WAL;

-- DDL sûrs dans B
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ctx_latest(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ctx TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks_latest(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ts INTEGER, price REAL, bid REAL, ask REAL
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS params(key TEXT PRIMARY KEY, val REAL);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO params(key,val) VALUES
 ('base_notional_usdt',100.0), ('risk_step_pct',0.015);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_plan(
  symbol TEXT, side TEXT, ctx TEXT, score REAL, ts INTEGER,
  entry REAL, lev INTEGER, qty REAL, notional REAL,
  sl REAL, tp1 REAL, tp2 REAL, tp3 REAL
);

-- ctx (buy/sell) instantané depuis A
DELETE FROM ctx_latest;
INSERT INTO ctx_latest(symbol,ctx,score,ts)
SELECT symbol,
       ctx,
       CASE WHEN ctx='buy' THEN pb WHEN ctx='sell' THEN ps ELSE ph END,
       ts
FROM A.v_contexts_A_latest
WHERE ctx IN ('buy','sell');

-- dernier tick par symbol depuis T
DELETE FROM ticks_latest;
WITH m AS (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) mts FROM T.ticks GROUP BY symbol)
INSERT INTO ticks_latest(symbol,ts,price,bid,ask)
SELECT t.symbol,t.ts,t.price,t.bid,t.ask
FROM T.ticks t JOIN m ON m.symbol=t.symbol AND m.mts=t.ts;

-- plans
DELETE FROM signals_B_plan;
WITH P AS (
  SELECT
    (SELECT val FROM params WHERE key='base_notional_usdt') AS base_notional,
    (SELECT val FROM params WHERE key='risk_step_pct')     AS step
)
INSERT INTO signals_B_plan(symbol,side,ctx,score,ts,entry,lev,qty,notional,sl,tp1,tp2,tp3)
SELECT
  c.symbol,
  CASE WHEN c.ctx='buy' THEN 'long' ELSE 'short' END AS side,
  c.ctx,
  ROUND(c.score,2),
  c.ts,
  t.price AS entry,
  CASE WHEN c.score>=40 THEN 5 WHEN c.score>=30 THEN 4
       WHEN c.score>=20 THEN 3 WHEN c.score>=10 THEN 2 ELSE 1 END AS lev,
  ROUND(CASE WHEN t.price>0 THEN ((SELECT base_notional FROM P)*(c.score/50.0))/t.price ELSE 0 END, 6) AS qty,
  ROUND((SELECT base_notional FROM P)*(c.score/50.0), 2) AS notional,
  CASE WHEN c.ctx='buy' THEN ROUND(t.price*(1-(SELECT step FROM P)),6)
       ELSE ROUND(t.price*(1+(SELECT step FROM P)),6) END AS sl,
  CASE WHEN c.ctx='buy' THEN ROUND(t.price*(1+(SELECT step FROM P)),6)
       ELSE ROUND(t.price*(1-(SELECT step FROM P)),6) END AS tp1,
  CASE WHEN c.ctx='buy' THEN ROUND(t.price*(1+2*(SELECT step FROM P)),6)
       ELSE ROUND(t.price*(1-2*(SELECT step FROM P)),6) END AS tp2,
  CASE WHEN c.ctx='buy' THEN ROUND(t.price*(1+3*(SELECT step FROM P)),6)
       ELSE ROUND(t.price*(1-3*(SELECT step FROM P)),6) END AS tp3
FROM ctx_latest c
JOIN ticks_latest t USING(symbol);

DETACH A; DETACH T;
"""
if __name__=="__main__":
    con=sqlite3.connect(BDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.executescript("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    con.executescript(SQL)
    n=con.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM signals_B_plan").fetchone()[0]
    print("signals_B_plan:", n)
    # échantillon
    for r in con.execute("SELECT symbol,side,entry,sl,tp1,ts FROM signals_B_plan ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 5"):
        print("|".join(map(str,r)))
    con.close()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db

cut_tf() {
  local tbl=$1 tf=$2 keep
  keep=$(sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT keep_rows FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='$tf';")
  [ -z "$keep" ] && keep=1000
  # Liste des symboles
  sqlite3 -newline $'\n' -list "$ADB" "SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM $tbl;" | while read -r sym; do
    [ -z "$sym" ] && continue
    # ts de coupure = ts de la N-ième plus récente
    ts_cut=$(sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT ts FROM $tbl WHERE symbol='$sym' ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1 OFFSET $((keep-1));")
    [ -z "$ts_cut" ] && continue
    sqlite3 "$ADB" "DELETE FROM $tbl WHERE symbol='$sym' AND ts < $ts_cut;"
  done
}

cut_tf ohlcv_5m  5m
cut_tf ohlcv_15m 15m
cut_tf ohlcv_30m 30m

# Sécurité: purge par temps max
sqlite3 "$ADB" "
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m  WHERE ts < strftime('%s','now') - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='5m');
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m WHERE ts < strftime('%s','now') - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='15m');
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m WHERE ts < strftime('%s','now') - (SELECT keep_secs FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='30m');
VACUUM;
"
echo "[compact_ohlcv_cutoff] done"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db"
LAG_MAX="${LAG_MAX_SEC:-60}"

latest_sig=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) FROM signals_B;")
latest_ord=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COALESCE(MAX(created_ts),0) FROM orders_sim;")
backlog=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM signals_B s LEFT JOIN orders_sim o ON o.signal_id=s.id WHERE o.id IS NULL;")

now=$(date +%s)
lag=$(( latest_sig - latest_ord ))
age_last_ord=$(( now - latest_ord ))

msg="WATCHDOG:
lag=${lag}s  age_last_order=${age_last_ord}s  backlog=${backlog}
sig_ts=$(date -d @${latest_sig} +'%F %T')  ord_ts=$(date -d @${latest_ord} +'%F %T')"

if [ "$lag" -gt "$LAG_MAX" ] || [ "$age_last_ord" -gt "$LAG_MAX" ]; then
  systemctl restart scalp-router.service || true
  if [ -n "${TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN:-}" ] && [ -n "${CHAT_ID:-}" ]; then
    curl -sS -X POST "https://api.telegram.org/bot${TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN}/sendMessage" \
      -d chat_id="${CHAT_ID}" -d text="$msg
ACTION: restart scalp-router.service" >/dev/null || true
  fi
else
  if [ -n "${TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN:-}" ] && [ -n "${CHAT_ID:-}" ]; then
    curl -sS -X POST "https://api.telegram.org/bot${TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN}/sendMessage" \
      -d chat_id="${CHAT_ID}" -d text="$msg" >/dev/null || true
  fi
fi

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="${ADB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"
for T in 5m 15m 30m; do
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
WITH cut AS (
  SELECT symbol,
         (SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_${T} t2 WHERE t2.symbol=t.symbol ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1 OFFSET 99) AS ts_cut
  FROM ohlcv_${T} t GROUP BY symbol
)
DELETE FROM ohlcv_${T}
WHERE ts < (SELECT ts_cut FROM cut WHERE cut.symbol=ohlcv_${T}.symbol AND ts_cut IS NOT NULL);
SQL
done

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

fail(){ echo "FAIL: $*" >&2; exit 1; }

# 0) durcir pour éviter les courses
/opt/scalp/project/scripts/harden_o_db.sh >/dev/null 2>&1 || true

# 1) couverture = 35
cov=$(sqlite3 -noheader "$ADB" "
SELECT '5m|'||COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_5m
UNION ALL SELECT '15m|'||COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_15m
UNION ALL SELECT '30m|'||COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_30m;")
echo "$cov" | awk -F'|' '{printf "%s|sy=%s\n",$1,$2}'
echo "$cov" | awk -F'|' '$2!=35 {bad=1} END{exit bad}' || fail "coverage sy!=35"

# 2) gaps = 0
gaps=$(sqlite3 -noheader -separator '|' "$ADB" "
WITH tf(name,step) AS (VALUES('ohlcv_5m',300),('ohlcv_15m',900),('ohlcv_30m',1800)),
rows AS (
  SELECT 'ohlcv_5m' name,300 step,symbol,COUNT(*) n,MIN(ts) t0,MAX(ts) t1 FROM ohlcv_5m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_15m',900,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_30m',1800,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m GROUP BY symbol
),
g AS (SELECT name, MAX(0, ((t1-t0)/step + 1 - n)) AS miss FROM rows)
SELECT name, SUM(miss) FROM g GROUP BY name;")
echo "$gaps" | awk -F'|' '{printf "%s|gaps=%s\n",$1,$2}'
echo "$gaps" | awk -F'|' '$2!=0 {bad=1} END{exit bad}' || fail "gaps!=0"

# 3) exactement 100 par symbole
for t in 5m 15m 30m; do
  sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM ohlcv_${t} GROUP BY symbol HAVING COUNT(*)!=100);" | grep -qx 0 \
    || fail "rows!=100 $t"
done

# 4) ensemble = univers courant
sqlite3 -noheader -separator '|' "$ADB" "
ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
WITH cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol),
     uni AS (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)
SELECT (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM uni)),
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM uni EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur));
DETACH DATABASE udb;" | grep -qx "0|0" || fail "set mismatch vs universe"

# 5) fraîcheur par palier: 5m libre, 15m=floor(5m,900), 30m=floor(5m,1800)
mx=$(sqlite3 -noheader -separator '|' "$ADB" "
SELECT (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_5m),
       (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m),
       (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m);")
echo "max_ts 5m|15m|30m: $mx"
awk -F'|' '{
  t5=$1; t15=$2; t30=$3;
  a15 = int(t5/900)*900;
  a30 = int(t5/1800)*1800;
  ok = (t5%300==0) && (t15==a15) && (t30==a30);
  exit(ok?0:1)
}' <<< "$mx" || fail "freshness/alignment"

echo "OK: o.db health strict"
