#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, os
UDB=os.getenv("UDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db")
ADB=os.getenv("ADB","/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
FIXED=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","BNBUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT"]
def get_top():
    con=sqlite3.connect(UDB)
    try:
        ts=con.execute("SELECT MAX(ts) FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30'").fetchone()[0]
        if ts:
            # pas de 'rank' → trie par 'score' décroissant si présent, sinon symbol
            cols=[r[1] for r in con.execute("PRAGMA table_info(top_scores)")]
            order="score DESC" if "score" in cols else "symbol ASC"
            q=f"SELECT symbol FROM top_scores WHERE name='TOP30' AND ts=? ORDER BY {order} LIMIT 30"
            base=[r[0] for r in con.execute(q,(ts,)).fetchall()]
        else:
            base=[]
    finally:
        con.close()
    out=[]; seen=set()
    for s in base+FIXED:
        if s not in seen:
            out.append(s); seen.add(s)
        if len(out)>=35: break
    return out
def save(syms):
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS u_syms(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY)")
    con.execute("DELETE FROM u_syms")
    con.executemany("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO u_syms(symbol) VALUES(?)", [(s,) for s in syms])
    con.close()
if __name__=="__main__":
    syms=get_top()
    save(syms)
    print("u_syms:",len(syms))
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="${ROOT:-/opt/scalp/project}"
BIN="$ROOT/bin"
DB="${DB:-$ROOT/data/u.db}"
VER="${VER:?specify VER}"

echo "== FINAL MARK =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$DB" "SELECT version, run_id, count, created_at FROM final_marks WHERE version='$VER';"

echo "== CODE HASHES =="
sqlite3 -csv "$DB" "SELECT file, sha256 FROM code_release WHERE version='$VER' ORDER BY file" | \
while IFS=, read -r file ref; do
  cur=$(sha256sum "$BIN/$file" | awk '{print $1}')
  [ "$ref" = "$cur" ] && match=yes || match=NO
  echo "$file expected=$ref current=$cur match=$match"
done

echo "== PUBLISHED POINTER =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$DB" "
WITH last AS (
  SELECT run_id, finished_at, count
  FROM universe_runs WHERE status='published'
  ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1
)
SELECT 'published_run_id', run_id FROM last
UNION ALL SELECT 'published_count', count FROM last
UNION ALL SELECT 'available_now', (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_universe_current);
"

echo "== SET EQUALITY vs FINAL SNAPSHOT =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$DB" "
WITH final AS (SELECT run_id FROM final_marks WHERE version='$VER'),
cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM v_universe_current),
snap AS (SELECT s.symbol FROM universe_snapshots s, final f WHERE s.run_id=f.run_id)
SELECT 'missing_from_current',
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM snap EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur))
UNION ALL
SELECT 'extra_in_current',
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM snap));
"

echo "-- diff symbols (current - final):"
sqlite3 -noheader "$DB" "
WITH final AS (SELECT run_id FROM final_marks WHERE version='$VER'),
cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM v_universe_current),
snap AS (SELECT s.symbol FROM universe_snapshots s, final f WHERE s.run_id=f.run_id)
SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM snap;
"
echo "-- diff symbols (final - current):"
sqlite3 -noheader "$DB" "
WITH final AS (SELECT run_id FROM final_marks WHERE version='$VER'),
cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM v_universe_current),
snap AS (SELECT s.symbol FROM universe_snapshots s, final f WHERE s.run_id=f.run_id)
SELECT symbol FROM snap EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur;
"

Path: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/ws_ticks_writer_v2.py
Size: 5247
MTime: 2025-10-10 11:05:56.308425655 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, sqlite3, time, ssl, signal, sys
from urllib.request import urlopen, Request
from urllib.parse import urlencode
import websockets

UDB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
TDB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
REST = "https://api.bitget.com/api/v2/mix/market/contracts"
PRODUCT = "USDT-FUTURES"
REFRESH_SEC = 300
KEEP_MIN = 15
CAP_PER_SYM = 5000
BATCH = 5
PAUSE = 0.2  # s entre paquets

def now_ms(): return int(time.time()*1000)

def http_get(url, params):
    q = url + "?" + urlencode(params)
    r = urlopen(Request(q, headers={"User-Agent":"ws-ticks"}), timeout=10)
    return json.loads(r.read().decode())

def get_universe():
    con = sqlite3.connect(UDB)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT symbol FROM v_universe_current LIMIT 35;")
    syms = [r[0].upper() for r in cur.fetchall()]
    con.close()
    return syms

def valid_usdt_futures_set():
    # REST renvoie la liste des contrats. On garde instId (v2 = BTCUSDT pour USDT-FUTURES).
    data = http_get(REST, {"productType": PRODUCT})
    insts = data.get("data", [])
    return { (it.get("instId") or it.get("symbol") or "").upper() for it in insts }

def write_rows(rows):
    if not rows: return
    con = sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None, timeout=10)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.executemany(
        "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks(symbol,instId,tradeId,ts_ms,price,size,side) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
        rows
    )
    cut = now_ms() - KEEP_MIN*60*1000
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM ticks WHERE ts_ms < ?", (cut,))
    con.commit(); con.close()
    # cap par symbole
    syms = {r[0] for r in rows}
    con = sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None, timeout=10)
    cur = con.cursor()
    for s in syms:
        cur.execute("""DELETE FROM ticks
                       WHERE symbol=? AND rowid NOT IN
                         (SELECT rowid FROM ticks WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY ts_ms DESC LIMIT ?)""",
                    (s, s, CAP_PER_SYM))
    con.commit(); con.close()

def build_args(instids):  # channel=trade, instId = "BTCUSDT"
    return [{"instType":PRODUCT, "channel":"trade", "instId":i} for i in instids]

def parse_msg(obj):
    out = []
    if not isinstance(obj, dict): return out
    if obj.get("action") not in ("snapshot","update"): return out
    arg = obj.get("arg") or {}
    instId = (arg.get("instId") or "").upper()
    sym = instId
    for d in obj.get("data", []):
        try:
            tradeId = str(d.get("tradeId") or "")
            if not tradeId: continue
            ts = int(d.get("ts") or now_ms())
            price = float(d.get("price"))
            size  = float(d.get("size"))
            side  = str(d.get("side") or "")
            out.append((sym, instId, tradeId, ts, price, size, side))
        except Exception:
            continue
    return out

async def send_batched(ws, op, args):
    # envoie par lots de BATCH avec pause courte
    for i in range(0, len(args), BATCH):
        payload = {"op": op, "args": args[i:i+BATCH]}
        await ws.send(json.dumps(payload))
        await asyncio.sleep(PAUSE)

async def run_ws():
    ssl_ctx = ssl.create_default_context()
    subs = set()
    last_refresh = 0
    valid = valid_usdt_futures_set()  # set d'instId valides côté Bitget
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, ssl=ssl_ctx, max_size=2**22) as ws:
                while True:
                    t = time.time()
                    if t - last_refresh > REFRESH_SEC or not subs:
                        want_syms = set(get_universe())
                        want = sorted(list(want_syms & valid))  # filtre aux seuls contrats existants
                        add = [i for i in want if i not in subs]
                        rem = [i for i in list(subs) if i not in want]
                        if rem:
                            await send_batched(ws, "unsubscribe", build_args(rem))
                        if add:
                            await send_batched(ws, "subscribe", build_args(add))
                        subs = set(want)
                        last_refresh = t
                        print("T: subs", len(subs), sorted(list(subs))[:10], flush=True)
                    try:
                        raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=5.0)
                    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                        continue
                    try:
                        obj = json.loads(raw)
                    except Exception:
                        continue
                    if "event" in obj:  # logs 'subscribe' / 'error'
                        print("T evt:", obj, flush=True)
                        continue
                    rows = parse_msg(obj)
                    if rows: write_rows(rows)
        except Exception as e:
            print("T ws error:", e, "→ reconnect in 3s", file=sys.stderr)
            await asyncio.sleep(3)

def main():
    loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
    for sig in (signal.SIGINT, signal.SIGTERM):
        try: loop.add_signal_handler(sig, loop.stop)
        except NotImplementedError: pass
    loop.run_until_complete(run_ws())

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

# assure table + colonne src
sqlite3 "$UDB" "PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000; CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS universe_current(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, updated_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')));"
has_src=$(sqlite3 "$UDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pragma_table_info('universe_current') WHERE name='src';")
if [ "$has_src" != "1" ]; then
  sqlite3 "$UDB" "ALTER TABLE universe_current ADD COLUMN src TEXT;"
fi

# rebuild depuis a.db
sqlite3 "$UDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
DELETE FROM universe_current;
INSERT INTO universe_current(symbol, src, updated_at)
SELECT symbol, 'a15', datetime('now')
FROM (
  SELECT DISTINCT symbol
  FROM adb.ohlcv_15m
  WHERE symbol IS NOT NULL
  ORDER BY symbol
  LIMIT 35
);
COMMIT;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_universe_current;
CREATE VIEW v_universe_current AS
SELECT symbol FROM universe_current ORDER BY symbol;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
SQL
echo "Universe OK"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

retry(){ n=0; until sqlite3 -noheader "$ADB" "$1"; do n=$((n+1)); [ $n -ge 5 ] && return 1; sleep 1; done }

# 1) 35 symboles et ensemble identique à l’univers
q1=$"ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
WITH cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM a_context_state),
     uni AS (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)
SELECT (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM cur)||'|'||
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM uni))||'|'||
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM uni EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur));
DETACH DATABASE udb;"
out=$(retry "$q1") || { echo "FAIL: locked"; exit 1; }
echo "$out" | awk -F'|' '{if($1!=35||$2!=0||$3!=0){print "FAIL: set/count"; exit 1}else{print "OK set/count"}}'

# 2) Probas cohérentes (somme≈1)
q2=$"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM a_context_state WHERE pb<0 OR ph<0 OR ps<0 OR ABS(pb+ph+ps-1)>0.001;"
bad=$(retry "$q2") || { echo "FAIL: locked"; exit 1; }
[ "$bad" = "0" ] || { echo "FAIL: probs invalid"; exit 1; }

# 3) Scores dans bornes larges
q3=$"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM a_context_state WHERE s IS NULL OR s<-20 OR s>20;"
bad=$(retry "$q3") || { echo "FAIL: locked"; exit 1; }
[ "$bad" = "0" ] || { echo "FAIL: scores out-of-range"; exit 1; }

echo "OK: a.db health strict"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

sqlite3 "$BDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_params(
  key TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  value TEXT NOT NULL
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO b_params(key,value) VALUES
  ('min_score_buy','60'),           -- seuil BUY sur score normalisé A
  ('max_score_sell','40'),          -- seuil SELL
  ('lookback_sec','180'),           -- fenêtre ticks pour volat
  ('min_sl_pct','0.25'),            -- SL min %
  ('rr','1.40'),                    -- risk:reward
  ('size_usd_base','50'),           -- taille nominale
  ('size_scale','1.50');            -- amplification selon score

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_plans(
  ts_utc  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  symbol  TEXT NOT NULL,
  side    TEXT NOT NULL,            -- BUY | SELL
  score   REAL NOT NULL,            -- 0..100
  price   REAL NOT NULL,            -- last
  sl      REAL NOT NULL,            -- stop
  tp      REAL NOT NULL,            -- take
  size_usd REAL NOT NULL,           -- taille
  vol_win REAL NOT NULL,            -- (max-min)/last sur fenêtre
  src     TEXT NOT NULL,            -- 'ticks'
  PRIMARY KEY(ts_utc, symbol)
);

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_b_latest;
CREATE VIEW v_b_latest AS
SELECT *
FROM (
  SELECT *, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts_utc DESC) rn
  FROM b_plans
) WHERE rn=1;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_b_exec;
CREATE VIEW v_b_exec AS
WITH last_ts AS (SELECT MAX(ts_utc) t FROM b_plans)
SELECT symbol, side, score, price, sl, tp, size_usd, ts_utc
FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT t FROM last_ts)
ORDER BY score DESC;

SQL

echo "B: schema ready."

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
LOCK="/opt/scalp/locks/a.db.lock"
echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] purge ohlcv..."

SQL=$(cat <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=60000;

-- 5m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m
WHERE (symbol,ts) NOT IN (
  SELECT symbol, ts FROM (
    SELECT symbol, ts,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_5m
  ) t WHERE rn <= 100
);

-- 15m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_15m
WHERE (symbol,ts) NOT IN (
  SELECT symbol, ts FROM (
    SELECT symbol, ts,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_15m
  ) t WHERE rn <= 100
);

-- 30m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_30m
WHERE (symbol,ts) NOT IN (
  SELECT symbol, ts FROM (
    SELECT symbol, ts,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_30m
  ) t WHERE rn <= 100
);

VACUUM;
SQL
)

/usr/bin/flock -w 120 "$LOCK" /usr/bin/sqlite3 "$DB" "$SQL"
echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] purge terminée."

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"

# Récupère les derniers symboles vus dans top_scores et crée des métriques par défaut si manquantes.
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;

WITH latest AS (
  SELECT s.name, s.ts
  FROM top_scores s
  JOIN (SELECT name, MAX(ts) ts FROM top_scores GROUP BY name) m
    ON m.name=s.name AND m.ts=s.ts
  ORDER BY s.ts DESC
  LIMIT 1
)
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO metrics_universe(symbol, vol_usdt_24h, price, spread_bps, active)
SELECT s.symbol,
       20000000.0 AS vol_usdt_24h, 1.0 AS price, 10.0 AS spread_bps, 1 AS active
FROM top_scores s
JOIN latest l ON l.name=s.name AND l.ts=s.ts;
SQL

echo "metrics_universe backfilled for symbols present in the freshest top_scores snapshot."

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

sqlite3 "$UDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS universe_current(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  updated_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);

DELETE FROM universe_current;
INSERT INTO universe_current(symbol)
SELECT symbol
FROM (
  SELECT symbol
  FROM adb.ohlcv_15m
  GROUP BY symbol
  ORDER BY symbol
  LIMIT 35
);

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_universe_current;
CREATE VIEW v_universe_current AS
SELECT symbol FROM universe_current ORDER BY symbol;

COMMIT;

SQL

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
SRC=/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db
TMP=/opt/scalp/project/data/t_tmp.db
BAK=/opt/scalp/project/data/t.bak.$(date +%s)
cp -f "$SRC" "$TMP"

sqlite3 "$TMP" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=DELETE;
PRAGMA synchronous=OFF;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks_retention(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK(id=1),
  keep_secs INTEGER,
  keep_rows INTEGER
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ticks_retention(id,keep_secs,keep_rows)
  VALUES(1,900,2000);
SQL

NOW=$(date +%s)
sqlite3 "$TMP" "DELETE FROM ticks WHERE ts < $NOW - (SELECT keep_secs FROM ticks_retention WHERE id=1);"

# cap par symbole sans fenêtre
sqlite3 -newline $'\n' -list "$TMP" "SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM ticks;" | while read -r sym; do
  [ -z "$sym" ] && continue
  keep=$(sqlite3 "$TMP" "SELECT keep_rows FROM ticks_retention WHERE id=1;")
  sqlite3 "$TMP" "
    DELETE FROM ticks
    WHERE symbol='$sym'
      AND rowid NOT IN (
        SELECT rowid FROM ticks
        WHERE symbol='$sym'
        ORDER BY ts DESC
        LIMIT $keep
      );
  "
done

sqlite3 "$TMP" 'VACUUM;'
mv "$SRC" "$BAK"
mv "$TMP" "$SRC"
echo "[clean_ticks_safe] done at $(date)"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db

cap_tf() {
  local tbl=$1 tf=$2
  local keep
  keep=$(sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT keep_rows FROM retention_cfg WHERE tf='$tf';")
  [ -z "$keep" ] && keep=1000
  # liste symboles présents
  sqlite3 -newline $'\n' -list "$ADB" "SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM $tbl;" | while read -r sym; do
    [ -z "$sym" ] && continue
    sqlite3 "$ADB" "
      DELETE FROM $tbl
      WHERE symbol='$sym'
        AND rowid NOT IN (
          SELECT rowid FROM $tbl
          WHERE symbol='$sym'
          ORDER BY ts DESC
          LIMIT $keep
        );
    "
  done
}

cap_tf ohlcv_1m  1m
cap_tf ohlcv_5m  5m
cap_tf ohlcv_15m 15m
cap_tf ohlcv_30m 30m

sqlite3 "$ADB" 'VACUUM;'
echo "[compact_ohlcv_keepN] done"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, sqlite3, time, sys

ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
BATCH=5
RUN_SECS=25
ACK_WAIT=5

def dec(b):
    if isinstance(b,(bytes,bytearray)):
        try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
        except: 
            try: return b.decode()
            except: return ""
    return b

def load_syms():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    cur=con.cursor()
    has = cur.execute("SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='u_syms_futures'").fetchone()
    table = "u_syms_futures" if has else "u_syms"
    rows = cur.execute(f"SELECT symbol FROM {table} ORDER BY symbol").fetchall()
    con.close()
    syms = [r[0] for r in rows if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT")]
    return syms[:35], table

async def sub_chunk(ws, chunk):
    args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in chunk]
    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))
    acks=set(); sample=None
    t0=time.time()
    while time.time()-t0<ACK_WAIT and len(acks)<len(chunk):
        try:
            raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=ACK_WAIT)
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            break
        msg=dec(raw)
        try:
            obj=json.loads(msg)
        except:
            continue
        if obj.get("event")=="subscribe":
            inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
            if inst in chunk: acks.add(inst)
        elif obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
            inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
            if inst in chunk:
                acks.add(inst)
                if not sample:
                    d=(obj.get("data") or [{}])[0]
                    sample=f"{inst} lastPr={d.get('lastPr') or d.get('last')} ts={d.get('ts')}"
    missing=[s for s in chunk if s not in acks]
    return acks, sample, missing

async def main():
    syms, src = load_syms()
    if not syms:
        print("Liste vide:", src); return
    print(f"Source={src}  count={len(syms)}")
    print("Souscription par paquets de", BATCH)
    counts={s:0 for s in syms}
    samples=[]

    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        # souscriptions
        for i in range(0,len(syms),BATCH):
            chunk=syms[i:i+BATCH]
            acks, sample, missing = await sub_chunk(ws, chunk)
            print("ACK", len(acks), "/", len(chunk), "missing:", missing)
            if sample: samples.append(sample)
            await asyncio.sleep(0.2)

        # lecture
        t0=time.time(); last_print=0
        while time.time()-t0 < RUN_SECS:
            try:
                raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=3)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"}))
                continue
            msg=dec(raw)
            try:
                obj=json.loads(msg)
            except:
                continue
            if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
                inst=(obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
                if inst in counts:
                    counts[inst]+=1
            # petit statut périodique
            if time.time()-last_print>5:
                got=sum(1 for v in counts.values() if v>0)
                total=sum(counts.values())
                print(f"[{int(time.time()-t0)}s] syms_ok={got}/{len(syms)} msgs={total}")
                last_print=time.time()

    total=sum(counts.values())
    ok=sorted([(k,v) for k,v in counts.items() if v>0], key=lambda x:-x[1])
    miss=[k for k,v in counts.items() if v==0]
    print("\n=== RÉSUMÉ ===")
    print("messages_total:", total, " | symbols_ok:", len(ok))
    for s in samples[:5]:
        print("sample:", s)
    for k,v in ok[:10]:
        print(f"{k}: {v} msgs")
    if miss:
        print("aucun flux pour:", ", ".join(miss))
if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, sqlite3, time

ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
RUN_SECS=20
BATCH=20  # taille d'un paquet d'abonnement

def load_syms():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    try:
        rows=con.execute("SELECT symbol FROM u_syms ORDER BY symbol").fetchall()
        syms=[r[0] for r in rows]
    finally:
        con.close()
    # garde au plus 35
    return [s for s in syms if isinstance(s,str) and s.endswith("USDT")][:35]

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except Exception:
        try: return b.decode()
        except Exception: return ""

async def subscribe(ws, syms):
    # en paquets pour éviter les rejets
    for i in range(0, len(syms), BATCH):
        args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in syms[i:i+BATCH]]
        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))

async def main():
    syms=load_syms()
    if not syms:
        print("Aucun symbole dans a.db.u_syms"); return
    print(f"TOP35={len(syms)} ->", syms)

    counts={s:0 for s in syms}
    errors=[]
    start=time.time()
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        await subscribe(ws, syms)
        while time.time()-start < RUN_SECS:
            try:
                raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=3)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"}))
                continue
            msg=ungzip(raw)
            try:
                obj=json.loads(msg)
            except Exception:
                continue
            if obj.get("event")=="error":
                errors.append(obj); continue
            if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
                inst = (obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
                if inst in counts: counts[inst]+=1

    # Résumé
    got    = sorted([(k,v) for k,v in counts.items() if v>0], key=lambda x:-x[1])
    noluck = [k for k,v in counts.items() if v==0]
    print("\n=== RESUME ===")
    print("messages_total =", sum(counts.values()))
    print("symbols_ok     =", len(got))
    for k,v in got[:10]:
        print(f"{k}: {v} msgs")
    if noluck:
        print("\nAucun message pour:", ", ".join(noluck))
    if errors:
        print("\nErrors:")
        for e in errors[:5]:
            print(e)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

----- CONTENT -----
import asyncio, sqlite3, time, os

ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
TDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

REFRESH_SEC=30  # fréquence (toutes les 30 s)

SQL_REFRESH = """
ATTACH '{ADB}' AS A;
ATTACH '{TDB}' AS T;
DELETE FROM ctx_latest;
INSERT INTO ctx_latest(symbol,ctx,score,ts)
SELECT symbol,ctx,
       CASE WHEN ctx='buy' THEN pb WHEN ctx='sell' THEN ps ELSE ph END,
       ts
FROM A.v_contexts_A_latest
WHERE ctx IN ('buy','sell');

DELETE FROM ticks_latest;
INSERT INTO ticks_latest(symbol,ts,price,bid,ask)
SELECT t.symbol,t.ts,t.price,t.bid,t.ask
FROM T.ticks t
JOIN (SELECT symbol,MAX(ts) mts FROM T.ticks GROUP BY symbol) m
  ON m.symbol=t.symbol AND m.mts=t.ts;

DELETE FROM signals_B_plan;

WITH P AS (
  SELECT
    (SELECT val FROM params WHERE key='base_notional_usdt') AS base_notional,
    (SELECT val FROM params WHERE key='risk_step_pct')       AS step
),
J AS (
  SELECT c.symbol,c.ctx,c.score,c.ts,tl.price,
         CASE WHEN c.ctx='buy' THEN 'long' ELSE 'short' END AS side
  FROM ctx_latest c JOIN ticks_latest tl USING(symbol)
),
S AS (
  SELECT j.*,p.base_notional,p.step,
         CASE WHEN j.score>=40 THEN 5 WHEN j.score>=30 THEN 4
              WHEN j.score>=20 THEN 3 WHEN j.score>=10 THEN 2 ELSE 1 END AS lev,
         (p.base_notional*(j.score/50.0)) AS notional
  FROM J j CROSS JOIN P p
)
INSERT INTO signals_B_plan(symbol,side,ctx,score,ts,entry,lev,qty,notional,sl,tp1,tp2,tp3)
SELECT s.symbol,s.side,s.ctx,ROUND(s.score,2),s.ts,s.price,
       s.lev,
       ROUND(CASE WHEN s.price>0 THEN s.notional/s.price ELSE 0 END,6),
       ROUND(s.notional,2),
       CASE WHEN s.side='long' THEN ROUND(s.price*(1-s.step),6)
            ELSE ROUND(s.price*(1+s.step),6) END,
       CASE WHEN s.side='long' THEN ROUND(s.price*(1+s.step),6)
            ELSE ROUND(s.price*(1-s.step),6) END,
       CASE WHEN s.side='long' THEN ROUND(s.price*(1+2*s.step),6)
            ELSE ROUND(s.price*(1-2*s.step),6) END,
       CASE WHEN s.side='long' THEN ROUND(s.price*(1+3*s.step),6)
            ELSE ROUND(s.price*(1-3*s.step),6) END
FROM S s;
DETACH A; DETACH T;
""".replace("{ADB}",ADB).replace("{TDB}",TDB)

async def loop():
    while True:
        try:
            con=sqlite3.connect(BDB, isolation_level=None)
            con.executescript(SQL_REFRESH)
            con.close()
            print(time.strftime("%H:%M:%S"),"B refresh OK")
        except Exception as e:
            print("B refresh ERR",e)
        await asyncio.sleep(REFRESH_SEC)

asyncio.run(loop())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, time, sqlite3

ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
TDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
BATCH=5
RUN_SECS=30

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except Exception:
        try: return b.decode()
        except Exception: return ""

def load_syms():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    cur=con.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='u_syms_futures'")
    has = cur.fetchone() is not None
    rows = cur.execute(f"SELECT symbol FROM {'u_syms_futures' if has else 'u_syms'}").fetchall()
    con.close()
    syms=[r[0] for r in rows if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT")]
    return syms[:35]

def tdb_init():
    con=sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
        symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, bid REAL, ask REAL,
        PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts))""")
    con.execute("""CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_ticks_latest AS
        SELECT t.* FROM ticks t
        JOIN (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) mts FROM ticks GROUP BY symbol) m
          ON m.symbol=t.symbol AND m.mts=t.ts""")
    con.close()

def parse_books5(obj):
    if obj.get("action") not in ("snapshot","update"): return []
    a=obj.get("arg",{})
    if a.get("instType")!="USDT-FUTURES" or a.get("channel")!="books5": return []
    inst=a.get("instId")
    rows=[]
    for d in obj.get("data",[]):
        bids=d.get("bids") or []; asks=d.get("asks") or []
        if not bids or not asks: continue
        bid=float(bids[0][0]); ask=float(asks[0][0]); mid=(bid+ask)/2.0
        ts=int(float(d.get("ts", time.time()*1000))/1000)
        rows.append((inst,ts,mid,bid,ask))
    return rows

def write(rows):
    if not rows: return
    con=sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.executemany("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,bid,ask) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.close()

async def subscribe(ws, syms):
    for i in range(0,len(syms),BATCH):
        chunk=syms[i:i+BATCH]
        args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"books5","instId":s} for s in chunk]
        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))
        await asyncio.sleep(0.2)

async def main():
    syms=load_syms()
    if not syms: print("liste vide"); return
    print("FUTURES syms:", len(syms), syms, flush=True)
    tdb_init()
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        await subscribe(ws, syms)
        t0=time.time(); n=0
        while time.time()-t0<RUN_SECS:
            try: raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(),timeout=5)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"})); continue
            msg=ungzip(raw)
            try: obj=json.loads(msg)
            except Exception: continue
            rows=parse_books5(obj)
            if rows:
                write(rows); n+=len(rows)
        print("rows_written:", n)
if __name__=="__main__": asyncio.run(main())

import asyncio, json, gzip, sqlite3, time, websockets, os

BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
XDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db"
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
PING=20
STEP=0.005  # 0.5 %

def now(): return int(time.time())

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except: return b.decode()

def ensure_schema():
    con=sqlite3.connect(XDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS account_sim(
      ts INTEGER,
      balance REAL DEFAULT 10000,
      equity REAL,
      PRIMARY KEY(ts)
    )""")
    con.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS positions_sim(
      symbol TEXT,
      side TEXT,
      entry REAL,
      qty REAL,
      lev INTEGER,
      sl REAL,
      sl_dyn REAL,
      tp1 REAL,
      tp2 REAL,
      tp3 REAL,
      ts_open INTEGER,
      ts_close INTEGER,
      status TEXT,
      pnl REAL DEFAULT 0,
      PRIMARY KEY(symbol, ts_open)
    )""")
    con.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_pos_status ON positions_sim(status)")
    con.close()

def load_signals(limit=10):
    con=sqlite3.connect(BDB)
    rows=con.execute("""
        SELECT symbol,side,entry,sl,tp1,tp2,tp3,lev,qty
        FROM v_signals_B_live
        ORDER BY score DESC LIMIT ?""",(limit,)).fetchall()
    con.close()
    return [dict(symbol=r[0],side=r[1],entry=r[2],sl=r[3],
                 tp1=r[4],tp2=r[5],tp3=r[6],lev=r[7],qty=r[8]) for r in rows]

def record_open(sig):
    con=sqlite3.connect(XDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("""INSERT OR IGNORE INTO positions_sim
      (symbol,side,entry,qty,lev,sl,sl_dyn,tp1,tp2,tp3,ts_open,status)
      VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)""",
      (sig['symbol'],sig['side'],sig['entry'],sig['qty'],sig['lev'],
       sig['sl'],sig['sl'],sig['tp1'],sig['tp2'],sig['tp3'],now(),'open'))
    con.close()

def open_positions():
    con=sqlite3.connect(XDB)
    rows=con.execute("""
      SELECT symbol,side,entry,qty,lev,sl,sl_dyn,tp1,tp2,tp3
      FROM positions_sim WHERE status='open'""").fetchall()
    con.close()
    out=[]
    for r in rows:
        out.append(dict(symbol=r[0],side=r[1],entry=r[2],qty=r[3],lev=r[4],
                        sl=r[5],sl_dyn=r[6] or r[5],tp1=r[7],tp2=r[8],tp3=r[9]))
    return out

def update_sl(sym,new_sl):
    con=sqlite3.connect(XDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("UPDATE positions_sim SET sl_dyn=? WHERE symbol=? AND status='open'",
                (new_sl, sym))
    con.close()

def close_position(sym,pnl):
    con=sqlite3.connect(XDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("UPDATE positions_sim SET status='closed', ts_close=?, pnl=? WHERE symbol=? AND status='open'",
                (now(), pnl, sym))
    con.close()
    update_equity()

def update_equity():
    con=sqlite3.connect(XDB, isolation_level=None)
    bal=con.execute("SELECT IFNULL(MAX(balance),10000) FROM account_sim").fetchone()[0]
    pnl=con.execute("SELECT SUM(pnl) FROM positions_sim WHERE status='closed'").fetchone()[0] or 0
    con.execute("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO account_sim(ts,balance,equity) VALUES(?,?,?)",(now(),bal,bal+pnl))
    con.close()

async def run():
    ensure_schema()
    sigs=load_signals(10)
    for s in sigs: record_open(s)
    syms=[s['symbol'] for s in sigs]
    subs=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in syms]
    async with websockets.connect(URI,ping_interval=None,max_size=2**22) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":subs}))
        print("Subscribed:",syms)
        last_ping=time.time()
        while True:
            if time.time()-last_ping>PING:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"}))
                last_ping=time.time()
            raw=await ws.recv()
            msg=ungzip(raw) if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)) else raw
            try: data=json.loads(msg)
            except: continue
            if data.get("action") not in ("snapshot","update"): continue
            for d in data.get("data",[]):
                sym=d["instId"]; px=float(d["lastPr"])
                for p in open_positions():
                    if p['symbol']!=sym: continue
                    if p['side']=="long" and px>p['entry']:
                        new_sl=max(p['sl_dyn'],px*(1-STEP))
                        if new_sl>p['sl_dyn']: update_sl(sym,new_sl)
                    elif p['side']=="short" and px<p['entry']:
                        new_sl=min(p['sl_dyn'],px*(1+STEP))
                        if new_sl<p['sl_dyn']: update_sl(sym,new_sl)
                    if p['side']=="long":
                        if px<=p['sl_dyn']:
                            pnl=(px-p['entry'])*p['qty']*p['lev']; print("SL hit",sym,pnl); close_position(sym,pnl)
                        elif px>=p['tp3']:
                            pnl=(p['tp3']-p['entry'])*p['qty']*p['lev']; print("TP3",sym,pnl); close_position(sym,pnl)
                    else:
                        if px>=p['sl_dyn']:
                            pnl=(p['entry']-px)*p['qty']*p['lev']; print("SL hit",sym,pnl); close_position(sym,pnl)
                        elif px<=p['tp3']:
                            pnl=(p['entry']-p['tp3'])*p['qty']*p['lev']; print("TP3",sym,pnl); close_position(sym,pnl)
            update_equity()

asyncio.run(run())
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
BIN="/opt/scalp/project/bin"
MAN="/opt/scalp/project/etc/b.manifest"
[ -r "$MAN" ] || { echo "absent: $MAN"; exit 2; }
# filtrer les fichiers manquants et mismatches
BAD=0
while IFS= read -r line; do
  sum="$(echo "$line" | awk '{print $1}')"
  file="$(echo "$line" | awk '{print $2}')"
  # compat chemin absolu/relatif
  base="$(basename "$file")"
  path="$BIN/$base"
  if [ ! -f "$path" ]; then
    echo "missing: $base"; BAD=1; continue
  fi
  cur="$(sha256sum "$path" | awk '{print $1}')"
  [ "$cur" = "$sum" ] || { echo "mismatch: $base"; BAD=1; }
done < "$MAN"
[ $BAD -eq 0 ] && { echo "integrity: ok"; exit 0; } || { echo "integrity: FAIL"; exit 1; }
----- FILE END -----

Path: /opt/scalp/project/bin/analyse_B_sql.sh
Size: 6557
MTime: 2025-10-10 14:15:05.343972736 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db}"
MIN_SCORE="${MIN_SCORE:-0.0}"
PLAN_MAX_AGE="${PLAN_MAX_AGE:-1800}"
COOLDOWN_SEC="${COOLDOWN_SEC:-300}"
MAX_CONSEC="${MAX_CONSEC:-3}"
REQUIRE_TREND="${REQUIRE_TREND:-1}"
ATR_PCT_1M_MIN="${ATR_PCT_1M_MIN:-0.10}"
ATR_SL="${ATR_SL:-1.2}"
ATR_TP="${ATR_TP:-1.8}"
PB_TOL_ATR_MULT="${PB_TOL_ATR_MULT:-0.15}"
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000; PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_plan(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
 symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, score REAL, side TEXT,
 entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL, qty REAL, margin REAL, notional REAL, created_ts INTEGER);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
 symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sigB_ts ON signals_B(created_ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sigB_sym_ts ON signals_B(symbol,created_ts);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_state(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, last_side TEXT, consec INTEGER, last_ts INTEGER);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _params;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _params AS
SELECT $MIN_SCORE AS min_score,$PLAN_MAX_AGE AS plan_age,$COOLDOWN_SEC AS cooldown,
       $MAX_CONSEC AS max_consec,$REQUIRE_TREND AS require_trend,$ATR_PCT_1M_MIN AS atr_min_pct,
       $ATR_SL AS k_sl,$ATR_TP AS k_tp,$PB_TOL_ATR_MULT AS pb_tol;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _m1;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _m1 AS
SELECT i.*, f.vwap20,f.bb_mid20,f.bb_up20,f.bb_dn20,f.macd,f.macd_signal9,f.macd_hist,f.obv
FROM v_indic_1m i
LEFT JOIN v_feat_1m f ON f.symbol=i.symbol AND f.ts=i.ts
WHERE (i.symbol,i.ts) IN (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) FROM v_indic_1m GROUP BY symbol);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _trend5;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _trend5 AS
SELECT symbol, CASE WHEN sma9>sma21 THEN 'BUY' ELSE 'SELL' END AS fast_side FROM v_indic5m_fast;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _ctx;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _ctx AS
SELECT symbol, ctx, pb, ph, ps, ts AS ctx_ts FROM v_contexts_A_latest;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _plans;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _plans AS
SELECT p.* FROM signals_B_plan p, _params pr
WHERE p.score >= pr.min_score AND p.created_ts >= strftime('%s','now')-pr.plan_age;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _cand_plan_ok;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _cand_plan_ok AS
SELECT p.symbol,p.side,p.entry,p.sl,p.tp,p.ctx AS reason,p.created_ts,
       m.ts AS bar_ts,m.atr_pct,m.atr14,m.close,m.sma21,
       c.ctx AS a_ctx,c.pb,c.ps, t.fast_side,(SELECT require_trend FROM _params) AS require_trend
FROM _plans p
JOIN _m1 m ON m.symbol=p.symbol
LEFT JOIN _ctx c ON c.symbol=p.symbol
LEFT JOIN _trend5 t ON t.symbol=p.symbol
WHERE m.atr_pct >= (SELECT atr_min_pct FROM _params)
  AND (c.symbol IS NULL OR (p.side='BUY' AND c.pb>=0.60) OR (p.side='SELL' AND c.ps>=0.60))
  AND ((SELECT require_trend FROM _params)=0 OR t.fast_side IS NULL OR t.fast_side=p.side);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _rule_break;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _rule_break AS
SELECT m.symbol,
       CASE WHEN c.ctx='bullish' AND m.close>m.hh_20_excl AND m.close>=COALESCE(m.vwap20,m.close) THEN 'BUY'
            WHEN c.ctx='bearish' AND m.close<m.ll_20_excl AND m.close<=COALESCE(m.vwap20,m.close) THEN 'SELL' END AS side,
       m.close AS entry,
       CASE WHEN c.ctx='bullish' THEN m.close - ((SELECT k_sl FROM _params)*m.atr14)
            WHEN c.ctx='bearish' THEN m.close + ((SELECT k_sl FROM _params)*m.atr14) END AS sl,
       CASE WHEN c.ctx='bullish' THEN m.close + ((SELECT k_tp FROM _params)*m.atr14)
            WHEN c.ctx='bearish' THEN m.close - ((SELECT k_tp FROM _params)*m.atr14) END AS tp,
       'breakoutN+VWAP+BB' AS reason, m.ts AS bar_ts, m.atr_pct
FROM _m1 m JOIN _ctx c ON c.symbol=m.symbol
WHERE m.atr_pct >= (SELECT atr_min_pct FROM _params)
  AND ( (c.ctx='bullish' AND m.close>m.hh_20_excl AND (m.bb_up20 IS NULL OR m.close>=m.bb_mid20))
     OR (c.ctx='bearish' AND m.close<m.ll_20_excl AND (m.bb_dn20 IS NULL OR m.close<=m.bb_mid20)) );

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _rule_macd_obv;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _rule_macd_obv AS
WITH obv_step AS (
  SELECT m.symbol,m.ts, m.obv - LAG(m.obv) OVER (PARTITION BY m.symbol ORDER BY m.ts) AS d_obv FROM _m1 m
)
SELECT m.symbol,
       CASE WHEN m.macd IS NOT NULL AND m.macd_signal9 IS NOT NULL AND m.macd>m.macd_signal9 AND COALESCE(o.d_obv,0)>=0 THEN 'BUY'
            WHEN m.macd IS NOT NULL AND m.macd_signal9 IS NOT NULL AND m.macd<m.macd_signal9 AND COALESCE(o.d_obv,0)<=0 THEN 'SELL' END AS side,
       m.close AS entry,
       m.close - ((SELECT k_sl FROM _params)*m.atr14) AS sl,
       m.close + ((SELECT k_tp FROM _params)*m.atr14) AS tp,
       'MACD≈SMA+OBV' AS reason, m.ts AS bar_ts, m.atr_pct
FROM _m1 m LEFT JOIN obv_step o ON o.symbol=m.symbol AND o.ts=m.ts
WHERE m.atr_pct >= (SELECT atr_min_pct FROM _params);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _rules_ok;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _rules_ok AS
SELECT r.*
FROM (SELECT * FROM _rule_break UNION ALL SELECT * FROM _rule_macd_obv) r
JOIN _m1 m ON m.symbol=r.symbol AND m.ts=r.bar_ts
LEFT JOIN _trend5 t ON t.symbol=r.symbol
WHERE r.side IS NOT NULL
  AND r.atr_pct >= (SELECT atr_min_pct FROM _params)
  AND ((SELECT require_trend FROM _params)=0 OR t.fast_side IS NULL OR t.fast_side=r.side);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _cand_all;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _cand_all AS
SELECT symbol,side,entry,sl,tp,reason,bar_ts FROM _cand_plan_ok
UNION ALL
SELECT symbol,side,entry,sl,tp,reason,bar_ts FROM _rules_ok;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _eligible;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible AS
SELECT c.symbol,c.side,c.entry,c.sl,c.tp,c.reason,c.bar_ts,
       COALESCE(b.last_side,'') AS last_side, COALESCE(b.consec,0) AS consec, COALESCE(b.last_ts,0) AS last_ts
FROM _cand_all c LEFT JOIN b_state b ON b.symbol=c.symbol;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _filtered;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _filtered AS
SELECT e.* FROM _eligible e,_params pr
WHERE (e.bar_ts - e.last_ts) >= pr.cooldown
  AND (CASE WHEN e.side=e.last_side THEN e.consec < pr.max_consec ELSE 1 END)
  AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM signals_B s WHERE s.symbol=e.symbol AND s.side=e.side AND s.created_ts >= e.bar_ts);

BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
INSERT INTO signals_B(symbol,side,price,reason,created_ts)
SELECT symbol,side,entry,reason,strftime('%s','now') FROM _filtered;

INSERT INTO b_state(symbol,last_side,consec,last_ts)
SELECT f.symbol, f.side,
       CASE WHEN f.side=COALESCE(b.last_side,'') THEN COALESCE(b.consec,0)+1 ELSE 1 END,
       f.bar_ts
FROM _filtered f LEFT JOIN b_state b ON b.symbol=f.symbol
ON CONFLICT(symbol) DO UPDATE SET
  last_side=excluded.last_side,
  consec=CASE WHEN b_state.last_side=excluded.last_side THEN b_state.consec+1 ELSE 1 END,
  last_ts=excluded.last_ts;
COMMIT;

SELECT 'emitted',COUNT(*) FROM _filtered;
SQL
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
UDB="${UDB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
ADB="${ADB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"

attempts=0
max=5
while :; do
  if sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS u_syms(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY);
DELETE FROM u_syms;
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO u_syms(symbol)
SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current;
COMMIT;
DETACH DATABASE udb;
SQL
  then
    echo "sync u.db → a.db.u_syms done"
    exit 0
  fi
  attempts=$((attempts+1))
  if [ $attempts -ge $max ]; then
    echo "sync failed after $attempts attempts" >&2
    exit 1
  fi
  sleep 1
done
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db}"
has_col(){ [ "$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pragma_table_info('$1') WHERE name='$2';")" -gt 0 ]; }
sqlite3 "$BDB" "PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000; PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_plan(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
 symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, score REAL, side TEXT,
 entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL,
 qty REAL, margin REAL, notional REAL,
 created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
 symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sigB_ts ON signals_B(created_ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sigB_sym_ts ON signals_B(symbol,created_ts);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_state(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, last_side TEXT, consec INTEGER, last_ts INTEGER);
"
for def in "entry REAL" "sl REAL" "tp REAL" "qty REAL" "margin REAL" "notional REAL" "created_ts INTEGER"; do
  n="${def%% *}"; has_col signals_B_plan "$n" || sqlite3 "$BDB" "ALTER TABLE signals_B_plan ADD COLUMN $def;"
done
for def in "symbol TEXT" "side TEXT" "price REAL" "reason TEXT" "created_ts INTEGER"; do
  n="${def%% *}"; has_col signals_B "$n" || sqlite3 "$BDB" "ALTER TABLE signals_B ADD COLUMN $def;"
done
echo "migrate: ok"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
SCRIPTS="$ROOT/scripts"
LOG="$ROOT/logs/ohlcv_daemon.log"
STEP=300         # 5 min
OFFSET=1         # hh:mm:01
GRACE=4          # re-essai si la close n'est pas dispo
RETRY=1

mkdir -p "$ROOT/logs"

align() {
  now=$(date +%s)
  next=$(( now - (now % STEP) + STEP + OFFSET ))
  sleep $(( next - now ))
}

expected_ts() {
  # timestamp de la bougie 5m qui vient de se clore
  n=$(date +%s)
  echo $(( n - (n % STEP) ))
}

have_expected() {
  exp="$1"
  sqlite3 -noheader "$ROOT/data/a.db" "
SELECT MIN(ok) FROM (
  SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END ok FROM ohlcv_5m
  UNION ALL
  SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END FROM ohlcv_15m
  UNION ALL
  SELECT CASE WHEN MAX(ts)=$exp THEN 1 ELSE 0 END FROM ohlcv_30m
);" 2>/dev/null
}

run_cycle() {
  "$SCRIPTS/fetch_ohlcv_once.sh"  >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  "$SCRIPTS/harden_o_db.sh"       >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  "$SCRIPTS/purge_non_current.sh" >> "$LOG" 2>&1 || true
}

while true; do
  align
  exp=$(expected_ts)
  run_cycle
  ok=$(have_expected "$exp" || echo 0)
  if [ "$ok" != "1" ] && [ "$RETRY" -gt 0 ]; then
    sleep "$GRACE"
    run_cycle
  fi
done
----- FILE END -----

MTime: 2025-10-10 10:02:24.808261099 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _src;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _src AS
SELECT symbol,'5m' tf,ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_5m
UNION ALL SELECT symbol,'15m',ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_15m
UNION ALL SELECT symbol,'30m',ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_30m;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _base;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _base AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,o,h,l,c,v,
       LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS cp
FROM _src;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _rsi;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _rsi AS
WITH g AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
         MAX(c-COALESCE(cp,c),0) AS g,
         MAX(COALESCE(cp,c)-c,0) AS l
  FROM _base
)
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       100-100.0/(1+AVG(g) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)
                    /NULLIF(AVG(l) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING),0)) AS rsi
FROM g;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _ema;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _ema AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       AVG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 9 PRECEDING)  AS ema_f,
       AVG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 21 PRECEDING) AS ema_s
FROM _base;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _macd;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _macd AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       (ema_f-ema_s) AS macd,
       AVG(ema_f-ema_s) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 8 PRECEDING) AS macd_sig
FROM _ema;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _adx;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _adx AS
WITH x AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,h,l,
         LAG(h) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS hp,
         LAG(l) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS lp
  FROM _base
),
dm AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
         MAX(h-COALESCE(hp,h),0) AS dmp,
         MAX(COALESCE(lp,l)-l,0) AS dmm
  FROM x
)
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       100*ABS(AVG(dmp) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)
             -AVG(dmm) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING))
       /(AVG(dmp) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)
        +AVG(dmm) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)+0.001) AS adx
FROM dm;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _obv;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _obv AS
WITH x AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,c,v,
         LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS cp
  FROM _base
),
o AS (
  SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
         SUM(CASE WHEN cp IS NULL THEN 0
                  WHEN c>cp THEN v
                  WHEN c<cp THEN -v
                  ELSE 0 END) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS obv
  FROM x
)
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,obv,
       obv-LAG(obv,20) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,tf ORDER BY ts) AS obv_slope
FROM o;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _merge;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _merge AS
SELECT b.symbol,b.tf,b.ts,b.c,b.v,
       e.ema_f,e.ema_s,m.macd,m.macd_sig,
       r.rsi,a.adx,o.obv_slope
FROM _base b
LEFT JOIN _ema e USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _macd m USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _rsi r USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _adx a USING(symbol,tf,ts)
LEFT JOIN _obv o USING(symbol,tf,ts);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _s_tf;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _s_tf AS
SELECT symbol,tf,ts,
       ((ema_f-ema_s)/NULLIF(ABS(ema_f)+ABS(ema_s),0))*0.4 +
       ((macd-macd_sig)/NULLIF(ABS(macd)+ABS(macd_sig),0))*0.3 +
       ((rsi-50)/50.0)*0.2 +
       ((adx-20)/20.0)*0.1 +
       (obv_slope/NULLIF(ABS(obv_slope)+1,0))*0.1 AS s
FROM _merge;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _S;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _S AS
WITH w AS (SELECT 0.5 AS w30,0.3 AS w15,0.2 AS w5)
SELECT s.symbol,
       SUM(CASE 
              WHEN tf='30m' THEN s.s*(SELECT w30 FROM w)
              WHEN tf='15m' THEN s.s*(SELECT w15 FROM w)
              WHEN tf='5m'  THEN s.s*(SELECT w5  FROM w)
              ELSE 0 END) AS S
FROM _s_tf s GROUP BY s.symbol;

-- Normalisation des probas: somme = 1
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _probs;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _probs AS
WITH raw AS (
  SELECT symbol,S,
         CASE WHEN S>0 THEN S ELSE 0 END AS pb_raw,
         CASE WHEN S<0 THEN -S ELSE 0 END AS ps_raw,
         CASE WHEN ABS(S)<=1 THEN 1-ABS(S) ELSE 0 END AS ph_raw
  FROM _S
),
z AS (
  SELECT symbol,S,pb_raw,ph_raw,ps_raw,(pb_raw+ph_raw+ps_raw) AS z FROM raw
)
SELECT symbol,S,
       CASE WHEN z=0 THEN 0.0 ELSE pb_raw/z END AS pb,
       CASE WHEN z=0 THEN 1.0 ELSE ph_raw/z END AS ph,
       CASE WHEN z=0 THEN 0.0 ELSE ps_raw/z END AS ps
FROM z;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _ctx;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _ctx AS
SELECT symbol,S,pb,ph,ps,
       CASE WHEN S>0.25 THEN 'bullish'
            WHEN S<-0.25 THEN 'bearish'
            ELSE 'range' END AS ctx
FROM _probs;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO a_context_state(symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,s,updated_at)
SELECT symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,S,datetime('now') FROM _ctx;

INSERT INTO a_signals(ts,symbol,s,pb,ph,ps,ctx)
SELECT datetime('now'),symbol,S,pb,ph,ps,ctx FROM _ctx;

COMMIT;
SQL

echo "A: build done (normalized probs)."
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${TDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db}"
: "${XDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db}"

# FILL des NEW
sqlite3 "$XDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000; PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db' AS tdb;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _new AS
SELECT o.id,o.symbol,o.side,o.price,o.qty,o.sl,o.tp,o.created_ts
FROM x_orders o LEFT JOIN x_positions p ON p.symbol=o.symbol
WHERE o.status='NEW' AND p.symbol IS NULL;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _nx AS
SELECT n.id,n.symbol,
       COALESCE(MIN(CASE WHEN t.ts_ms >= n.created_ts*1000 THEN t.ts_ms END),
                MAX(t.ts_ms)) AS nx_ms
FROM _new n JOIN tdb.ticks t ON t.instId=n.symbol
GROUP BY n.id;


CREATE TEMP TABLE _exec AS
SELECT n.id,n.symbol,n.side,n.qty,
       CASE WHEN n.side='BUY'
            THEN n.price*(1 + (SELECT slippage_bps FROM x_params WHERE id=1)/10000.0)
            ELSE n.price*(1 - (SELECT slippage_bps FROM x_params WHERE id=1)/10000.0) END AS fill_px,
       x.nx_ms
FROM _new n JOIN _nx x USING(id);

INSERT INTO x_fills(order_id,symbol,side,price,qty,fill_ts,kind)
SELECT id,symbol,side,fill_px,qty, nx_ms/1000,'OPEN' FROM _exec;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO x_positions(symbol,side,qty,entry,sl,tp,open_ts)
SELECT o.symbol,o.side,e.qty,e.fill_px,o.sl,o.tp,e.nx_ms/1000
FROM x_orders o JOIN _exec e ON e.id=o.id;

UPDATE x_orders SET status='FILLED', updated_ts=(SELECT nx_ms/1000 FROM _exec WHERE _exec.id=x_orders.id)
WHERE id IN (SELECT id FROM _exec);

DETACH DATABASE tdb;
SQL

# SL/TP et PnL + wallet
sqlite3 "$XDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000; PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db' AS tdb;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _lt AS
SELECT t.instId AS symbol,
       MAX(t.ts_ms) AS ts_ms,
       (SELECT price FROM tdb.ticks t2 WHERE t2.instId=t.instId ORDER BY t2.ts_ms DESC LIMIT 1) AS px
FROM tdb.ticks t
WHERE t.instId IN (SELECT symbol FROM x_positions)
GROUP BY t.instId;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _hits AS
SELECT p.symbol,p.side,p.qty,p.entry,p.sl,p.tp,l.px,l.ts_ms
FROM x_positions p JOIN _lt l ON l.symbol=p.symbol
WHERE (p.side='BUY'  AND ((p.sl IS NOT NULL AND l.px<=p.sl) OR (p.tp IS NOT NULL AND l.px>=p.tp)))
   OR (p.side='SELL' AND ((p.sl IS NOT NULL AND l.px>=p.sl) OR (p.tp IS NOT NULL AND l.px<=p.tp)));

CREATE TEMP TABLE _closed AS
SELECT
 (SELECT id FROM x_orders o WHERE o.symbol=h.symbol AND o.status='FILLED' ORDER BY o.id DESC LIMIT 1) AS order_id,
 h.symbol, CASE WHEN h.side='BUY' THEN 'SELL' ELSE 'BUY' END AS side,
 h.px AS price, h.qty AS qty, h.ts_ms/1000 AS fill_ts
FROM _hits h;

INSERT INTO x_fills(order_id,symbol,side,price,qty,fill_ts,kind)
SELECT order_id,symbol,side,price,qty,fill_ts,'CLOSE' FROM _closed;

INSERT INTO x_ledger(symbol,event,detail,pnl,ts)
SELECT c.symbol,'CLOSE','SLTP',
       CASE WHEN (SELECT side FROM x_positions WHERE symbol=c.symbol)='BUY'
            THEN (c.price - (SELECT entry FROM x_positions WHERE symbol=c.symbol))*c.qty
            ELSE ((SELECT entry FROM x_positions WHERE symbol=c.symbol) - c.price)*c.qty END,
       c.fill_ts
FROM _closed c;

DELETE FROM x_positions WHERE symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM _closed);
UPDATE x_orders SET status='CLOSED', updated_ts=strftime('%s','now')
WHERE symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM _closed) AND status='FILLED';

-- wallet: balance = start_balance + SUM(pnl), equity = balance
UPDATE x_wallet
SET balance = (SELECT start_balance FROM x_wallet WHERE id=1)
              + COALESCE((SELECT SUM(pnl) FROM x_ledger),0),
    equity = balance,
    updated_ts = strftime('%s','now')
WHERE id=1;

DETACH DATABASE tdb;
SQL

echo "paper: ok"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
fail(){ echo "FAIL: $*" >&2; exit 1; }

echo "== latest plans =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$BDB" "
WITH last_ts AS (SELECT MAX(ts_utc) t FROM b_plans)
SELECT symbol, side, ROUND(score,2), ROUND(price,6), ROUND(sl,6), ROUND(tp,6),
       ROUND(size_usd,2), ROUND(vol_win,3)
FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT t FROM last_ts)
ORDER BY score DESC LIMIT 12;
"

bad=$(sqlite3 -noheader "$BDB" "
WITH last_ts AS (SELECT MAX(ts_utc) t FROM b_plans),
chk AS (SELECT side, price, sl, tp FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT t FROM last_ts))
SELECT COUNT(*) FROM chk
WHERE (side='BUY'  AND NOT(sl<price AND tp>price))
   OR (side='SELL' AND NOT(sl>price AND tp<price));
")
[ "$bad" = "0" ] || fail "SL/TP incohérents ($bad)"

echo "OK: b.db health strict"

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${TDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db}"
: "${ADB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"
sqlite3 "$ADB" "PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_1m(symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
 open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
 PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts));"
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<'SQL'
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db' AS tdb;
WITH s AS (
  SELECT instId AS symbol,
         (CAST(ts_ms AS INTEGER)/1000) AS ts_s,
         price, size
  FROM tdb.ticks
),
m AS (
  SELECT symbol,(ts_s/60)*60 AS ts, price, size,
         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,(ts_s/60)*60 ORDER BY ts_s ASC)  rn_o,
         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol,(ts_s/60)*60 ORDER BY ts_s DESC) rn_c
  FROM s
),
agg AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts,
         MAX(CASE WHEN rn_o=1 THEN price END) AS open,
         MAX(CASE WHEN rn_c=1 THEN price END) AS close,
         MIN(price) AS low, MAX(price) AS high, SUM(size) AS volume
  FROM m GROUP BY symbol, ts
)
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ohlcv_1m(symbol,ts,open,high,low,close,volume)
SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume FROM agg;
DETACH DATABASE tdb;
SQL
echo "ohlcv_1m built from t.db.ticks"

Size: 3461
MTime: 2025-10-10 12:20:01.641717624 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
TDB="$ROOT/data/t.db"
UDB="$ROOT/data/u.db"
BDB="$ROOT/data/b.db"

SQLQ=$(cat <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$ADB"' AS adb;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$TDB"' AS tdb;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$UDB"' AS udb;

-- Paramètres
WITH P AS (
  SELECT
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='min_score_buy')   AS REAL) AS min_sb,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='max_score_sell')  AS REAL) AS max_ss,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='lookback_sec')    AS INTEGER) AS lb,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='min_sl_pct')      AS REAL) AS min_sl,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='rr')              AS REAL) AS rr,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='size_usd_base')   AS REAL) AS sbase,
    CAST((SELECT value FROM b_params WHERE key='size_scale')      AS REAL) AS sscale
)
-- Univers en cours
, U AS (
  SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current
)
-- Score A normalisé 0..100 et flag BUY/SELL/NONE
, A AS (
  SELECT s.symbol,
         50.0 + 50.0*MAX(MIN(s.s,1.0),-1.0) AS score,
         CASE
           WHEN s.s>=0.25 THEN 'BUY'
           WHEN s.s<=-0.25 THEN 'SELL'
           ELSE 'NONE'
         END AS flag
  FROM adb.a_context_state s
  JOIN U USING(symbol)
)
-- Référence ticks sur fenêtre lookback
, REF AS (
  SELECT
    symbol,
    MAX(ts_ms) AS ts_last,
    MAX(price) AS pmax,
    MIN(price) AS pmin,
    (SELECT price FROM tdb.ticks t2 WHERE t2.symbol=t.symbol ORDER BY ts_ms DESC LIMIT 1) AS plast
  FROM tdb.ticks t
  WHERE ts_ms >= (CAST(strftime('%s','now') AS INTEGER)*1000 - (SELECT lb*1000 FROM P))
  GROUP BY symbol
)
-- Candidats BUY
, CB AS (
  SELECT A.symbol,'BUY' AS side, A.score, R.plast, R.pmax, R.pmin,
         CASE WHEN R.plast>0 THEN (R.pmax-R.pmin)/R.plast*100 ELSE 0 END AS vol_pct
  FROM A JOIN REF R USING(symbol), P
  WHERE A.flag='BUY' AND A.score >= (SELECT min_sb FROM P)
)
-- Candidats SELL
, CS AS (
  SELECT A.symbol,'SELL' AS side, A.score, R.plast, R.pmax, R.pmin,
         CASE WHEN R.plast>0 THEN (R.pmax-R.pmin)/R.plast*100 ELSE 0 END AS vol_pct
  FROM A JOIN REF R USING(symbol), P
  WHERE A.flag='SELL' AND A.score <= (SELECT max_ss FROM P)
)
, C AS (SELECT * FROM CB UNION ALL SELECT * FROM CS)
-- Gestion du risque: SL% = max(vol*1.2, min_sl)
, RISK AS (
  SELECT C.*,
         MAX(vol_pct*1.20, (SELECT min_sl FROM P)) AS sl_pct,
         (SELECT rr FROM P) AS rr,
         (SELECT sbase FROM P) AS sbase,
         (SELECT sscale FROM P) AS sscale
  FROM C
)
-- Plan: SL/TP/size
, PLAN AS (
  SELECT
    symbol, side, score,
    plast AS price,
    CASE WHEN side='BUY'  THEN plast*(1.0 - sl_pct/100.0)
         ELSE plast*(1.0 + sl_pct/100.0) END AS sl,
    CASE WHEN side='BUY'  THEN plast*(1.0 + (sl_pct*rr)/100.0)
         ELSE plast*(1.0 - (sl_pct*rr)/100.0) END AS tp,
    MIN(MAX(sbase*(1.0 + sscale*((score-60.0)/40.0)), sbase*0.5), sbase*3.0) AS size_usd,
    vol_pct
  FROM RISK
)
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO b_plans(ts_utc,symbol,side,score,price,sl,tp,size_usd,vol_win,src)
SELECT datetime('now'), symbol, side, score, price, sl, tp, size_usd, vol_pct, 'ticks' FROM PLAN;

DETACH DATABASE adb; DETACH DATABASE tdb; DETACH DATABASE udb;
SQL
)

# retries soft contre "database is locked"
for i in 1 2 3 4 5; do
  if sqlite3 "$BDB" "$SQLQ"; then
    echo "B: build ok"; exit 0
  fi
  sleep 0.8
done
echo "B: build failed (locked)"; exit 1
----- FILE END -----

Size: 1391
MTime: 2025-10-10 09:54:51.448342049 +0200

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
BIN="$ROOT/bin"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
mkdir -p "$BIN"

# Tables de versionnage si absentes
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_release(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  file TEXT NOT NULL,
  sha256 TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  PRIMARY KEY(version,file)
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS a_final_marks(
  version TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  symbols INTEGER NOT NULL,
  bullish INTEGER NOT NULL,
  bearish INTEGER NOT NULL,
  range   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS a_snapshots(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  s REAL NOT NULL, pb REAL NOT NULL, ph REAL NOT NULL, ps REAL NOT NULL, ctx TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(version,symbol)
);
SQL

# Figer scripts
install -m 0755 "$ROOT/scripts/build_a_once.sh"   "$BIN/build_a_once.sh"
install -m 0755 "$ROOT/scripts/health_a_db.sh"    "$BIN/health_a_db.sh"
install -m 0755 "$ROOT/scripts/health_a_strict.sh" "$BIN/health_a_strict.sh"

VER="${VER:-analysisA-$(date -u +%F-T%H%MZ)}"
for f in build_a_once.sh health_a_db.sh health_a_strict.sh; do
  sha=$(sha256sum "$BIN/$f" | awk '{print $1}')
  sqlite3 "$ADB" "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO code_release(version,file,sha256) VALUES('$VER','$f','$sha');"
done
echo "A release frozen: $VER"

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${ADB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db}"

sqlB(){ sqlite3 "$BDB" "$@"; }

# retry runner to bypass transient locks
runB(){
  tries=0; max=6
  while :; do
    if sqlite3 "$BDB" 1>/dev/null 2>/dev/null <<SQL
$1
SQL
    then break; fi
    tries=$((tries+1))
    [ $tries -ge $max ] && { echo "fatal: database is locked"; exit 1; }
    sleep 1
  done
}

# pragmas
sqlB "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=12000; PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;"

# drop sécurisé
typ=$(sqlB "SELECT COALESCE(type,'') FROM sqlite_master WHERE name='v_indic5m_fast' LIMIT 1;")
[ "$typ" = "table" ] && sqlB "DROP TABLE IF EXISTS v_indic5m_fast;"
[ "$typ" = "view"  ] && sqlB "DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS v_indic5m_fast;"

# table cible
runB "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS v_indic5m_fast(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  ts INTEGER,
  sma9 REAL,
  sma21 REAL
);"

# build à partir de A.ohlcv_5m (colonnes: symbol, ts, c)
runB "
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
WITH base AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, c AS close
  FROM adb.ohlcv_5m
),
ema AS (
  SELECT b.symbol, b.ts,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 8 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21
  FROM base b
),
last AS (
  SELECT e.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn
  FROM ema e
)
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO v_indic5m_fast(symbol,ts,sma9,sma21)
SELECT symbol, ts, sma9, sma21 FROM last WHERE rn=1;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
"

echo "== v_indic5m_fast built =="
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
VER="${VER:?specify VER}"

echo "== CODE HASHES =="
sqlite3 -csv "$ADB" "SELECT file,sha256 FROM code_release ORDER BY file" 2>/dev/null | while IFS=, read -r f ref; do
  [ -f "$ROOT/bin/$f" ] || { echo "$f missing"; continue; }
  cur=$(sha256sum "$ROOT/bin/$f" | awk '{print $1}')
  match=no; [ "$cur" = "$ref" ] && match=yes
  echo "$f expected=$ref current=$cur match=$match"
done

echo "== FINAL MARKS =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "SELECT version, tf, max_ts, symbols, rows_per_symbol, created_at FROM o_final_marks WHERE version='$VER' ORDER BY tf;"

echo "== HEALTH STRICT =="
"$ROOT/bin/health_o_strict.sh"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
VER="${VER:?specify VER}"

echo "== CODE HASHES =="
sqlite3 -csv "$ADB" "SELECT file,sha256 FROM code_release WHERE version LIKE 'analysisA-%' ORDER BY file" 2>/dev/null | while IFS=, read -r f ref; do
  [ -f "$ROOT/bin/$f" ] || { echo "$f missing"; continue; }
  cur=$(sha256sum "$ROOT/bin/$f" | awk '{print $1}')
  echo "$f expected=$ref current=$cur match=$([ "$ref" = "$cur" ] && echo yes || echo NO)"
done

echo "== FINAL MARK =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "SELECT version, symbols, bullish, bearish, range, created_at FROM a_final_marks WHERE version='$VER';"

echo "== SAMPLE SNAPSHOT =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "SELECT symbol, s, ctx FROM a_snapshots WHERE version='$VER' ORDER BY s DESC LIMIT 5;"

echo "== HEALTH STRICT =="
"$ROOT/bin/health_a_strict.sh"

MTime: 2025-10-10 12:37:09.577588276 +0200

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${ADB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db}"

sqlA(){ sqlite3 "$ADB" "$@"; }
sqlB(){ sqlite3 "$BDB" "$@"; }

echo "== Fix AB interface =="

# PRAGMAs
sqlB "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;"
sqlA "PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;"

# Helpers
obj_type(){ sqlB "SELECT COALESCE(type,'') FROM sqlite_master WHERE name='$1' LIMIT 1;"; }
safe_drop(){
  t="$(obj_type "$1")"
  case "$t" in
    table) sqlB "DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $1;" ;;
    view)  sqlB "DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS $1;" ;;
    *) : ;;
  esac
}
has_table_A(){ [ "$(sqlA "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='$1';")" -gt 0 ]; }
find_col(){
  tbl="$1"; shift
  for c in "$@"; do
    if [ "$(sqlA "SELECT 1 FROM pragma_table_info('$tbl') WHERE name='$c' LIMIT 1;")" = "1" ]; then
      echo "$c"; return 0
    fi
  done
  echo ""
}

# 1) Tables B minimales
sqlB "
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_plan(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, score REAL, side TEXT,
  entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL, qty REAL, margin REAL, notional REAL, created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sigB_ts ON signals_B(created_ts);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_state(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, last_side TEXT, consec INTEGER, last_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS v_contexts_A_latest(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ctx TEXT, pb REAL, ph REAL, ps REAL, ts INTEGER
);
"

# 2) contexts_A_latest
HAS_CTX="$(sqlA "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='contexts_A';")"
sqlB "BEGIN IMMEDIATE; DELETE FROM v_contexts_A_latest; COMMIT;"
if [ "$HAS_CTX" -gt 0 ]; then
  sqlB "
  ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
  BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
  INSERT INTO v_contexts_A_latest(symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,ts)
  SELECT c.symbol, c.ctx, c.pb, c.ph, c.ps, c.ts
  FROM adb.contexts_A c
  WHERE c.ts IN (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM adb.contexts_A c2 WHERE c2.symbol=c.symbol);
  COMMIT; DETACH DATABASE adb;
  "
else
  sqlB "
  ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
  WITH lb AS (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) ts FROM adb.ohlcv_1m GROUP BY symbol)
  BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
  INSERT INTO v_contexts_A_latest(symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,ts)
  SELECT o.symbol,'fallback',o.c,o.h,o.l,o.ts
  FROM adb.ohlcv_1m o JOIN lb ON lb.symbol=o.symbol AND lb.ts=o.ts;
  COMMIT; DETACH DATABASE adb;
  " 2>/dev/null || true
fi

# 3) Détection colonnes OHLCV 1m
if ! has_table_A "ohlcv_1m"; then echo "Erreur: ADB.ohlcv_1m absente"; exit 1; fi
S1=$(find_col ohlcv_1m symbol sym ticker)
T1=$(find_col ohlcv_1m ts t timestamp time epoch)
O1=$(find_col ohlcv_1m o open o_open)
H1=$(find_col ohlcv_1m h high o_high)
L1=$(find_col ohlcv_1m l low o_low)
C1=$(find_col ohlcv_1m c close o_close)
V1=$(find_col ohlcv_1m v volume vol)

for v in S1 T1 O1 H1 L1 C1; do [ -n "$(eval echo \$$v)" ] || { echo "Erreur: colonne manquante pour $v dans ohlcv_1m"; exit 1; }; done
[ -n "$V1" ] || V1="0.0"

# 4) v_indic_1m matérialisée, drop sécurisé
safe_drop v_indic_1m
sqlB "
CREATE TABLE v_indic_1m(
  symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
  open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
  spread_frac REAL, vol_sma20 REAL,
  sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL, sma50 REAL,
  atr14 REAL, atr_pct REAL,
  hh_20_excl REAL, ll_20_excl REAL
);
"
sqlB "
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
WITH base AS (
  SELECT $S1 AS symbol, $T1 AS ts, $O1 AS open, $H1 AS high, $L1 AS low, $C1 AS close,
         COALESCE($V1,0.0) AS volume
  FROM adb.ohlcv_1m
),
ema AS (
  SELECT b.symbol, b.ts, b.open,b.high,b.low,b.close,b.volume,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 8 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 49 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma50
  FROM base b
),
rng AS (
  SELECT e.*,
         MAX(high) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING) AS hh_20_excl,
         MIN(low)  OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING) AS ll_20_excl
  FROM ema e
),
atr AS (
  SELECT r.*,
         AVG(high - low) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 13 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS atr14
  FROM rng r
)
INSERT INTO v_indic_1m
SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume,
       0.0005 AS spread_frac,
       0.0    AS vol_sma20,
       sma9, sma21, sma50,
       COALESCE(atr14,0.0) AS atr14,
       CASE WHEN close>0 AND atr14>0 THEN atr14/close*100.0 ELSE 0.0 END AS atr_pct,
       hh_20_excl, ll_20_excl
FROM atr;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
"

# 5) v_indic5m_fast matérialisée
USE_5M=0
if has_table_A "ohlcv_5m"; then
  S5=$(find_col ohlcv_5m symbol sym ticker)
  T5=$(find_col ohlcv_5m ts t timestamp time epoch)
  C5=$(find_col ohlcv_5m c close o_close)
  if [ -n "$S5" ] && [ -n "$T5" ] && [ -n "$C5" ]; then USE_5M=1; fi
fi

safe_drop v_indic5m_fast
sqlB "CREATE TABLE v_indic5m_fast(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ts INTEGER, sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL);"

if [ "$USE_5M" -eq 1 ]; then
  sqlB "
  ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
  WITH base AS (SELECT $S5 AS symbol, $T5 AS ts, $C5 AS close FROM adb.ohlcv_5m),
  ema AS (
    SELECT b.symbol, b.ts,
           AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 8 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
           AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21
    FROM base b
  ),
  last AS (SELECT e.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn FROM ema e)
  INSERT INTO v_indic5m_fast(symbol,ts,sma9,sma21)
  SELECT symbol, ts, sma9, sma21 FROM last WHERE rn=1;
  DETACH DATABASE adb;
  "
else
  sqlB "
  ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
  WITH m1 AS (
    SELECT $S1 AS symbol, (($T1/300)*300) AS ts5, $C1 AS close
    FROM adb.ohlcv_1m
  ),
  lastbar AS (
    SELECT symbol, ts5, MAX(rowid) AS rid
    FROM (SELECT rowid, symbol, ts5 FROM m1) t
    GROUP BY symbol, ts5
  ),
  base AS (
    SELECT m.symbol, m.ts5 AS ts, m.close
    FROM m1 m JOIN lastbar lb ON lb.rid = m.rowid
  ),
  ema AS (
    SELECT b.symbol, b.ts,
           AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 8 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
           AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21
    FROM base b
  ),
  last AS (SELECT e.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn FROM ema e)
  INSERT INTO v_indic5m_fast(symbol,ts,sma9,sma21)
  SELECT symbol, ts, sma9, sma21 FROM last WHERE rn=1;
  DETACH DATABASE adb;
  "
fi

echo "== Fix done =="
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
UDB="${UDB:-$DATA/u.db}"
ODB="${ODB:-$DATA/o.db}"
ADB="${ADB:-$DATA/a.db}"
TDB="${TDB:-$DATA/t.db}"
BDB="${BDB:-$DATA/b.db}"
XDB="${XDB:-$DATA/x.db}"
now=$(date +%s)

sql(){ sqlite3 "$1" -tabs "$2"; }
hdr(){ printf "== %s ==\n" "$1"; }
sep(){ printf -- "------------------------------\n"; }

# U
hdr "U (univers)"
sql "$UDB" "
SELECT 'runs_total',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM universe_runs),0);
SELECT 'published_last_run',COALESCE((SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs WHERE status='published' ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1),0);
SELECT 'available_now',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_universe_current),0);
"

# O
sep; hdr "O (ohlcv raw)"
sql "$ODB" "
SELECT 'ohlcv_5m_rows',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_5m),0);
SELECT 'ohlcv_15m_rows',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_15m),0);
SELECT 'ohlcv_30m_rows',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_30m),0);
SELECT 'ohlcv_5m_last_ts',COALESCE((SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_5m),0);
"

# A
sep; hdr "A (1m + u_syms + context)"
sql "$ADB" "
SELECT 'u_syms_rows',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM u_syms),0);
SELECT 'ohlcv_1m_rows',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_1m),0);
SELECT 'ohlcv_1m_last_ts',COALESCE((SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_1m),0);
SELECT 'contexts_latest',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_contexts_A_latest),0);
"

# T
sep; hdr "T (ticks)"
sql "$TDB" "
SELECT 'symbols',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT instId) FROM ticks),0);
SELECT 'ticks_total',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ticks),0);
SELECT 'last_tick_ms',COALESCE((SELECT MAX(ts_ms) FROM ticks),0);
"

# B
sep; hdr "B (indics + signaux)"
sql "$BDB" "
SELECT 'v_indic_1m_rows',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_indic_1m),0);
SELECT 'v_indic_1m_last_ts',COALESCE((SELECT MAX(ts) FROM v_indic_1m),0);
SELECT 'v_indic5m_fast_rows',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_indic5m_fast),0);
SELECT 'signals_B_total',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM signals_B),0);
"

# X
sep; hdr "X (paper)"
sql "$XDB" "
SELECT 'orders_NEW',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM x_orders WHERE status='NEW'),0);
SELECT 'orders_FILLED',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM x_orders WHERE status='FILLED'),0);
SELECT 'orders_CLOSED',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM x_orders WHERE status='CLOSED'),0);
SELECT 'positions_open',COALESCE((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM x_positions),0);
SELECT 'wallet_balance',COALESCE((SELECT balance FROM x_wallet WHERE id=1),0);
"

# Résumé OK/ALERT
sep; hdr "Summary U→O→A→T→B→X"
last_tick_ms=$(sqlite3 "$TDB" "SELECT COALESCE(MAX(ts_ms),0) FROM ticks;")
a1_last=$(sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT COALESCE(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_1m;")
o5_last=$(sqlite3 "$ODB" "SELECT COALESCE(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_5m;")
age_tick=$(( (now*1000 - last_tick_ms)/1000 ))
age_a1=$(( now - a1_last ))
age_o5=$(( now - o5_last ))
printf "U ok: %s\n" "$(sqlite3 "$UDB" "SELECT CASE WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_universe_current)>0 THEN 'OK' ELSE 'ALERT' END;")"
printf "O 5m: %s (age=%ss)\n" "$([ $age_o5 -le 900 ] && echo OK || echo ALERT)" "$age_o5"
printf "A 1m: %s (age=%ss)\n" "$([ $age_a1 -le 180 ] && echo OK || echo ALERT)" "$age_a1"
printf "T:    %s (age=%ss)\n" "$([ $age_tick -le 120 ] && echo OK || echo ALERT)" "$age_tick"
b_rows=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_indic_1m;")
printf "B v_indic_1m rows: %s\n" "$b_rows"
x_pos=$(sqlite3 "$XDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM x_positions;")
printf "X positions: %s\n" "$x_pos"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
BIN="$ROOT/bin"
BDB="$ROOT/data/b.db"
mkdir -p "$BIN"

sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_release(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  file TEXT NOT NULL,
  sha256 TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  PRIMARY KEY(version,file)
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_final_marks(
  version TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  ts_utc TEXT NOT NULL,
  n_pairs INTEGER NOT NULL,
  n_buy INTEGER NOT NULL,
  n_sell INTEGER NOT NULL,
  avg_score REAL NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_snapshots(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  side TEXT NOT NULL,
  score REAL NOT NULL,
  price REAL NOT NULL,
  sl REAL NOT NULL,
  tp REAL NOT NULL,
  size_usd REAL NOT NULL,
  ts_utc TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(version,symbol)
);
SQL

install -m 0755 "$ROOT/scripts/build_b_once.sh"     "$BIN/build_b_once.sh"
install -m 0755 "$ROOT/scripts/health_b_strict.sh"  "$BIN/health_b_strict.sh"
install -m 0755 "$ROOT/scripts/run_b_daemon.sh"     "$BIN/run_b_daemon.sh"

VER="${VER:-analysisB-$(date -u +%F-T%H%MZ)}"
for f in build_b_once.sh health_b_strict.sh run_b_daemon.sh; do
  sha=$(sha256sum "$BIN/$f" | awk '{print $1}')
  sqlite3 "$BDB" "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO code_release(version,file,sha256) VALUES('$VER','$f','$sha');"
done
echo "B release frozen: $VER"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="${ADB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"

echo "== coverage per TF (symbols x rows) =="
for t in ohlcv_5m ohlcv_15m ohlcv_30m; do
  printf -- "-- %s\n" "$t"
  sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol), SUM(cnt)
    FROM (SELECT symbol, COUNT(*) cnt FROM $t GROUP BY symbol);"
done

echo "== gaps check (0 attendu) =="
sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "
WITH tf(name,step) AS (VALUES('ohlcv_5m',300),('ohlcv_15m',900),('ohlcv_30m',1800)),
rows AS (
  SELECT 'ohlcv_5m' name,300 step,symbol,COUNT(*) n,MIN(ts) t0,MAX(ts) t1 FROM ohlcv_5m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_15m',900,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_30m',1800,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m GROUP BY symbol
),
gaps AS (
  SELECT name, symbol, MAX(0, ((t1-t0)/step + 1 - n)) AS missing FROM rows
)
SELECT name, SUM(missing) FROM gaps GROUP BY name;"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="${ADB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"

# 1) Dédoublonner (garde la + récente par (symbol,ts))
for T in 5m 15m 30m; do
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
DELETE FROM ohlcv_${T}
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol, ts ORDER BY rowid DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_${T}
  ) WHERE rn > 1
);
SQL
done

# 2) Compacter à exactement 100 bougies / symbole
for T in 5m 15m 30m; do
sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
DELETE FROM ohlcv_${T}
WHERE rowid IN (
  SELECT rowid FROM (
    SELECT rowid,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_${T}
  ) WHERE rn > 100
);
SQL
done

# 3) Contrainte d’unicité (après dédup, donc ça passe)
for T in 5m 15m 30m; do
sqlite3 "$ADB" "CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS uq_ohlcv_${T} ON ohlcv_${T}(symbol, ts);"
done

echo "o.db durci: dedup + 100 fixes + unique(symbol,ts)."
----- FILE END -----
