MTime: 2025-10-10 14:14:47.279953166 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db}"
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000; PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS v_feat_1m;
CREATE TABLE v_feat_1m(
  symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
  open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
  tp REAL, vwap20 REAL,
  bb_mid20 REAL, bb_up20 REAL, bb_dn20 REAL,
  macd REAL, macd_signal9 REAL, macd_hist REAL,
  obv REAL
);
WITH b AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume, (high+low+close)/3.0 AS tp
  FROM v_indic_1m
),
w AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume, tp,
    CASE WHEN SUM(volume) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 19 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) > 0
         THEN SUM(tp*volume) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 19 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)
              / SUM(volume)  OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 19 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)
         ELSE NULL END                                            AS vwap20,
    AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 19 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma20,
    AVG(close*close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 19 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS ex2_20,
    AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 11 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma12,
    AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 25 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma26,
    LAG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts) AS prev_close
  FROM b
),
w2 AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume, tp, vwap20, sma20, ex2_20,
         (sma12 - sma26) AS macd_raw,
         CASE WHEN prev_close IS NULL THEN 0.0
              WHEN close>prev_close THEN +volume
              WHEN close<prev_close THEN -volume
              ELSE 0.0 END AS obv_step
  FROM w
),
w3 AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume, tp, vwap20,
         sma20 AS bb_mid20,
         CASE WHEN ex2_20 IS NOT NULL AND sma20 IS NOT NULL THEN sma20 + 2.0*sqrt(MAX(ex2_20 - sma20*sma20,0.0)) END AS bb_up20,
         CASE WHEN ex2_20 IS NOT NULL AND sma20 IS NOT NULL THEN sma20 - 2.0*sqrt(MAX(ex2_20 - sma20*sma20,0.0)) END AS bb_dn20,
         macd_raw AS macd,
         AVG(macd_raw) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 8 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS macd_signal9,
         SUM(obv_step) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS obv
  FROM w2
)
INSERT INTO v_feat_1m
SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume, tp, vwap20,
       bb_mid20, bb_up20, bb_dn20,
       macd, macd_signal9, (macd-macd_signal9) AS macd_hist, obv
FROM w3;
SQL
echo "features: ok"
----- FILE END -----

-- table des trades matérialisés

  symbol TEXT, side TEXT, reason TEXT, score REAL,
  qty REAL,

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
INTERVAL_SEC="${INTERVAL_SEC:-7200}"
RETRY_DELAY="${RETRY_DELAY:-600}"
MAX_RETRY="${MAX_RETRY:-2}"

while true; do
  if DB="$DB" "$(dirname "$0")/build_universe.sh"; then
    sleep "$INTERVAL_SEC"
  else
    i=0
    while [ $i -lt $MAX_RETRY ]; do
      sleep "$RETRY_DELAY"
      if DB="$DB" "$(dirname "$0")/build_universe.sh"; then
        break
      fi
      i=$((i+1))
    done
    sleep "$INTERVAL_SEC"
  fi
done
----- FILE END -----

Path: /opt/scalp/project/bin/build_universe.sh
Size: 6373
MTime: 2025-10-09 19:35:45.183683140 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="${DB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db}"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$DB")"
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;

INSERT INTO universe_runs(started_at, status) VALUES(datetime('now'), 'running');
CREATE TEMP TABLE _run(id INTEGER); INSERT INTO _run VALUES (last_insert_rowid());
CREATE TEMP TABLE _status(ok INTEGER, reason TEXT); INSERT INTO _status VALUES (1,NULL);

CREATE TEMP TABLE _p AS
SELECT
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_usdt_volume_24h') AS REAL) AS min_vol,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_price') AS REAL) AS min_price,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='max_spread_bps') AS REAL) AS max_spread_bps,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='min_count') AS INTEGER) AS min_count,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='target_count') AS INTEGER) AS target_count,
  CAST((SELECT value FROM params WHERE key='max_churn') AS REAL) AS max_churn;

-- Pool multi-sources
CREATE TEMP TABLE _latest AS
SELECT name, MAX(ts) AS ts
FROM top_scores
WHERE name IN ('TOP35','TOP30','TOP100_VOL','FIXED5')
GROUP BY name;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _pool0 AS
SELECT s.symbol, s.score, s.name,
       CASE s.name
         WHEN 'TOP35' THEN 1
         WHEN 'TOP30' THEN 2
         WHEN 'TOP100_VOL' THEN 3
         WHEN 'FIXED5' THEN 4
         ELSE 9
       END AS pri
FROM top_scores s
JOIN _latest l ON l.name=s.name AND l.ts=s.ts;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _pool AS
WITH ranked AS (
  SELECT symbol, score, name, pri,
         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY pri ASC, score DESC) AS r
  FROM _pool0
)
SELECT symbol, score, name, pri
FROM ranked
WHERE r=1
ORDER BY pri ASC, score DESC;

UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'no_top_scores')
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _pool)=0;

-- Filtres pass1
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible1 AS
SELECT p.symbol, p.score
FROM _pool p
JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p)
  AND p.symbol NOT IN (SELECT symbol FROM blacklist);

-- Whitelist + core
INSERT INTO _eligible1(symbol,score)
SELECT w.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM whitelist w
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=w.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p);

INSERT INTO _eligible1(symbol,score)
SELECT c.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM core_symbols c
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=c.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT max_spread_bps FROM _p);

-- Filtres pass2 relaxés si pass1 insuffisant
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible2 AS
SELECT p.symbol, p.score
FROM _pool p
JOIN metrics_universe m USING(symbol)
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p)
  AND p.symbol NOT IN (SELECT symbol FROM blacklist);

INSERT INTO _eligible2(symbol,score)
SELECT w.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM whitelist w
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=w.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p);

INSERT INTO _eligible2(symbol,score)
SELECT c.symbol, COALESCE(p.score,0.0)
FROM core_symbols c
LEFT JOIN _pool p USING(symbol)
JOIN metrics_universe m ON m.symbol=c.symbol
WHERE m.active=1
  AND m.vol_usdt_24h >= (SELECT 0.5*min_vol FROM _p)
  AND m.price >= (SELECT min_price FROM _p)
  AND m.spread_bps <= (SELECT 2.0*max_spread_bps FROM _p);

-- Fusion + coupe
CREATE TEMP TABLE _eligible_final AS
SELECT symbol, MAX(score) AS score FROM (
  SELECT * FROM _eligible1
  UNION ALL
  SELECT * FROM _eligible2
  WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _eligible1) < (SELECT min_count FROM _p)
) GROUP BY symbol;

CREATE TEMP TABLE _cand AS
SELECT symbol, score
FROM _eligible_final
ORDER BY score DESC
LIMIT (SELECT target_count FROM _p);

-- Min requis
UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'too_few_symbols')
WHERE (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _cand) < (SELECT min_count FROM _p);

-- Churn
CREATE TEMP TABLE _prev AS
SELECT symbol
FROM universe_snapshots
WHERE run_id = (SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs WHERE status='published' ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1);

CREATE TEMP TABLE _churn AS
WITH prev_c AS (SELECT COUNT(*) AS c FROM _prev),
inter_c AS (SELECT COUNT(*) AS c FROM _cand c JOIN _prev p USING(symbol)),
r AS (
  SELECT (SELECT c FROM prev_c) AS prev_cnt,
         (SELECT c FROM inter_c) AS inter_cnt,
         (SELECT target_count FROM _p) AS tgt,
         (SELECT max_churn FROM _p) AS max_churn
)
SELECT prev_cnt, inter_cnt, tgt,
       CASE WHEN tgt>0 THEN 1.0 - (1.0*inter_cnt/tgt) ELSE 1.0 END AS churn,
       max_churn
FROM r;

UPDATE _status SET ok=0, reason=COALESCE(reason,'high_churn')
WHERE (SELECT prev_cnt FROM _churn) = (SELECT tgt FROM _churn)
  AND (SELECT churn FROM _churn) > (SELECT max_churn FROM _churn);

-- Publication
INSERT INTO universe_snapshots(run_id, symbol)
SELECT (SELECT id FROM _run), symbol
FROM _cand
WHERE (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1;

UPDATE universe_runs
SET status = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1 THEN 'published' ELSE 'failed' END,
    finished_at = datetime('now'),
    count = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1 THEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM _cand) END,
    reason = (SELECT reason FROM _status),
    symbol_list = CASE WHEN (SELECT ok FROM _status)=1
      THEN (SELECT GROUP_CONCAT(symbol, ',') FROM (SELECT symbol FROM _cand ORDER BY score DESC)) END
WHERE run_id=(SELECT id FROM _run);

COMMIT;
SQL

status=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT status FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
run_id=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT run_id FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
reason=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT reason FROM universe_runs ORDER BY run_id DESC LIMIT 1")
echo "run_id=$run_id status=$status reason=${reason:-none}"
[ "$status" = "published" ] && sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(*) AS count FROM v_universe_current;"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${XDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db}"

has_col(){ sqlite3 "$XDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pragma_table_info('$1') WHERE name='$2';"; }

sqlite3 "$XDB" "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_params(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK(id=1),
 risk_usd REAL, max_pos_per_symbol INTEGER, leverage REAL, slippage_bps REAL
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO x_params(id,risk_usd,max_pos_per_symbol,leverage,slippage_bps)
VALUES(1,50.0,1,3.0,2.0);
"

# x_params colonnes manquantes
[ "$(has_col x_params tp_mult)" = 0 ] && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_params ADD COLUMN tp_mult REAL;"
[ "$(has_col x_params sl_mult)" = 0 ] && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_params ADD COLUMN sl_mult REAL;"
[ "$(has_col x_params score_boost)" = 0 ] && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_params ADD COLUMN score_boost REAL;"
[ "$(has_col x_params risk_pct)" = 0 ] && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_params ADD COLUMN risk_pct REAL;"
[ "$(has_col x_params base_ccy)" = 0 ] && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_params ADD COLUMN base_ccy TEXT;"

sqlite3 "$XDB" "UPDATE x_params SET
 tp_mult=COALESCE(tp_mult,1.8),
 sl_mult=COALESCE(sl_mult,1.2),
 score_boost=COALESCE(score_boost,0.5),
 risk_pct=COALESCE(risk_pct,0.02),
 base_ccy=COALESCE(base_ccy,'USDT')
WHERE id=1;"

# tables
sqlite3 "$XDB" "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_state(id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK(id=1), last_signal_id INTEGER);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO x_state(id,last_signal_id) VALUES(1,0);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_orders(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
 symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, qty REAL,
 sl REAL, tp REAL, reason TEXT,
 status TEXT, signal_id INTEGER, created_ts INTEGER, updated_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_xo_sym_status ON x_orders(symbol,status);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_positions(
 symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, side TEXT, qty REAL, entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL, open_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_fills(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, order_id INTEGER, symbol TEXT,
 side TEXT, price REAL, qty REAL, fill_ts INTEGER, kind TEXT
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_ledger(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, symbol TEXT, event TEXT, detail TEXT, pnl REAL, ts INTEGER
);"

# x_orders colonnes manquantes
[ "$(has_col x_orders score)" = 0 ]    && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_orders ADD COLUMN score REAL;"
[ "$(has_col x_orders leverage)" = 0 ] && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_orders ADD COLUMN leverage REAL;"
[ "$(has_col x_orders margin)" = 0 ]   && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_orders ADD COLUMN margin REAL;"
[ "$(has_col x_orders notional)" = 0 ] && sqlite3 "$XDB" "ALTER TABLE x_orders ADD COLUMN notional REAL;"

# wallet paper
sqlite3 "$XDB" "
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_wallet(
 id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK(id=1),
 start_balance REAL, balance REAL, equity REAL, updated_ts INTEGER
);
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO x_wallet(id,start_balance,balance,equity,updated_ts)
VALUES(1,1000.0,1000.0,1000.0,strftime('%s','now'));
"
echo "X schema+wallet: ok"

MTime: 2025-10-10 13:19:55.841515700 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${ADB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db}"

sqlB(){ sqlite3 "$BDB" "$@"; }

# PRAGMAs
sqlB "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=12000; PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;"

# drop safe
drop_obj(){ t=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COALESCE(type,'') FROM sqlite_master WHERE name='$1'"); 
  [ "$t" = "table" ] && sqlB "DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $1;"; 
  [ "$t" = "view"  ] && sqlB "DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS $1;"; }

# Tables B minimales
sqlB "
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B_plan(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, ctx TEXT, score REAL, side TEXT,
  entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL, qty REAL, margin REAL, notional REAL, created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B(
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  symbol TEXT, side TEXT, price REAL, reason TEXT, created_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sigB_ts ON signals_B(created_ts);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_state(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, last_side TEXT, consec INTEGER, last_ts INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS v_contexts_A_latest(
  symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ctx TEXT, pb REAL, ph REAL, ps REAL, ts INTEGER
);
"

# v_contexts_A_latest depuis A
sqlB "
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
DELETE FROM v_contexts_A_latest;
INSERT INTO v_contexts_A_latest(symbol,ctx,pb,ph,ps,ts)
SELECT c.symbol, COALESCE(c.ctx,'fallback'), COALESCE(c.pb, o.c), COALESCE(c.ph, o.h), COALESCE(c.ps, o.l), COALESCE(c.ts, o.ts)
FROM (
  SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) ts FROM adb.ohlcv_5m GROUP BY symbol
) lb
JOIN adb.ohlcv_5m o ON o.symbol=lb.symbol AND o.ts=lb.ts
LEFT JOIN adb.contexts_A c ON c.symbol=o.symbol
;
COMMIT;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
"

# v_indic5m_fast
drop_obj v_indic5m_fast
sqlB "CREATE TABLE v_indic5m_fast(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ts INTEGER, sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL);"
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
WITH base AS (SELECT symbol, ts, c AS close FROM adb.ohlcv_5m),
ema AS (
  SELECT b.symbol, b.ts,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 8  PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21
  FROM base b
),
last AS (SELECT e.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn FROM ema e)
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO v_indic5m_fast(symbol,ts,sma9,sma21)
SELECT symbol, ts, sma9, sma21 FROM last WHERE rn=1;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
SQL

# v_indic_1m (schéma attendu par B, alimenté par 5m)
drop_obj v_indic_1m
sqlB "CREATE TABLE v_indic_1m(
  symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
  open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
  spread_frac REAL, vol_sma20 REAL,
  sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL, sma50 REAL,
  atr14 REAL, atr_pct REAL,
  hh_20_excl REAL, ll_20_excl REAL
);"
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
WITH base AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, o AS open, h AS high, l AS low, c AS close, v AS volume
  FROM adb.ohlcv_5m
),
ema AS (
  SELECT b.*,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 8  PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 49 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma50
  FROM base b
),
rng AS (
  SELECT e.*,
         MAX(high) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING) AS hh_20_excl,
         MIN(low)  OVER  (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING) AS ll_20_excl
  FROM ema e
),
atr AS (
  SELECT r.*,
         AVG(high - low) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 13 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS atr14
  FROM rng r
)
INSERT INTO v_indic_1m
SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume,
       0.0005, 0.0,
       sma9, sma21, sma50,
       COALESCE(atr14,0.0),
       CASE WHEN close>0 AND atr14>0 THEN atr14/close*100.0 ELSE 0.0 END,
       hh_20_excl, ll_20_excl
FROM atr;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
SQL

echo "v_indic5m_fast rows: $(sqlB 'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_indic5m_fast;')"
echo "v_indic_1m rows:    $(sqlB 'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_indic_1m;')"

Path: /opt/scalp/project/bin/build_x_trades.sh
Size: 1493
MTime: 2025-10-10 16:15:53.911365714 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
XDB="${XDB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db}"

sqlite3 "$XDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000;

-- open/close par ordre
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _fo;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _fo AS
SELECT order_id, price AS entry_px, qty, fill_ts AS entry_ts
FROM x_fills WHERE kind='OPEN';

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _fc;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _fc AS
SELECT order_id, price AS exit_px, fill_ts AS exit_ts
FROM x_fills WHERE kind='CLOSE';

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _j;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _j AS
SELECT
  o.id AS order_id, o.symbol, o.side, o.reason, o.score,
  fo.qty, fo.entry_px, fc.exit_px, fo.entry_ts, fc.exit_ts, o.sl, o.tp
FROM x_orders o
JOIN _fo fo ON fo.order_id=o.id
JOIN _fc fc ON fc.order_id=o.id;

-- PnL, rendement, durée
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _p;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _p AS
SELECT
  order_id,symbol,side,reason,score,qty,entry_px,exit_px,entry_ts,exit_ts,sl,tp,
  CASE WHEN side='BUY'  THEN (exit_px-entry_px)*qty
       WHEN side='SELL' THEN (entry_px-exit_px)*qty
       ELSE 0 END AS pnl,
  CASE WHEN entry_px>0 THEN
       100.0 * (CASE WHEN side='BUY' THEN (exit_px-entry_px)/entry_px
                     ELSE (entry_px-exit_px)/entry_px END)
       ELSE 0 END AS ret_pct,
  (exit_ts-entry_ts) AS hold_secs
FROM _j;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO x_trades(order_id,symbol,side,reason,score,qty,entry_px,exit_px,entry_ts,exit_ts,sl,tp,pnl,ret_pct,hold_secs)
SELECT order_id,symbol,side,reason,score,qty,entry_px,exit_px,entry_ts,exit_ts,sl,tp,pnl,ret_pct,hold_secs
FROM _p;
SQL

echo "trades built"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
BDB="$ROOT/data/b.db"
VER="${VER:?specify VER, ex: VER=analysisB-2025-10-10T12-00Z}"

sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_final_marks(
  version TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  ts_utc TEXT NOT NULL,
  n_pairs INTEGER NOT NULL,
  n_buy INTEGER NOT NULL,
  n_sell INTEGER NOT NULL,
  avg_score REAL NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS b_snapshots(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
  side TEXT NOT NULL,
  score REAL NOT NULL,
  price REAL NOT NULL,
  sl REAL NOT NULL,
  tp REAL NOT NULL,
  size_usd REAL NOT NULL,
  ts_utc TEXT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(version,symbol)
);

WITH last AS (SELECT MAX(ts_utc) t FROM b_plans),
rows AS (SELECT * FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT t FROM last))
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO b_final_marks(version, ts_utc, n_pairs, n_buy, n_sell, avg_score)
SELECT '$VER',
       (SELECT t FROM last),
       COUNT(*),
       SUM(side='BUY'),
       SUM(side='SELL'),
       COALESCE(AVG(score),0)
FROM rows;

DELETE FROM b_snapshots WHERE version='$VER';
INSERT INTO b_snapshots(version,symbol,side,score,price,sl,tp,size_usd,ts_utc)
SELECT '$VER',symbol,side,score,price,sl,tp,size_usd,ts_utc
FROM b_plans WHERE ts_utc=(SELECT MAX(ts_utc) FROM b_plans);
SQL

echo "B final marked: $VER"

Size: 454
MTime: 2025-10-10 13:58:10.798881184 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
SYMBOL="${1:?ex: BTCUSDT}"; INTERVAL="${2:?ex: 1m}"; LIMIT="${3:-500}"
OUT="${4:-/tmp/klines.csv}"
# REST → JSON → lignes → CSV(ts,o,h,l,c,v). Sans jq.
curl -s "https://api.binance.com/api/v3/klines?symbol=${SYMBOL}&interval=${INTERVAL}&limit=${LIMIT}" \
| sed 's/^\[\[//; s/\]\]$//' | tr -d '"' | sed 's/\],\[/\n/g' \
| awk -F, '{ if(NF>=6){ printf "%d,%s,%s,%s,%s,%s\n", $1/1000,$2,$3,$4,$5,$6 } }' > "$OUT"
echo "$OUT"
----- FILE END -----

Size: 3527
MTime: 2025-10-10 15:07:37.222253442 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db}"
: "${XDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db}"
: "${TDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db}"

sqlite3 "$XDB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000;
ATTACH DATABASE '$BDB' AS bdb;
ATTACH DATABASE '$TDB' AS tdb;

-- params + balance
CREATE TEMP TABLE _par AS
SELECT COALESCE(risk_usd,50.0) AS risk_usd,
       COALESCE(risk_pct,0.02) AS risk_pct,
       COALESCE(leverage,3.0)  AS leverage,
       COALESCE(tp_mult,1.8)   AS tp_mult,
       COALESCE(sl_mult,1.2)   AS sl_mult,
       COALESCE(score_boost,0.5) AS score_boost
FROM x_params WHERE id=1;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _bal AS SELECT balance FROM x_wallet WHERE id=1;

-- symboles tradables (ticks <= 10 min)
CREATE TEMP TABLE _tradable AS
SELECT DISTINCT instId AS symbol
FROM tdb.ticks
WHERE ts_ms >= (strftime('%s','now')-3600)*1000;

-- nouveaux signaux > last_id ET tradables
CREATE TEMP TABLE _st AS SELECT COALESCE(last_signal_id,0) AS last_id FROM x_state WHERE id=1;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _src AS
SELECT s.id AS signal_id, s.symbol, s.side, s.price, s.reason, s.created_ts
FROM bdb.signals_B s, _st
WHERE s.id > _st.last_id
  AND s.symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM _tradable);

-- plan récent (SL/TP/score)
CREATE TEMP TABLE _plan AS
SELECT p.*
FROM bdb.signals_B_plan p
JOIN (
  SELECT symbol, side, MAX(created_ts) mx FROM bdb.signals_B_plan GROUP BY symbol, side
) mx ON mx.symbol=p.symbol AND mx.side=p.side AND mx.mx=p.created_ts;

-- dédup stricte via UNIQUE (ignore si existe déjà)
CREATE TEMP TABLE _ins AS
SELECT s.signal_id,s.symbol,s.side,s.price,s.reason,s.created_ts,
       (SELECT sl FROM _plan WHERE symbol=s.symbol AND side=s.side ORDER BY created_ts DESC LIMIT 1) AS sl,
       (SELECT tp FROM _plan WHERE symbol=s.symbol AND side=s.side ORDER BY created_ts DESC LIMIT 1) AS tp,
       COALESCE((SELECT score FROM _plan WHERE symbol=s.symbol AND side=s.side ORDER BY created_ts DESC LIMIT 1),0.0) AS score,
       (SELECT leverage FROM _par) AS leverage,
       ROUND(
         CASE WHEN (SELECT risk_pct FROM _par) > 0
              THEN (SELECT balance FROM _bal)*(SELECT risk_pct FROM _par)/NULLIF(s.price,0)
              ELSE (SELECT risk_usd FROM _par)/NULLIF(s.price,0) END
       ,6) AS qty
FROM _src s
WHERE NOT EXISTS(
  SELECT 1 FROM x_orders xo WHERE xo.symbol=s.symbol AND xo.side=s.side AND xo.created_ts=s.created_ts
);

-- compléter SL/TP si absents
UPDATE _ins
SET tp = COALESCE(tp,
        price * (CASE WHEN side='BUY'
                      THEN 1+((SELECT tp_mult FROM _par)+(SELECT score_boost FROM _par)*score)/100.0
                      ELSE 1-((SELECT tp_mult FROM _par)+(SELECT score_boost FROM _par)*score)/100.0 END)),
    sl = COALESCE(sl,
        price * (CASE WHEN side='BUY'
                      THEN 1-(SELECT sl_mult FROM _par)/100.0
                      ELSE 1+(SELECT sl_mult FROM _par)/100.0 END));

ALTER TABLE _ins ADD COLUMN notional REAL;
ALTER TABLE _ins ADD COLUMN margin REAL;
UPDATE _ins SET notional=price*qty, margin=(price*qty)/NULLIF(leverage,0);

INSERT OR IGNORE INTO x_orders(symbol,side,price,qty,sl,tp,reason,score,leverage,margin,notional,status,signal_id,created_ts,updated_ts)
SELECT symbol,side,price,qty,sl,tp,reason,score,leverage,margin,notional,'NEW',signal_id,created_ts,created_ts
FROM _ins;

-- avancer pointeur seulement si insert
UPDATE x_state
SET last_signal_id = COALESCE((SELECT MAX(signal_id) FROM _ins),(SELECT last_signal_id FROM x_state WHERE id=1))
WHERE id=1;

DETACH DATABASE bdb; DETACH DATABASE tdb;
SQL
echo "import: ok"
----- FILE END -----

Path: /opt/scalp/project/bin/build_indicators_from_5m.sh

MTime: 2025-10-10 12:41:49.050302349 +0200

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${ADB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"       # contient ohlcv_5m (colonnes: symbol, ts, o,h,l,c,v)
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/scalp.db}"

sqlB(){ sqlite3 "$BDB" "$@"; }

# pragmas + anti-lock
sqlB "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=12000; PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;"

# drop safe
drop_obj(){ t=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COALESCE(type,'') FROM sqlite_master WHERE name='$1'"); 
  [ "$t" = "table" ] && sqlB "DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $1;"; 
  [ "$t" = "view"  ] && sqlB "DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS $1;"; }

# 1) v_indic5m_fast (déjà attendu par B)
drop_obj v_indic5m_fast
sqlB "CREATE TABLE v_indic5m_fast(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ts INTEGER, sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL);"
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
WITH base AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, c AS close
  FROM adb.ohlcv_5m
),
ema AS (
  SELECT b.symbol, b.ts,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 8 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
         AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21
  FROM base b
),
last AS (SELECT e.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn FROM ema e)
INSERT OR REPLACE INTO v_indic5m_fast(symbol,ts,sma9,sma21)
SELECT symbol, ts, sma9, sma21 FROM last WHERE rn=1;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
SQL

# 2) v_indic_1m — on l’alimente depuis le 5m pour satisfaire B sans dépendre du 1m
#    Les noms restent "1m" pour l’interface, mais la granularité est 5m.
drop_obj v_indic_1m
sqlB "CREATE TABLE v_indic_1m(
  symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
  open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
  spread_frac REAL, vol_sma20 REAL,
  sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL, sma50 REAL,
  atr14 REAL, atr_pct REAL,
  hh_20_excl REAL, ll_20_excl REAL
);"
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
WITH base AS (
  SELECT symbol, ts, o AS open, h AS high, l AS low, c AS close, v AS volume
  FROM adb.ohlcv_5m
),
ema AS (
  SELECT b.*,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 8  PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma9,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 49 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma50
  FROM base b
),
rng AS (
  SELECT e.*,
         MAX(high) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING) AS hh_20_excl,
         MIN(low)  OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING) AS ll_20_excl
  FROM ema e
),
atr AS (
  SELECT r.*,
         AVG(high - low) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 13 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS atr14
  FROM rng r
)
INSERT INTO v_indic_1m
SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume,
       0.0005 AS spread_frac,
       0.0    AS vol_sma20,
       sma9, sma21, sma50,
       COALESCE(atr14,0.0) AS atr14,
       CASE WHEN close>0 AND atr14>0 THEN atr14/close*100.0 ELSE 0.0 END AS atr_pct,
       hh_20_excl, ll_20_excl
FROM atr;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
SQL

echo "== indicators from 5m built =="

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${ADB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"
SYMBOL="${1:?SYMBOL}"; INTERVAL="${2:?1m|3m}"; CSV="${3:?/tmp/klines.csv}"

sqlite3 "$ADB" "
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_1m(symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, open REAL,high REAL,low REAL,close REAL,volume REAL, PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts));
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_3m(symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, open REAL,high REAL,low REAL,close REAL,volume REAL, PRIMARY KEY(symbol,ts));
"

TMP="tmp_import_$(date +%s)"
sqlite3 "$ADB" ".mode csv" "CREATE TEMP TABLE $TMP(ts,open,high,low,close,volume);" ".import '$CSV' $TMP"

case "$INTERVAL" in
  1m) sqlite3 "$ADB" "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ohlcv_1m(symbol,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) SELECT '$SYMBOL',ts,open,high,low,close,volume FROM $TMP;" ;;
  3m) sqlite3 "$ADB" "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO ohlcv_3m(symbol,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) SELECT '$SYMBOL',ts,open,high,low,close,volume FROM $TMP;" ;;
  *) echo "interval inconnu"; exit 1 ;;
esac

sqlite3 "$ADB" "DROP TABLE $TMP;"
echo "ingested: $SYMBOL $INTERVAL"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

fail(){ echo "FAIL: $*" >&2; exit 1; }

# 0) durcir pour éviter les courses
/opt/scalp/project/scripts/harden_o_db.sh >/dev/null 2>&1 || true

# 1) couverture = 35
cov=$(sqlite3 -noheader "$ADB" "
SELECT '5m|'||COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_5m
UNION ALL SELECT '15m|'||COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_15m
UNION ALL SELECT '30m|'||COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_30m;")
echo "$cov" | awk -F'|' '{printf "%s|sy=%s\n",$1,$2}'
echo "$cov" | awk -F'|' '$2!=35 {bad=1} END{exit bad}' || fail "coverage sy!=35"

# 2) gaps = 0
gaps=$(sqlite3 -noheader -separator '|' "$ADB" "
WITH tf(name,step) AS (VALUES('ohlcv_5m',300),('ohlcv_15m',900),('ohlcv_30m',1800)),
rows AS (
  SELECT 'ohlcv_5m' name,300 step,symbol,COUNT(*) n,MIN(ts) t0,MAX(ts) t1 FROM ohlcv_5m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_15m',900,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ohlcv_30m',1800,symbol,COUNT(*),MIN(ts),MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m GROUP BY symbol
),
g AS (SELECT name, MAX(0, ((t1-t0)/step + 1 - n)) AS miss FROM rows)
SELECT name, SUM(miss) FROM g GROUP BY name;")
echo "$gaps" | awk -F'|' '{printf "%s|gaps=%s\n",$1,$2}'
echo "$gaps" | awk -F'|' '$2!=0 {bad=1} END{exit bad}' || fail "gaps!=0"

# 3) exactement 100 par symbole
for t in 5m 15m 30m; do
  sqlite3 "$ADB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM ohlcv_${t} GROUP BY symbol HAVING COUNT(*)!=100);" | grep -qx 0 \
    || fail "rows!=100 $t"
done

# 4) ensemble = univers courant
sqlite3 -noheader -separator '|' "$ADB" "
ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
WITH cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM ohlcv_15m GROUP BY symbol),
     uni AS (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)
SELECT (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM uni)),
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM uni EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur));
DETACH DATABASE udb;" | grep -qx "0|0" || fail "set mismatch vs universe"

# 5) fraîcheur par palier: 5m libre, 15m=floor(5m,900), 30m=floor(5m,1800)
mx=$(sqlite3 -noheader -separator '|' "$ADB" "
SELECT (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_5m),
       (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m),
       (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m);")
echo "max_ts 5m|15m|30m: $mx"
awk -F'|' '{
  t5=$1; t15=$2; t30=$3;
  a15 = int(t5/900)*900;
  a30 = int(t5/1800)*1800;
  ok = (t5%300==0) && (t15==a15) && (t30==a30);
  exit(ok?0:1)
}' <<< "$mx" || fail "freshness/alignment"

echo "OK: o.db health strict"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
BIN="/opt/scalp/project/bin"
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
ok(){ printf "OK  - %s\n" "$1"; }
ko(){ printf "FAIL- %s\n" "$1"; exit 1; }

# 0) présence dossiers et scripts clés
[ -d "$BIN" ] || ko "bin directory manquant"
for f in env_ab.sh migrate_b_schema.sh build_ohlcv1m_from_ticks.sh \
          ensure_ab_indicators_atomic.sh build_features_1m.sh analyse_B_sql.sh \
          tick_gate_B.sh run_B_loop.sh check_b_health.sh \
          b_manifest_init.sh b_manifest_verify.sh; do
  [ -x "$BIN/$f" ] || ko "$f manquant ou non exécutable"
done
ok "scripts présents"

# 1) intégrité manifeste
if "$BIN/b_manifest_verify.sh" >/dev/null 2>&1; then ok "manifest integrity"; else ko "manifest integrity"; fi

# 2) santé B (tables)
v1=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE name='v_indic_1m';")
v5=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE name='v_indic5m_fast';")
ft=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE name='v_feat_1m';")
[ "$v1" = "1" ] && ok "v_indic_1m" || ko "v_indic_1m"
[ "$v5" = "1" ] && ok "v_indic5m_fast" || ko "v_indic5m_fast"
[ "$ft" = "1" ] && ok "v_feat_1m" || ko "v_feat_1m"

# 3) volumes min
rows_indic=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_indic_1m;")
rows_feat=$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_feat_1m;")
[ "$rows_indic" -gt 0 ] && ok "v_indic_1m rows=$rows_indic" || ko "v_indic_1m vide"
[ "$rows_feat"  -gt 0 ] && ok "v_feat_1m rows=$rows_feat" || ko "v_feat_1m vide"

# 4) exécution analyse_B à blanc
if BDB="$BDB" "$BIN/analyse_B_sql.sh" >/dev/null 2>&1; then ok "analyse_B_sql.sh run"; else ko "analyse_B_sql.sh run"; fi

# 5) tick gate
if BDB="$BDB" "$BIN/tick_gate_B.sh" >/dev/null 2>&1; then ok "tick_gate_B"; else ko "tick_gate_B"; fi

echo "SELFTEST OK"
----- FILE END -----

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ensure_ab_indicators_atomic.sh
Size: 4902
MTime: 2025-10-10 14:45:53.465979735 +0200
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${ADB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db}"
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db}"
sqlA(){ sqlite3 "$ADB" "$@"; }
sqlB(){ sqlite3 "$BDB" "$@"; }

sqlB "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL; PRAGMA busy_timeout=20000; PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;"

# source auto
HAS1="$(sqlA "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='ohlcv_1m';")"
SRC="5m"; [ "$HAS1" -gt 0 ] && [ "$(sqlA "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_1m;")" -gt 0 ] && SRC="1m"
T="ohlcv_5m"; [ "$SRC" = "1m" ] && T="ohlcv_1m"

# map colonnes
colA(){ tbl="$1"; shift; for c in "$@"; do
  [ "$(sqlA "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pragma_table_info('$tbl') WHERE name='$c';")" -gt 0 ] && { echo "$c"; return; }
done; echo ""; }
S=$(colA "$T" symbol sym) ; TS=$(colA "$T" ts timestamp epoch)
O=$(colA "$T" open o)    ; H=$(colA "$T" high h)
L=$(colA "$T" low l)     ; C=$(colA "$T" close c)
V=$(colA "$T" volume v)
for k in S TS O H L C; do eval "x=\$$k"; [ -n "$x" ] || { echo "col manquante $k dans $T"; exit 1; }; done
[ -n "$V" ] || V="0.0"

SUF="_new_$(date +%s)_$$"
V1="v_indic_1m$SUF"
V5="v_indic5m_fast$SUF"

# build v_indic_1m temp
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
CREATE TABLE $V1(
  symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER,
  open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
  spread_frac REAL, vol_sma20 REAL,
  sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL, sma50 REAL,
  atr14 REAL, atr_pct REAL,
  hh_20_excl REAL, ll_20_excl REAL
);
WITH base AS (
  SELECT $S AS symbol, $TS AS ts, $O AS open, $H AS high, $L AS low, $C AS close, COALESCE($V,0.0) AS volume
  FROM adb.$T
),
ema AS (
  SELECT b.*,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 8  PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21,
         AVG(close) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 49 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma50
  FROM base b
),
rng AS (
  SELECT e.*,
         MAX(high) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING) AS hh_20_excl,
         MIN(low)  OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING)  AS ll_20_excl
  FROM ema e
),
atr AS (
  SELECT r.*,
         AVG(high - low) OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 13 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS atr14
  FROM rng r
)
INSERT INTO $V1
SELECT symbol, ts, open, high, low, close, volume,
       0.0005, 0.0,
       sma9, sma21, sma50,
       COALESCE(atr14,0.0),
       CASE WHEN close>0 AND atr14>0 THEN atr14/close*100.0 ELSE 0.0 END,
       hh_20_excl, ll_20_excl
FROM atr;
DETACH DATABASE adb;
SQL

# build v_indic5m_fast temp
if [ "$(sqlA "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='ohlcv_5m';")" -gt 0 ]; then
  S5=$(colA ohlcv_5m symbol sym); T5=$(colA ohlcv_5m ts timestamp epoch); C5=$(colA ohlcv_5m close c)
  sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
  ATTACH DATABASE '$ADB' AS adb;
  CREATE TABLE $V5(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ts INTEGER, sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL);
  WITH base AS (SELECT $S5 AS symbol, $T5 AS ts, $C5 AS close FROM adb.ohlcv_5m),
  ema AS (
    SELECT b.symbol, b.ts,
           AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 8 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)  AS sma9,
           AVG(b.close) OVER (PARTITION BY b.symbol ORDER BY b.ts ROWS BETWEEN 20 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS sma21
    FROM base b
  ),
  last AS (SELECT e.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn FROM ema e)
  INSERT OR REPLACE INTO $V5(symbol,ts,sma9,sma21)
  SELECT symbol, ts, sma9, sma21 FROM last WHERE rn=1;
  DETACH DATABASE adb;
SQL
else
  sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
  CREATE TABLE $V5(symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ts INTEGER, sma9 REAL, sma21 REAL);
  WITH last AS (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) ts FROM $V1 GROUP BY symbol)
  INSERT INTO $V5
  SELECT i.symbol, i.ts, i.sma9, i.sma21
  FROM $V1 i JOIN last l ON l.symbol=i.symbol AND l.ts=i.ts;
SQL
fi

# vérifs avant swap
ok_v1="$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='$V1';")"
ok_v5="$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='$V5';")"
rows_v1="$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $V1;")"
rows_v5="$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $V5;")"
[ "$ok_v1" -eq 1 ] && [ "$ok_v5" -eq 1 ] && [ "$rows_v1" -gt 0 ] && [ "$rows_v5" -gt 0 ] || { echo "build incomplete"; sqlB "DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $V1; DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $V5;"; exit 0; }

# swap avec retries
n=0; max=8
while :; do
  if sqlite3 "$BDB" <<SQL
  PRAGMA busy_timeout=20000;
  BEGIN IMMEDIATE;
  DROP TABLE IF EXISTS v_indic5m_fast;
  ALTER TABLE $V5 RENAME TO v_indic5m_fast;
  DROP TABLE IF EXISTS v_indic_1m;
  ALTER TABLE $V1 RENAME TO v_indic_1m;
  COMMIT;
SQL
  then echo "indic: SRC=$SRC"; exit 0; fi
  n=$((n+1)); [ $n -ge $max ] && { echo "swap failed: locked"; sqlB "DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $V1; DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $V5;"; exit 1; }
  sleep $n
done
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash

WITH last AS (
  SELECT run_id, finished_at, count, reason
  FROM universe_runs WHERE status='published'
  ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT 1
)
SELECT 'run_id', run_id FROM last
UNION ALL SELECT 'finished_at', finished_at FROM last

UNION ALL SELECT 'available_now', (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v_universe_current);
"

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
XDB="${XDB:-/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db}"

sqlite3 "$XDB" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode tabs
PRAGMA busy_timeout=15000;

-- tables temporaires
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _t_all;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _t_all AS
SELECT symbol, reason, pnl, ret_pct, exit_ts FROM x_trades;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _t_30;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _t_30 AS
SELECT * FROM _t_all
WHERE exit_ts >= strftime('%s','now') - 30*86400;

-- par symbole
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _sym;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _sym AS
SELECT
  symbol,
  COUNT(*) AS n,
  SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS wins,
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)*1.0
        / NULLIF(ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl<0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)),0),2) AS pf,
  ROUND(AVG(pnl),2) AS exp_pnl,
  ROUND(AVG(ret_pct),2) AS avg_ret
FROM _t_all
GROUP BY symbol;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _sym30;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _sym30 AS
SELECT
  symbol,
  COUNT(*) AS n30,
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)*1.0/COUNT(*),2) AS win_rate30,
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)*1.0
        / NULLIF(ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl<0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)),0),2) AS pf30,
  ROUND(AVG(pnl),2) AS exp30
FROM _t_30
GROUP BY symbol;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO x_stats_symbol(symbol,n,wins,win_rate,pf,exp_pnl,avg_ret,
                                      n30,win_rate30,pf30,exp30)
SELECT s.symbol,
       s.n,
       s.wins,
       ROUND(s.wins*1.0/NULLIF(s.n,0),2),
       s.pf,
       s.exp_pnl,
       s.avg_ret,
       COALESCE(s30.n30,0),
       COALESCE(s30.win_rate30,0),
       COALESCE(s30.pf30,0),
       COALESCE(s30.exp30,0)
FROM _sym s
LEFT JOIN _sym30 s30 USING(symbol);

-- par raison
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _rsn;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _rsn AS
SELECT
  reason,
  COUNT(*) AS n,
  SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS wins,
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)*1.0
        / NULLIF(ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl<0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)),0),2) AS pf,
  ROUND(AVG(pnl),2) AS exp_pnl,
  ROUND(AVG(ret_pct),2) AS avg_ret
FROM _t_all
GROUP BY reason;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO x_stats_reason(reason,n,wins,win_rate,pf,exp_pnl,avg_ret,med_ret)
SELECT reason,
       n,
       wins,
       ROUND(wins*1.0/NULLIF(n,0),2),
       pf,
       exp_pnl,
       avg_ret,
       NULL
FROM _rsn;

-- par symbole+raison
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS _sr;
CREATE TEMP TABLE _sr AS
SELECT
  symbol,
  reason,
  COUNT(*) AS n,
  SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS wins,
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)*1.0
        / NULLIF(ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN pnl<0 THEN pnl ELSE 0 END)),0),2) AS pf,
  ROUND(AVG(pnl),2) AS exp_pnl
FROM _t_all
GROUP BY symbol,reason;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO x_stats_symbol_reason(symbol,reason,n,wins,win_rate,pf,exp_pnl)
SELECT symbol,
       reason,
       n,
       wins,
       ROUND(wins*1.0/NULLIF(n,0),2),
       pf,
       exp_pnl
FROM _sr;
SQL

echo "stats built"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

retry(){ n=0; until sqlite3 -noheader "$ADB" "$1"; do n=$((n+1)); [ $n -ge 5 ] && return 1; sleep 1; done }

# 1) 35 symboles et ensemble identique à l’univers
q1=$"ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;
WITH cur AS (SELECT symbol FROM a_context_state),
     uni AS (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)
SELECT (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM cur)||'|'||
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM cur EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM uni))||'|'||
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT symbol FROM uni EXCEPT SELECT symbol FROM cur));
DETACH DATABASE udb;"
out=$(retry "$q1") || { echo "FAIL: locked"; exit 1; }
echo "$out" | awk -F'|' '{if($1!=35||$2!=0||$3!=0){print "FAIL: set/count"; exit 1}else{print "OK set/count"}}'

# 2) Probas cohérentes (somme≈1)
q2=$"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM a_context_state WHERE pb<0 OR ph<0 OR ps<0 OR ABS(pb+ph+ps-1)>0.001;"
bad=$(retry "$q2") || { echo "FAIL: locked"; exit 1; }
[ "$bad" = "0" ] || { echo "FAIL: probs invalid"; exit 1; }

# 3) Scores dans bornes larges
q3=$"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM a_context_state WHERE s IS NULL OR s<-20 OR s>20;"
bad=$(retry "$q3") || { echo "FAIL: locked"; exit 1; }
[ "$bad" = "0" ] || { echo "FAIL: scores out-of-range"; exit 1; }

echo "OK: a.db health strict"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

# Sanity
echo "BDB=$BDB"
sqlite3 "$BDB" "PRAGMA busy_timeout=12000;"

echo "schema v_indic_1m:"
sqlite3 "$BDB" ".schema v_indic_1m" || { echo "v_indic_1m absente"; exit 1; }

echo "sample v_indic_1m:"
sqlite3 "$BDB" -tabs "SELECT symbol,ts,ROUND(sma9,6) sma9,ROUND(sma21,6) sma21,ROUND(close,6) close FROM v_indic_1m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 5;"

# Insert rule_sma
sqlite3 "$BDB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=12000;
INSERT INTO signals_B_plan(symbol,ctx,score,side,entry,sl,tp,qty,margin,notional,created_ts)
SELECT i.symbol,'rule_sma',ABS(i.sma9-i.sma21),
       CASE WHEN i.sma9>i.sma21 THEN 'BUY' ELSE 'SELL' END,
       i.close, i.close*0.98, i.close*1.02, 0,0,0, strftime('%s','now')
FROM v_indic_1m i
JOIN (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) ts FROM v_indic_1m GROUP BY symbol) lb
ON lb.symbol=i.symbol AND lb.ts=i.ts;
SQL

echo "counts:"
sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COUNT(*) AS signals_B_plan FROM signals_B_plan;"
sqlite3 "$BDB" -tabs "SELECT * FROM signals_B_plan ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 5;"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
ADB="$ROOT/data/a.db"
UDB="$ROOT/data/u.db"
VER="${VER:?specify VER, ex: VER=ohlcv-2025-10-10T12-00Z}"

# Vérif stricte avant marquage
/opt/scalp/project/bin/health_o_strict.sh >/dev/null

sqlite3 "$ADB" <<SQL
PRAGMA busy_timeout=8000;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS o_final_marks(
  version TEXT NOT NULL,
  tf TEXT NOT NULL,
  max_ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
  symbols INTEGER NOT NULL,
  rows_per_symbol INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')),
  PRIMARY KEY(version, tf)
);

ATTACH DATABASE '$UDB' AS udb;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO o_final_marks(version, tf, max_ts, symbols, rows_per_symbol)
SELECT '$VER','5m',
       (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_5m),
       (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_5m WHERE symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)),
       100;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO o_final_marks(version, tf, max_ts, symbols, rows_per_symbol)
SELECT '$VER','15m',
       (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_15m),
       (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_15m WHERE symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)),
       100;

INSERT OR REPLACE INTO o_final_marks(version, tf, max_ts, symbols, rows_per_symbol)
SELECT '$VER','30m',
       (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m),
       (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol) FROM ohlcv_30m WHERE symbol IN (SELECT symbol FROM udb.v_universe_current)),
       100;

DETACH DATABASE udb;
SQL

echo "Final OHLCV marked: $VER"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT symbol), COUNT(*)/COUNT(DISTINCT symbol)
FROM a_signals;
"

SELECT ctx, COUNT(*) FROM a_context_state GROUP BY ctx;
"

echo "== extremes =="

SELECT MIN(s), MAX(s), AVG(s) FROM a_context_state;
"

sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "
SELECT symbol,s,pb,ps,ctx
FROM a_context_state
ORDER BY s DESC LIMIT 5;
"
sqlite3 -tabs "$ADB" "
SELECT symbol,s,pb,ps,ctx
FROM a_context_state
ORDER BY s ASC LIMIT 5;
"

echo "== consistency check =="
sqlite3 "$ADB" "
SELECT CASE
  WHEN COUNT(*)=35 THEN 'OK: 35 symbols'
  ELSE 'FAIL: count mismatch' END

#!/usr/bin/env sh
set -eu
: "${BDB:=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db}"
LASTF="/opt/scalp/project/data/.last_ts_5m"
CUR_TS="$(sqlite3 "$BDB" "SELECT COALESCE(MAX(ts),0) FROM v_indic5m_fast;")"

[ "$CUR_TS" -le "$PREV_TS" ] && { echo "skip: no new fast tick"; exit 0; }
[ -x /opt/scalp/project/bin/analyse_B_sql.sh ] && BDB="$BDB" /opt/scalp/project/bin/analyse_B_sql.sh || true
echo "$CUR_TS" > "$LASTF"
echo "B déclenché sur ts=$CUR_TS"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, time, gzip

URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except Exception:
        try: return b.decode()
        except Exception:
            return ""

def fmt_sample(obj):
    a=obj.get("arg",{})
    d=(obj.get("data") or [{}])[0]
    return f"{a.get('instType')}/{a.get('channel')}/{a.get('instId')} | ts={d.get('ts')} | last={d.get('lastPr') or d.get('last')}"

CASES = [
    # 1) Ce que tu cites (v2 public)
    ("USDT-FUTURES ticker BTC,ETH",
     [{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"},
      {"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"ETHUSDT"}]),
    # 2) Même chose mais instId suffixé _UMCBL
    ("USDT-FUTURES ticker *_UMCBL",
     [{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT_UMCBL"},
      {"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":"ETHUSDT_UMCBL"}]),
    # 3) instType en minuscule 'umcbl' (souvent rejeté)
    ("umcbl ticker BTC,ETH",
     [{"instType":"umcbl","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"},
      {"instType":"umcbl","channel":"ticker","instId":"ETHUSDT"}]),
    # 4) books5 en USDT-FUTURES pour comparer
    ("USDT-FUTURES books5 BTC,ETH",
     [{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"books5","instId":"BTCUSDT"},
      {"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"books5","instId":"ETHUSDT"}]),
]

async def run_case(name, args, seconds=12):
    print(f"\n=== CASE: {name} ===")
    try:
        async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
            await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"subscribe","args":args}))
            t0=time.time(); n=0; errs=0; sample=None
            while time.time()-t0 < seconds:
                try:
                    raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=3)
                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"}))
                    continue
                msg = ungzip(raw) if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)) else raw
                try:
                    obj=json.loads(msg)
                except Exception:
                    continue
                if obj.get("event")=="error":
                    errs+=1
                    print("ERR ->", obj)
                    continue
                if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot","update"):
                    n+=1
                    if not sample:
                        sample = fmt_sample(obj)
            print(f"received={n}  errors={errs}  sample={sample}")
    except Exception as e:
        print("connect_err:", e)

async def main():
    for name,args in CASES:
        await run_case(name,args,seconds=12)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

import asyncio, json, gzip, time, sqlite3, websockets, os

ADB=os.getenv("ADB","/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
BDB=os.getenv("BDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db")
XDB=os.getenv("XDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db")
TDB=os.getenv("TDB","/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db")
URI="wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

FIXED={"BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","BNBUSDT","XRPUSDT"}
CAP=35
REFRESH_SEC=300
PING_SEC=20

def ungzip(b):
    try: return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except: 
        try: return b.decode()
        except: return ""

def table_exists(db_path, table):
    try:
        con=sqlite3.connect(db_path); cur=con.execute("SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name=?", (table,))
        ok=cur.fetchone() is not None; con.close(); return ok
    except: return False

def ctx_symbols():
    try:
        con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
        rows=con.execute("""
          WITH m AS (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) mts FROM contexts_A GROUP BY symbol)
          SELECT c.symbol
          FROM contexts_A c JOIN m ON (c.symbol=m.symbol AND c.ts=m.mts)
          WHERE c.ctx!='none' AND c.symbol LIKE '%USDT'
        """).fetchall()
        con.close()
        return {r[0] for r in rows}
    except: return set()

def open_pos_symbols():
    syms=set()
    for db in (XDB, BDB, ADB):
        if not os.path.exists(db): continue
        for t in ("positions_open","positions_open_new","positions_sim"):
            if table_exists(db, t):
                try:
                    con=sqlite3.connect(db)
                    rows=con.execute(f"SELECT DISTINCT symbol FROM {t}").fetchall()
                    con.close()
                    syms.update(r[0] for r in rows if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT"))
                except: pass
    return syms

def pick_universe():
    s = set()
    s |= ctx_symbols()
    s |= open_pos_symbols()
    s |= FIXED
    s = {x for x in s if x and x.endswith("USDT")}
    return sorted(list(s))[:CAP]

def ensure_tdb():
    con=sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    con.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
      symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, price REAL, bid REAL, ask REAL,
      PRIMARY KEY(symbol, ts)
    )""")
    con.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_sym_ts ON ticks(symbol, ts)")
    # vue latest
    con.execute("""DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_ticks_latest;""")
    con.execute("""CREATE VIEW v_ticks_latest AS
    SELECT t.* FROM ticks t
    JOIN (SELECT symbol, MAX(ts) mts FROM ticks GROUP BY symbol) m
      ON m.symbol=t.symbol AND m.mts=t.ts;""")
    # rétention 200
    con.execute("""DROP VIEW IF EXISTS _retention_plan;""")
    con.execute("""CREATE VIEW _retention_plan AS
    SELECT rowid FROM (
      SELECT rowid, ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY symbol ORDER BY ts DESC) rn
      FROM ticks
    ) WHERE rn>200;""")
    con.close()

def write_rows(rows):
    if not rows: return
    con=sqlite3.connect(TDB, isolation_level=None)
    con.executemany("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ticks(symbol,ts,price,bid,ask) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.execute("DELETE FROM ticks WHERE rowid IN (SELECT rowid FROM _retention_plan)")
    con.close()

def parse_tick(obj):
    if not isinstance(obj, dict): return []
    if obj.get("action") not in ("snapshot","update"): return []
    arg=obj.get("arg",{})
    if arg.get("channel")!="ticker": return []
    data=obj.get("data") or []
    out=[]
    for d in data:
        sym=d.get("instId"); last=d.get("lastPr"); bid=d.get("bidPr") or last; ask=d.get("askPr") or last
        ts=int(float(d.get("ts") or time.time()*1000)/1000)
        try:
            out.append((sym, ts, float(last), float(bid), float(ask)))
        except: continue
    return out

async def subscribe(ws, syms, op="subscribe"):
    if not syms: return
    args=[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":s} for s in syms]
    await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":op,"args":args}))

async def run():
    ensure_tdb()
    current=set()
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
                last_ping=time.time(); last_refresh=0
                print("T: connected")
                while True:
                    now=time.time()
                    if now-last_refresh>REFRESH_SEC or not current:
                        want=set(pick_universe())
                        add=list(want-current); rem=list(current-want)
                        if rem: await subscribe(ws, rem, "unsubscribe")
                        if add: await subscribe(ws, add, "subscribe")
                        current=want; last_refresh=now
                        print("T: universe", len(current), sorted(list(current))[:10], "...")
                    if now-last_ping>PING_SEC:
                        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"})); last_ping=now
                    try:
                        raw=await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=3.0)
                    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                        continue
                    msg = ungzip(raw) if isinstance(raw,(bytes,bytearray)) else raw
                    try: obj=json.loads(msg)
                    except: continue
                    rows=parse_tick(obj)
                    if rows: write_rows(rows)
        except Exception as e:
            print("T: ws_err", e); await asyncio.sleep(2)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, time, ujson as json, websockets

URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"   # endpoint WS Bitget
# ✅ marché MC (Market Composite)
SUB = {"op":"subscribe","args":[
    {"instType":"MC","channel":"ticker","instId":"BTCUSDT"}
]}

async def main():
    try:
        async with websockets.connect(
            URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20, close_timeout=5, max_size=2**20
        ) as ws:
            await asyncio.sleep(1)
            await ws.send(json.dumps(SUB))
            print("✅ Subscribed to Bitget MC BTCUSDT ticker")
            start = time.time()
            while time.time() - start < 20:
                msg = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=20)
                if isinstance(msg, (bytes, bytearray)):
                    msg = msg.decode(errors="ignore")
                try:
                    data = json.loads(msg)
                except Exception:
                    continue
                if "data" in data:
                    print("📊 WS OK:", str(data)[:200])
                    return
                if data.get("event") in ("subscribe","subscribed") or data.get("code") in (0,"0"):
                    print("📩 SUB ACK:", data)
            print("❌ WS FAIL: no data received in 20s")
    except Exception as e:
        print("🚨 WS FAIL:", type(e).__name__, e)

asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os,sqlite3,time,sys,collections,math

UDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
TDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
BDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
XDB="/opt/scalp/project/data/x.db"

def row(q,db):
    try:
        con=sqlite3.connect(db); r=con.execute(q).fetchone(); con.close(); return r or (0,)
    except: return (0,)

def fetch(q,db):
    try:
        con=sqlite3.connect(db); r=con.execute(q).fetchall(); con.close(); return r
    except: return []

def pct(a,b):
    try:
        return 100.0*(a-b)/b if b else 0.0
    except: return 0.0

def clear(): sys.stdout.write("\033[H\033[J")

while True:
    t0=time.time()
    # --- TOP 35 ---
    n_top=row("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM u_symbols",UDB)[0]
    next_top=7200-int(time.time()%7200)
    # --- OHLCV ---
    o5=row("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_5m",ADB)[0]
    o15=row("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_15m",ADB)[0]
    o30=row("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_30m",ADB)[0]
    next_ohlcv=300-int(time.time()%300)
    # --- CONTEXTE ---
    ctxs=fetch("SELECT ctx,COUNT(*) FROM v_contexts_A_latest GROUP BY ctx",ADB)
    ctx_map={r[0]:r[1] for r in ctxs}
    buy3=fetch("SELECT symbol FROM v_contexts_A_latest WHERE ctx='buy' LIMIT 3",ADB)
    sell3=fetch("SELECT symbol FROM v_contexts_A_latest WHERE ctx='sell' LIMIT 3",ADB)
    hold3=fetch("SELECT symbol FROM v_contexts_A_latest WHERE ctx='hold' LIMIT 3",ADB)
    # --- TICKS ---
    # map prix courants
    prices={s:p for s,p in fetch("SELECT symbol,price FROM v_ticks_latest",TDB)}
    tickn=len(prices)
    tickts=row("SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ticks",TDB)[0]
    lag=int(time.time()-tickts) if tickts else 999
    # --- SIGNAUX ---
    sigs=fetch("SELECT symbol,side,ROUND(notional,2),datetime(ts,'unixepoch','localtime') FROM signals_B_plan ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 5",BDB)

    # --- POSITIONS (open/closed) ---
    pos_open=fetch("""SELECT symbol,side,entry,qty,lev,sl_dyn,tp3,ts_open
                      FROM positions_sim WHERE status='open'
                      ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 5""",XDB)
    all_open=fetch("""SELECT symbol,side,entry,qty,lev FROM positions_sim WHERE status='open'""",XDB)
    closed=fetch("""SELECT symbol,side,pnl,entry,qty,lev
                    FROM positions_sim WHERE status='closed'""",XDB)

    # Récap par coin
    rec=collections.defaultdict(lambda: dict(open_cnt=0, float_pnl=0.0, closed_cnt=0, win_cnt=0, realized_pnl=0.0, realized_base=0.0))
    # ouverts
    for sym,side,entry,qty,lev in all_open:
        px=prices.get(sym, entry)
        pnl = (px-entry)*qty*lev if side=='long' else (entry-px)*qty*lev
        r=rec[sym]; r["open_cnt"]+=1; r["float_pnl"]+=pnl
    # clos
    for sym,side,pnl,entry,qty,lev in closed:
        r=rec[sym]; r["closed_cnt"]+=1; r["realized_pnl"]+=pnl
        r["win_cnt"] += 1 if pnl>0 else 0
        r["realized_base"] += (entry*qty)  # base notionnelle pour % réalisé

    # Tri par importance (pnl cumulé absolu)
    ordering=sorted(rec.items(), key=lambda kv: abs(kv[1]["float_pnl"]+kv[1]["realized_pnl"]), reverse=True)
    # Format recap rows
    recap_rows=[]
    for sym,stats in ordering[:12]:  # affiche top 12 lignes
        open_cnt=stats["open_cnt"]
        float_pnl=stats["float_pnl"]
        closed_cnt=stats["closed_cnt"]
        win_rate=(100.0*stats["win_cnt"]/closed_cnt) if closed_cnt else 0.0
        realized=stats["realized_pnl"]
        realized_pct=(100.0*realized/(stats["realized_base"] or 1.0))
        recap_rows.append((sym, open_cnt, realized_pct, float_pnl, closed_cnt, win_rate, realized))

    # --- Affichage ---
    clear()
    print("═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════")
    print(f" DASHBOARD LIVE – {time.strftime('%H:%M:%S')}   refresh 2 s ")
    print("═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════")
    print(f"TOP35: {n_top:2d} actifs | reload dans {next_top:4d}s")
    print(f"OHLVC 5m:{o5:6d} 15m:{o15:6d} 30m:{o30:6d} | reload dans {next_ohlcv:4d}s")
    print(f"CTX: buy={ctx_map.get('buy',0)} hold={ctx_map.get('hold',0)} sell={ctx_map.get('sell',0)} none={ctx_map.get('none',0)}")
    print(f"BUY: {[r[0] for r in buy3]} | HOLD: {[r[0] for r in hold3]} | SELL: {[r[0] for r in sell3]}")
    print(f"TICKS: {tickn} symbols | lag {lag}s")
    print("───────────── DERNIERS SIGNAUX ────────────────────────────────────────────────")
    for s in sigs:
        sym,side,notional,ts=s
        is_open = any(po[0]==sym for po in pos_open) or any(ao[0]==sym for ao in all_open)
        posstat="OPEN" if is_open else "–"
        print(f"{ts[-8:]}  {sym:10} {side:5}  {notional:>8.2f} USDT   {posstat}")

    print("───────────── RÉCAP PAR COIN (open/%réal./PnLflottant | clos/win%/PnLréal.) ──")
    print("SYMBOL      OPEN  %REAL     PNL_FLOAT    CLOSED  WIN%    PNL_REAL")
    for sym,open_cnt,real_pct,fpnl,closed_cnt,wr,realized in recap_rows:
        print(f"{sym:10}  {open_cnt:>4}  {real_pct:>6.2f}%  {fpnl:>11.2f}   {closed_cnt:>6}  {wr:>5.1f}%  {realized:>10.2f}")

    print("───────────── POSITIONS ACTIVES (5 dernières ouvertes) ───────────────────────")
    for sym,side,entry,qty,lev,sl,tp3,ts_open in pos_open:
        price=prices.get(sym, entry)
        dist_tp=pct(tp3,price)
        dist_sl=pct(price,sl if sl is not None else price)
        pnl=(price-entry)*qty*lev*(1 if side=='long' else -1)
        print(f"{sym:10} {side:5}  {price:>10.4f}  PnL {pnl:>9.2f}  ΔTP {dist_tp:>6.2f}%  ΔSL {dist_sl:>6.2f}%")

    print("───────────── 5 DERNIERS TRADES CLOS ─────────────────────────────────────────")
    hist=fetch("SELECT symbol,side,pnl,datetime(ts_close,'unixepoch','localtime') FROM positions_sim WHERE status='closed' ORDER BY ts_close DESC LIMIT 5",XDB)
    for h in hist:
        print(f"{h[3][-8:]}  {h[0]:10} {h[1]:5}  PnL {h[2]:>9.2f}")

    sys.stdout.flush()
    time.sleep(max(0,2-(time.time()-t0)))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, websockets, json, gzip, time

URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
SYMS = ["BTCUSDT", "APTUSDT"]
RUN_SECS = 15

def ungzip(b):
    try:
        return gzip.decompress(b).decode()
    except Exception:
        try:
            return b.decode()
        except Exception:
            return ""

async def probe(channel):
    args = [{"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": channel, "instId": s} for s in SYMS]
    counts = {s: 0 for s in SYMS}
    errors = []

    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=None, max_size=2**22) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op": "subscribe", "args": args}))
        start = time.time()
        while time.time() - start < RUN_SECS:
            try:
                raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=4)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"op": "ping"}))
                continue
            msg = ungzip(raw)
            try:
                obj = json.loads(msg)
            except Exception:
                continue
            if obj.get("event") == "error":
                errors.append(obj)
                continue
            if obj.get("action") in ("snapshot", "update"):
                inst = (obj.get("arg") or {}).get("instId")
                if inst in counts:
                    counts[inst] += 1

    print(f"\n=== {channel.upper()} ===")
    print("messages reçus :", counts, " | erreurs :", len(errors))
    if errors:
        for e in errors[:5]:
            print("ERR", e)

async def main():
    for channel in ("ticker", "books5"):
        await probe(channel)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, ccxt

ADB="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
TF_LIST=("5m","15m","30m")
LIMIT=100

def get_symbols():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB)
    for t in ("u_syms","u_symbols"):
        try:
            rows=con.execute(f"SELECT symbol FROM {t}").fetchall()
            if rows:
                con.close()
                return [r[0] for r in rows if isinstance(r[0],str) and r[0].endswith("USDT")]
        except sqlite3.Error:
            pass
    con.close(); return []

def ensure_tables():
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
    for tf in TF_LIST:
        con.execute(f"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_{tf}(
            symbol TEXT, ts INTEGER, o REAL, h REAL, l REAL, c REAL,
            PRIMARY KEY(symbol, ts))""")
    con.close()

def bitget_symbol(ex, raw):
    base = raw[:-4] if raw.endswith("USDT") else raw  # <- FIX ICI
    # 1) préférer un marché futures USDT (UMCBL/perp)
    for m in ex.markets.values():
        if m.get("base")==base and m.get("quote")=="USDT" and (m.get("swap") or "UMCBL" in m.get("id","")):
            return m["symbol"]              # ex: BTC/USDT:USDT
    # 2) sinon spot USDT
    for m in ex.markets.values():
        if m.get("base")==base and m.get("quote")=="USDT" and not m.get("swap"):
            return m["symbol"]              # ex: BTC/USDT
    # 3) fallback explicite futures, puis spot
    return f"{base}/USDT:USDT" if f"{base}/USDT:USDT" in ex.markets else f"{base}/USDT"

def insert_rows(tf, rows):
    if not rows: return
    con=sqlite3.connect(ADB, isolation_level=None)
    con.executemany(f"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ohlcv_{tf}(symbol,ts,o,h,l,c) VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?)", rows)
    con.close()

def main():
    syms=get_symbols()
    if not syms:
        print("Aucun symbole dans a.db (u_syms/u_symbols)"); return
    ensure_tables()
    ex=ccxt.bitget({'enableRateLimit': True})
    ex.load_markets()
    for tf in TF_LIST:
        batch=[]
        for s in syms:
            msym=bitget_symbol(ex, s)
            try:
                for t,o,h,l,c,v in ex.fetch_ohlcv(msym, timeframe=tf, limit=LIMIT):
                    batch.append((s, int(t//1000), float(o), float(h), float(l), float(c)))
                time.sleep(ex.rateLimit/1000)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[WARN] {s} {tf}: {msym} -> {e}"); time.sleep(0.2)
        insert_rows(tf,batch)
        print(f"[OK] ohlcv_{tf}: {len(batch)} lignes")
    print("Terminé.")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()
